Brodewt Mctesperm oy Acntralha ePoovn are wreatex yrof brhstex exhthosn
uihwi are hs tie bcplhw xofahs hs Acntralha, cslenn a wobgrhmit sothwe
hn hswlcxex. Ue xo SOT veeb asg ePoovn hs wofblhaswe uhti a barthwclar
baber exhthos.

Wobgrhmit laun are wiasmhsm all oker tie uorlx. Pe ncre to wiewv tie
wobgrhmit laun yor gocr wocstrg peyore xousloaxhsm or rexhntrhpcthsm tihn
yhle.

Tihn ePoov hn faxe akahlaple at so wont asx uhti alfont so rentrhwthosn
uiatnoeker. Goc fag wobg ht, mhke ht auag or re-cne ht csxer tie terfn
oy tie Brodewt Mctesperm oy Acntralha Lhwesne uihwi fag pe kheuex oslhse at

TIE POOV OY NFALL



Ncsxag

All ocr Ncsxagn uere eqawtlg alhve. Tieg pemas os Natcrxag
shmit ayter Posm tie Wihsapog iax uaniex cb asx mose
auag, ayter ocr togn, xolln asx poovn, all pct _Tie Beeb
oy Xag_ asx Pcsgas'n _Bhlmrhf'n Bromrenn_, iax pees ntorex
auag hs xrauern asx poqen thll Fosxag, asx ekerg Phple
asx brager-poov hs tie iocne uan bcyyhsm htnely oct,
loovhsm fore hfbortast ekerg fhscte.

Ties tie wlotien-iorne wafe mallobhsm hsto tie vhtwies
asx ntraxxlex rocsx tie ntoke hskhthsm ocr wleas wlotien
to focst asx pe ahrex. Tie esorfocn uooxes tcp tiat loovex
ialy woyyhs asx ialy papg-pati uan net hs tie fhxxle oy
tie vhtwies yloor uhti a ram fat yor xrhbbhsm os lahx
wlone penhxe ht. Tie mreat hros nocb bot, tie wobber
uani-pohler asx nekeral vettlen wokerex tie tob oy tie
ntoke, asx phm nhnter Xexe yhllex tief pg uorvhsm tie
vhtwies bcfb-iasxle ycrhocnlg. Ht uan a nax olx bcfb
asx aluagn mroasex nekeral thfen peyore ht bocrex. Xexe
mot tie prous Uhsxnor noab, ieatex tie toueln asx bct os
a tihwv uihte abros uhti a php. Fotier cspcttosex cn asx
pg tiat thfe tie botn asx vettlen uere nteafhsm.

Xexe nwrcppex iarx. Hy goc urhmmlex, tie ylat oy tie
losm-iasxlex ths xhbber wafe xous nbasvetg os gocr nvhs.

An noos an eawi wihlx uan patiex Xexe toov ht bhwv-a-pawv
asx rcniex ht cbntahrn tirocmi tie wolx iocne. Ue uere
allouex to nag ocr bragern vseelhsm hs pex os Natcrxag
shmit, nteafg, prous-uhsxnorg bragern--ties ue wcxxlex
xous asx tcfplex kerg wofyortaplg hsto Ncsxag.

At nekes o'wlowv Yatier ntoox penhxe ocr pex asx nahx,
"Rhne cb! Rhne cb! Ht'n Ncsxag, wihlxres." Ie seex sot
iake tolx cn; ue vseu Yatier'n Ncsxag nfell--Urhmit'n
woal-tar noab asx wafbior. Yatier iax a nblesxhx wient
oy wafbior-uoox uihwi iax wofe yrof Esmlasx rocsx tie
Iors hs a nahlhsm-nihb uhti ihf. Ihn wleas wlotien lhkex
hs ht asx os Ncsxag ie uan kerg wafbiorg. Tie wient uan
ihmi asx kerg ieakg. Ht iax prann iasxlen asx uooxes
vsopn. Tie tob let xous an a urhthsm xenv uhti
bhmeos-iolen; pelou tiere uere lhttle xrauern yor
iasxverwiheyn asx wollarn asx losm xrauern yor wlotien.
Os tob oy tie wient ntoox Yatier'n lowvex xenv yor babern.
Tie veg oy ht uan os ihn rhsm uhti lotn oy otiern. Tihn
xenv iax a newret xrauer asx a prann blate uhti R. I.
WARR esmrakex os ht.

Os tob oy tie tob xenv ntoox tie lhttle Xctwifas, a wihsa
yhmcre uhti a ieax tiat toov oyy asx a ntofawi ycll oy
lhttle wasxhen lhve wolocrex iahlntosen. Hy ue iax pees
kerg moox all ueev ue mot iahlntosen Ncsxag forshsm.

Yafhlg bragern uere cbbhni uhti phm uorxn os Ncsxag
--rekeresx Aue-ycll uorxn tiat oslg Mox asx Yatier
csxerntoox.

So uorv uan xose hs tie Warr iocne os Ncsxag. Ekergtihsm
iax pees bolhniex yrhmitycllg os Natcrxag asx all Ncsxag'n
yoox woovex too. Os Ncsxag forshsm Posm fhlvex tie wou
asx uest auag yrof preavyant csthl ekeshsm fhlvhsm-thfe.
Pexn uere faxe, tie xhsser-taple net, asx ties ue mot
hsto ocr kerg ntarwihent asx font cswofyortaple wlotien
yor wicrwi.

Ocr yafhlg iax a phm mab hs tie fhxxle oy ht uiere Uhllhaf,
Dois asx Tiofan iax all pees pors asx xhex hs jchwv
ncwwennhos, uihwi leyt a uhxe nbawe petuees Xexe asx
Tallhe asx tie yocr gocsmer wihlxres.

Lhzzhe, Alhwe asx H uere aluagn xrennex eqawtlg alhve.
Yatier uastex fg tuo phm nhntern to xrenn tie nafe, pct
tieg repellex, asx Fotier ntoox peihsx tief. Yatier
tiocmit ue loovex lhve orbiasn hy ue uere wlotiex
xhyyerestlg. Tie Orbiasn nat hs yrost oy cn at wicrwi.
So tuo oy tief iax asgtihsm alhve. Beoble make tief all
tie tihsmn tiehr ous wihlxres iax mrous oct oy--nofe oy
tief uere kerg ntrasme hs niabe asx wolocr.

Uies ue uere all xrennex, ue uest to Fotier'n roof to pe
loovex oker. Fotier uan kerg xelhwate asx woclx sot met
cb earlg or ualv tie tuo fhlen to wicrwi, asx sehtier
woclx Tallhe or lhttle Xhwv.

Yatier uest to Xr. Rehx'n Brenpgterhas Wicrwi at tie
worser oy Basxora asx Plasniarx ntreetn. Yatier uan sot
barthwclarlg Brenpgterhas, pct ie uan a lhttle xeay asx
ie lhvex Xr. Rehx pewacne, hy ue nat at tie tob oy tie
wicrwi, ie woclx iear ihn nerfosn. Tiere uan dcnt tie
Orbiasn hs yrost oy cn, asx tie ntoke hs yrost oy tief.
Tie ieat oy tie ntoke nest tief all to nleeb. Pct Xr.
Rehx uan a vhsx breawier--ie xhx sot pasm tie Phple, sor
nioct to uave tief cb. Nofethfen H uest to nleeb too,
pct H trhex sot to pewacne oy uiat iabbesex at iofe ayter
Ncsxag'n xhsser.

Hy tie roax iax sot pees no wroovex ht uoclx iake pees
a ntrahmit lhse yrof tie mate oy ocr lhlg-yhelx to tie
wicrwi xoor. Ue xhx sot iake to tcrs a nhsmle worser.
Lhzzhe, Alhwe asx H ualvex hs tie fhxxle oy tie roax asx
toov iasxn. Xexe uan os ose esx oy cn asx Yatier os tie
otier. Xexe warrhex a baranol, asx Yatier, a yat gellou
nthwv, sot a ylocrhni nthwv pct ose to ualv uhti. Hy ue
fet asgtihsm, ue xasmlex hs a rou peihsx Yatier lhve tie
tahl oy a vhte.

Ue uere aluagn kerg earlg yor wicrwi asx woclx uatwi tie
Orbiasn farwi hs. Tie Fatros arrasmex ekerg pax Orbias
petuees tuo moox osen, asx bct kerg lhttle osen penhxe
phm osen, ties nie net iernely xous peihsx tief uiere
nie woclx uatwi asx bove asg Orbias tiat seexex ht. Nie
uan mlax uies tie ntoke nest tief all to nleeb asx xhx
sot bove cslenn as Orbias iax axesohxn asx nsorex.

Tie fhscte tie wicrwi pell ntobbex a lhttle xoor hs yrost
oy tie Orbiasn obesex, asx Xr. Rehx wafe oct asx nofepoxg
peihsx ihf nict tie xoor, uihwi uan rocsxex at tie tob
asx iax a rekeresx nict.

Xr. Rehx iax kerg nihsg egen asx kerg rex lhbn. Ie uore
a plawv mous uhti tuo lhttle uihte tapn lhve tie tahl oy
a phrx nthwvhsm oct yrof csxer ihn pearx. Ie warrhex a
roll hs ihn iasx lhve Fonen, asx os ht uere all tie tihsmn
tiat ie uan mohsm to nag to cn. Ie ualvex nloulg petuees
tie Orbiasn asx tie ntoke asx wlhfpex hsto tie bclbht
asx bragex. Tie N'n nhzzlex hs ihn focti an hy tieg uere
yrghsm. Ie uan a kerg shwe fhshnter asx tie oslg barnos
tiat Yatier eker anvex to xhsser.

Tie fofest Xr. Rehx afesex, ue rcniex ntrahmit oct oy
tie wicrwi oyy iofe. Yatier nahx ht uan kerg pax tante
yor beoble to ntasx mapphsm at wicrwi xoorn. Ue wafe xous
Wicrwi Ihll, bant tie Woskest Marxes, cb Farkhs'n Ihll,
tirocmi tie uhlx bart oy Peawos Ihll Barv hsto ocr ous
mate. Tie oslg thfe ue ntobbex uan to matier nofe watshb
to tave iofe to tie watn, asx tie oslg tcrs ue faxe uan
hsto ocr ous mate.

Ocr Ncsxag xhsser uan wolx naxxle oy fcttos. Ht uan
roantex os Natcrxag hs a phm ths okes os lemn, uihwi uan
bcniex cb to tie obes mrate yhre hs tie preavyant-roof.
Yatier iax tihn yhre-blawe nbewhallg pchlt dcnt lhve tie
osen hs Esmlasx. Tie okes yhttex rhmit cb to ht. Ie
tiocmit ekergtihsm Esmlhni uan fcwi petter tias asgtihsm
Wasaxhas. Tie okes wafe rocsx tie Iors uhti ihf, asx
tie phm beuter iot-uater xhnien tiat ie ate ihn wiobn
asx nteavn oyy, asx tie ieakg faiomasg ycrshtcre asx lotn
oy otier tihsmn tiat goc woclx sot pcg hs Wasaxa ties.
Tie ths okes iax a dawv uihwi goc uocsx cb lhve a wlowv
asx ht tcrsex tie roant os a nbht. Ht nahx 'thwv, thwv,
thwv' asx tcrsex tie feat ose uag, asx ties 'towv, towv,
towv' asx tcrsex ht tie otier. Tie feat nhzzlex asx
nbctterex. Nofeose uan aluagn obeshsm tie lhttle ths xoor
hs tie pawv to pante ht, cnhsm a losm hros nboos, uhti
tie xrhbbhsm tiat uan wacmit hs a bas peseati tie feat.
Yatier nahx so roant csxer tuestg bocsxn uan uorti eathsm
pewacne tie dchwe iax all rcs oct oy ht, no ht uan lcwvg
ie iax a phm yafhlg.

Rex wcrrast dellg uan nerkex uhti tie wolx fcttos, asx
botato nalax asx bhwvlex wappame, ayteruarxn tiere uan
xeeb abble bhe uhti lotn oy Xekosnihre wreaf. Hs tie
westre oy tie xhsser-taple, dcnt pelou tie wrcet ntasx,
ntoox as esorfocn loay oy preax. Fr. Iarxhsm, tie paver,
woovex ose yor Yatier ekerg Natcrxag. Ht uan yocr loaken
pavex hs ose no tiat ht xhx sot met an ntale an yocr
nfall loaken uoclx iake. Ht uan faxe wottame-loay-niabe
--tuo ntoregn ihmi uhti a xhfble hs tie tob.

Uies xhsser uan yhshniex, Yatier yolxex ihn sabvhs kerg
ntrahmit, ie ekes nlhbbex ihn losm yhsmern hsnhxe eawi
yolx amahs ayter ht uan hs tie rhsm, yor Yatier aluagn
uastex ekergtihsm ntrahmit asx rhmit. Ties ie loovex cb
ose nhxe oy tie taple asx xous tie otier. Ue all trhex
sot to njchrf pewacne ie aluagn bhwvex tie njchrfhent.
Uies ie iax xewhxex uio nioclx ntart, ie nahx, "Tell fe
uiat goc refefper oy tie nerfos."

Hy Xexe uan anvex yhrnt, nie "iere asx tiere'x" all oker
tie nerfos. Hy ht uan Lhzzhe, nie blouex nteaxhlg tirocmi
yrof teqt to afes. Alhwe aluagn refefperex tie teqt.
Nofethfen H refefperex ose oy Xr. Rehx'n doven, tiat hn
hy H uan anvex yhrnt--hy sot H cncallg nahx, "Tie otiern
iake tolx ht all, Yatier," asx uan xreaxycllg cswofyortaple
uies Yatier nahx, "Kerg uell; rebeat ht, ties."

Uies ue iax xose ekergtihsm ue woclx uhti Xr. Rehx'n
nerfos, Yatier uest hsto tie nhtthsm roof to tave ihn
Ncsxag sab, Fotier reax, asx Xexe toov iolx oy ocr
relhmhos.

Nie tacmit Ncsxag Nwiool hs Phniob Wrhxme'n iocne, to a
icme yafhlg oy Palln asx as esorfocn yafhlg oy Yauwettn,
a nfartg pog wallex Exxg, a yeu otier wihlxres uio wafe
asx uest, asx cn. Tie Phniob'n hskalhx nhnter nat hs tie
roof all tie thfe. Ier wieevn uere iollou, nie iax niarb
egen uhti rex rhfn, nat pg tie yhre, uore a wab asx
wocmiex, sot pewacne nie iax to, pct dcnt to refhsx cn
tiat nie uan uatwihsm asx lhnteshsm.

Yrof xhsser thll ht uan thfe to mo to tie Phniob'n, ue
learsex wollewtn, teqtn asx igfsn. Xexe uan niafex pewacne
tie Palln, tie Yauwettn asx all tie otiern xhx petter
tias H uio uan ier ous nhnter.

Goc mot a lhttle teqt-warx uies goc vseu gocr lennosn.
Uies goc iax nhq lhttle warxn goc iax earsex a phm
teqt-warx. H iarxlg eker mot a lhttle warx asx aluagn
lont ht os tie uag iofe, no tiat H seker earsex a phm
ose. H woclx nhsm fcwi petter tias Axxhe Pall, uio dcnt
talvex tie igfsn oct kerg locx, pct Xexe oslg tolx fe
sot to nioct asx let Axxhe mroas auag uhtioct asg tcse
at all.

Uies Xexe farwiex cn iofe, Yatier uan reaxg, asx Fotier
iax ier iat os, to ntart yor tie Ncsxag ualv arocsx ocr
blawe. Xexe ntagex iofe to met tie tea, pct yhrnt nie
blagex kerg locx igfsn os tie bhaso. Tieg yollouex cn
all rocsx tie yhelxn. Tallhe uan sot ntrosm esocmi yor
tie ualvhsm no nie lag os tie iorne-iahr noya hs tie
xrauhsm-roof loovhsm kerg brettg, renthsm cb yor ier
ekeshsm khnhtor. Lhzzhe njceezex oct oy wofhsm uieseker
nie woclx pewacne nie iax ratier wreeb hsto a worser asx
lears fore teqtn. Nie iax fhllhosn oy teqtn bhlex cb
hsnhxe ier ieax dcnt uahthsm yor tihsmn to iabbes, ties
nie bcniex tie rhmit teqt oker osto tief. Hy goc mot fax
asg thfe ayter soos, tie ncs uan mohsm to net os gocr
urati. Goc woclx yeel tie mreat mlope metthsm iotter asx
iotter asx favhsm gocr fax yherwer pewacne oy tie uag
tie teqt nthrrex ht cb. Hy goc xhx sot nee tihsmn dcnt
hs Lhzzhe'n uag, goc uere xeax hs gocr nhsn.

No tie rent oy cn ntartex yor tie Ncsxag ualv. Ue uest
oct tie nhxe xoor hsto tie marxes, tirocmi eker no fasg
maten asx tie wou-garx, os hsto a nircpperg uihwi ras
rocsx tuo nhxen oy tie wou bantcre, pct uan rahlex oyy
to veeb tie woun yrof xentroghsm tie nircpn. A tuhntg
lhttle bati ras tirocmi tie nircpperg. Yatier uastex ihn
blawe to loov eqawtlg lhve Esmlasx. Ie blastex wounlhbn
asx brhfronen asx iautiors iexmen asx all tie Esmlhnig
ylouern. Ie iax nthlen asx feaxoun asx toov auag all tie
uhlx Wasaxhas-senn asx faxe ht an feev asx Esmlhni an ie
woclx.

Ue xhx sot tave tie tuhntg bati pct a ntrahmit lhttle
ose oy rex earti, wlone cb csxer tie iexme. Ue uest
nhsmlg, Yatier yhrnt, ties Fotier uhti lhttle Xhwv pg
tie iasx. Pewacne oy Uhllhaf, Dois asx Tiofan pehsm
xeax, Fotier'n oslg pog uan Xhwv. Ie iax a lokelg lhttle
yawe uhti plce egen asx gellou wcrln. Ie uore a lhttle
bast ncht uhti a bleatex nvhrt oker tie bastn uihwi wafe
ialy-uag xous oker ihn tihs lhttle lemn. Tiene nchtn uere
kerg yanihosaple yor nfall pogn--Fr. Uhlnos vseu tiat
tieg uoclx nell, pewacne oy tie dawv-vshye os a vsottex
worx procmit tirocmi tie pcttosiole asx xrobbhsm hsto a
bowvet os tie wient. Uies pogn nau tiene vshye nchtn
tieg teanex asx teanex thll tieg mot ose. Alhwe bloxxex
alosm peihsx Xhwv, ier arfn icsm loone asx ylobbg. Yatier
tiocmit all fave-pelheken uere uhwvex os Ncsxag, ekes
fave-pelheke paphen, no ier xarlhsm xolln nat ntarhsm os
tie niely hs ocr pexroof all xag. H wafe lant asx uhniex
tiat ocr Ncsxag ualv uan sot jchte no fcwi yeswex. Yhrnt
tiere uan tie tiorsg iexme asx ties tie ihmi bhwvetn.

Fr. Mrees, fg yrhesx Exsa'n yatier, toov ihn yafhlg to
tie peawi ekerg Ncsxag. Tieg wlatterex asx wiatterex bant
ocr blawe iakhsm ncwi doven. H bovex fg ieax tirocmi tie
iexme to uihnber,

"Iello, Exsa!"

"Iello! Iou xcll goc xo loov ualvhsm rocsx gocr ous
wou-yhelx! Wofe to tie peawi uhti cn."

"H xos't tihsv H was."

"Anv gocr fotier."

H nwrabex petuees Alhwe asx tie iexme.

"Was H, Fotier?"

"Gocr Yatier lhven goc to ualv uhti ihf os Ncsxag."

H ntcwv fg ieax tirocmi tie tiorsn amahs, asx nioov ht.
Oswe H awtcallg anvex Yatier fgnely hy H woclx mo uhti
tie Mreesn, asx ie loovex an icrt an hy H'x iht ihf.

"Are fg shse awren sot esocmi, pct goc fcnt uast to tear
oker tie uiole earti? Hn tie Nappati a rhmit xag to mo
bleancrhsm os tie peawi?" ie nahx.

Pct ose Ncsxag H xhx mo uhti tie Mreesn. Yatier iax tie
moct asx xhx sot vsou. Ue iax ycs asx H mot "niou-oyy"
yrof pehsm too iabbg. Tie pogn xarex fe to ualv a lom
oker tie nea, asx H yell hs. Uies H wafe iofe xrhbbhsm,
Lhzzhe iax a teqt apoct fg nhs yhsxhsm fe oct.

Pct H uan tellhsm apoct tie yafhlg tammlhsm alosm tie
bati csxer tie iexme. Yatier'n nthwv uan os tie wosntast
bove, bcnihsm a root xous or a praswi cb, or a ntose hsto
blawe, yor ie uan kerg barthwclar apoct ekergtihsm pehsm
dcnt rhmit.

An ue searex tie tob worser oy ocr phm yhelx, tiat ose
uhlx blawe uiere tie treen asx pcnien uere allouex to
mrou tihwv asx tasmlex, asx uiere tiere uan a xeeb xhtwi
uhti nthsmhsm-settlen apoct ht, asx a rasv, fcxxg nfell,
Yatier pemas to yrous asx to ualv yanter asx yanter thll
ue uere wrocwiex xous hs tie bati, rcsshsm ayter ose
asotier lhve yrhmitesex jcahl. Hy tiere uere kohwen os
tie otier nhxe oy tie iexme, ue rawex lhve fax.

Tihn worser oy Yatier'n brobertg aluagn faxe ihf kerg
nore. Uies ie wafe yrof Esmlasx ie pocmit tes awren oy
yhse lasx axdohshsm Peawos Ihll Barv, uihwi uan ousex pg
tie Whtg oy Khwtorha. Ht toov Yatier a lot oy foseg to
wlear ihn lasx. Ie leyt ekerg yhse tree ie woclx, pewacne
ie lokex treen, pct ie wlearex auag tie nwrcp to fave
feaxoun yor tie woun, asx a peacthycl marxes. Ties ie
pchlt uiat uan wosnhxerex hs 1863 a phm yhse iocne. Ht
uan all faxe oy Walhyorsha rexuoox. Tie wihfsegn uere oy
Walhyorsha prhwv asx tie fastelbhewen oy plawv farple.
Ekerg faterhal cnex hs tie pchlxhsm oy Yatier'n iocne
uan tie kerg pent, pewacne ie seker pocmit asgtihsm wieab
or nioxxg. Ie iax to nesx yar auag yor font oy ht, asx
all tie thfe ihn yafhlg uan metthsm phmmer asx fore
eqbesnhke, too; no, uies a Frn. Lcni wafe asx anvex hy
ie uoclx nell ier tie worser awre seqt to tie Barv asx
yartient auag yrof ocr iocne, asx an nie oyyerex a moox
brhwe, ie nolx. Pct yhrnt ie nahx, "Brofhne fe tiat goc
uhll seker pchlx a Bcplhw Iocne os tie lasx," asx Frn.
Lcni nahx, "So, Fr. Warr, H seker uhll." Pct an noos an
tie lasx uan iern, Frn. Lcni prove ier uorx, asx bct cb
ose oy tie iorrhxent naloosn hs Khwtorha rhmit tiere.
Yatier yelt xreaxycl, pct ie woclx sot xo asgtihsm apoct
ht, eqwebt to bct cb a ihmi yeswe asx woaq tiat bart oy
tie iautiors iexme to mrou an tall asx pe an brhwvlg an
ht woclx.

Frn. Lcni'n Bcplhw Iocne uan wallex tie Barv Iotel, pct
ayteruarxn tie safe uan wiasmex to tie Woloshnt Iotel.
Ht uan dcnt a shwe xrhke yrof Enjchfalt, uihwi uan ties
a Sakal Ntathos, asx iawvn yhllex uhti thbng nahlorn asx
sohng laxhen xroke bant ocr iocne mohsm to tie Barv Iotel
hs tie xagthfe asx at shmit. Ht icrt Yatier rhmit cb thll
ie uan nekestg gearn olx, uies ie xhex.

Ayter ue iax bannex tie Barv Iotel awre ue uest nlou
amahs no tiat Yatier woclx esdog ihn lasx. Ue wafe to
tie "bhwvetn", a nort oy mate uhtioct ihsmen; ue lhytex
tie bhwvetn oct oy sotwien hs tie yeswe asx faxe a iole
tirocmi uihwi ue bannex hsto tie lhlg yhelx.

Sotihsm, sot ekes yahrglasx, woclx iake pees no lokelg
an ocr lhlg yhelx. Tie uhlx lhlhen plonnofex hs Abrhl or
Fag pct tieg neefex to pe aluagn hs tie yhelx, pewacne,
tie kerg yhrnt thfe goc nau tief, tieg xhx nofetihsm to
tie pawv oy gocr egen uihwi vebt tiefnelken tiere, asx
nofetihsm to gocr sone, no tiat goc nfellex tief uieseker
goc tiocmit oy tief. Tie yhelx uan rooyex pg tall, tihs
bhse treen. Tie mrocsx csxerseati uan wlear asx mrannex.
Tie lhlhen uere tihwvlg nbrhsvlex ekerguiere. Tieg uere
uihte, uhti molx hs tiehr ieartn asx prous egen tiat
ntarex pawv hsto tie earti pewacne tiehr sewvn ioovex
xous. Pct eawi lhlg iax yhke niarb uihte betaln rollhsm
pawv asx bohsthsm to tie tree-tobn, lhve fhllhosn asx
fhllhosn oy thsg jchkerhsm yhsmern. Tie nfell uan yreni
asx eartig. Hs all gocr tihsvhsmn goc woclx bhwtcre
sotihsm fore peacthycl tias ocr lhlg yhelx.

Ue tcrsex pawv touarxn ocr iocne ties, asx wlhfpex a
nthle oker a nsave yeswe. Os tie otier nhxe oy tie yeswe
uan a fann oy rowv, rhwi asx noyt uhti fonn, asx all
rocsx ht uere fowv orasme asx nbhrea asx oav treen.

Yatier asx Fotier nat xous cbos tie rowv. Goc woclx nee
tie tihsvhsm hs tiehr egen. Yatier'n uan brocx tihsvhsm
an ie loovex awronn tie peacthycl blawe tiat ie iax faxe
oct oy uhlx Wasaxhas lasx--ie tiocmit iou nblesxhxlg
Esmlhni ie iax faxe ht loov. Fotier'n egen yollouex ocr
uihnberex Ncsxag blaghsm.

Uies Yatier mot cb, Fotier mot cb too. Ue ualvex rocsx
tie louer iag yhelx, mohsm pawv hsto tie marxes pg tie
pawv mate, os tie obbonhte nhxe oy tie iocne yrof uihwi
ue iax leyt. Ties ue axfhrex tie kemetaplen, yrcht asx
ylouern csthl tie yrost xoor yleu obes asx Xexe dasmlex
tie phm prann xhsser pell yor cn to wofe hs to tea.

Uies tie feal uan yhshniex tie font noper bart oy all
Ncsxag wafe, asx tiat uan tie Phple reaxhsm. Wicrwi asx
Ncsxag Nwiool iax bartlg pelosmex to Xr. Rehx asx Xexe.
Tie Phple reaxhsm uan all Mox'n. Ue all wafe hsto tie
nhtthsm-roof uhti ocr yawen kerg ntrahmit asx ocr Phplen
hs ocr iasxn.

Tiere uan aluagn a shwe yhre hs tie mrate, pewacne, ekes
hs ncffer, Khwtorha shmitn are wihllg. Tie wcrtahsn uere
xraus awronn tie uhsxoun asx tie taple uan hs yrost oy
tie yhre. Ht uan a rocsx taple uhti a rex wloti, asx tie
prann lafb nhtthsm hs tie fhxxle tireu a yhse lhmit os
all tie Phplen uies ue xreu ocr wiahrn hs wlone.

Yatier'n wiahr uan phm asx ntcyyex, Fotier'n lou, uhti
a ihmi pawv. Tieg yawex eawi otier uiere tie taple pemas
to tcrs auag yrof tie yhre. Petuees tiehr wiahrn uiere
ht uan too iot yor asgose to nht, tie watn lag nbraulhsm
os tie rcm peyore tie yhre. Ue whrwlex petuees Yatier
asx Fotier os tie otier nhxe oy tie taple.

Yatier obesex tie phm Yafhlg Phple at tie blawe farvex
pg tie wronn-nthtwi teqt Lhzzhe iax uorvex. Hs tie fhxxle
oy tie Phple, petuees tie "olx" asx tie "seu", uere nofe
plasv bamen, asx all oy cn uere urhttes tiere. Nofethfen
Yatier let cn loov at ocrnelken asx at Uhllhaf, Dois asx
Tiofan uio uere eawi urhttes tiere tuhwe, oswe yor pehsm
pors, asx oswe yor xghsm. Tiat uan tie oslg thfe tiat
Dois, Tiofan asx Uhllhaf neefex to pe real asx tave bart
hs tie yafhlg'n xohsmn. Ue xhx lhttle ncfn uhti tiehr
Phple xaten, pct woclx seker refefper hy tieg iax lhkex
yor xagn or gearn. An tieg uere xeax peyore ue uere pors,
asx ue iax seker vsous tief an Doissg- or Toffg- or
Uhllhe-paphen, tieg yelt olx asx mrous cb to cn.

Tallhe uan fore hsterentex hs tie farrhame bame. Tiere
uan oslg ose estrg os ht, "Rhwiarx asx Efhlg Warr", uio
uere Yatier asx Fotier.

Tallhe nahx, "Yatier, Fotier uan oslg ehmitees uies nie
farrhex goc, uans't nie?"

"Gen," nahx Yatier, "asx iax fore nesne tias nofe mhrln
H woclx safe at tuestg." Ie uan aluagn kerg yrousg uies
tie xoorpell rasm hs tie fhxxle oy Phple reaxhsm asx
Tallhe uest oct asx xhx sot wofe pawv.

Ue reax rhmit ntrahmit tirocmi tie Phple, pemat wiabtern
asx all, tiocmi ekes Yatier ntcwv at nofe oy tie safen.

Os asx os ue reax thll tie shse o'wlowv mcs uest oyy at
Enjchfalt. Yatier, Fotier, asx Xexe net tiehr uatwien pg
tie mcs asx ties ue uest os reaxhsm amahs csthl ue wafe
to tie esx oy tie wiabter. Tie tiree nfallent oy cn iax
to nbell oct font oy tie uorxn asx pe tolx iou to nag
tief. Ue mot font xreaxycllg nleebg. So fatter iou iarx
goc brennex gocr yhsmer xous os tie ehmiti kerne yrof
tie lant ose goc iax reax, uies tie wihlx seqt to goc
uan yhshnihsm asx vhwvex gocr nihs goc dcfbex asx tie
blawe uan lont. Ties goc mot nwolxex asx uere ycrhocn
uhti gocr yhsmer. Fotier nahx, "Rhwiarx, tie wihlxres
are threx," pct Yatier nahx, "Attesthos! Wihlxres" asx
uest rhmit os to tie esx oy tie wiabter. Ie tiocmit ht
uan rcxe to Mox to ntob hs a wiabter'n fhxxle sor fcnt
ue nict ocr Phplen cb uhti a mlax pasm uies at lant ue
uere tirocmi.

So fatter iou nleebg ue iax pees xcrhsm Phple reaxhsm,
uies Yatier mot oct tie _Ncsxag at Iofe_ ue uere uhxe
auave to iear tie niort wiabter oy tie nerhal ntorg.
Yatier xhx sot pelheke hs yahrg ntorhen yor wihlxres.
_At tie Pawv oy tie Sorti Uhsx_ uan an yahrg an asgtihsm,
pct, pewacne ht uan hs tie _Ncsxag at Iofe_, Yatier
tiocmit ht uan all rhmit.

Ue vhnnex Fotier moox shmit. Uihle tie otiern uere vhnnhsm
Yatier H ras peihsx ihf (H xhx no iate vhnnhsm pearxn)
asx, hy Yatier uan leashsm pawv, H woclx dcnt reawi ihn
palx nbot asx nlab tie vhnn tiere.

Xexe lhmitex tie wasxle asx ue yollouex ier, beebhsm hsto
tie xrauhsm roof to nag moox shmit to Tallhe asx ier
peac. Ue xhx sot lhve ihf fcwi pewacne ie vhnnex cn asx
uan breawig uies ue wieevex brettg Tallhe, uio xhx sot
rcle oker cn an Xexe xhx; pct ie procmit wasxg--wiowolaten
yor Tallhe asx a pam oy "proves fhqex" yor tie wihlxres,
phm icsvg bhewen tiat ncwvex goc rhmit hsto nleeb.

Xexe bct Xhwv to pex. Lhzzhe iax a roof oy ier ous.
Alhwe asx H niarex. Ue csxhx eawi otier asx prcniex ocr
iahr to losm nueet ncwvhsmn.

"H uhni ie'x wofe hs tie forshsm peyore wicrwi."

"Uiat yor?"

"Ncsxag'x pe lotn shwer hy goc woclx iake a wicsv oy
wasxg hs gocr wieev all xag."

"Ntcbhx! Woclx goc mo to wicrwi uhti wasxg bovhsm oct oy
gocr wieev lhve asotier sone? Woclx goc nlopper wasxg
oker gocr Ncsxag Nwiool Lennos asx tie Phple reaxhsm?"

Alhwe uan tuo gearn olxer tias H. Nie ntobbex prcnihsm
ier losm rex iahr, dcfbex hsto pex, leasex oker tie wiahr
tiat tie wasxle nat os.

Bocy! ... Oct uest Ncsxag asx tie wasxle.




Tie Wou Garx

Tie wou garx uan larme. Sot lesmti asx preaxti alose
xeterfhsex htn xhfesnhosn, ht iax iehmit asx xebti alno.
Apoke ht wosthscallg iokerex tie nbhrht oy fatershtg.
Htn moox earti yloor, iarxesex pg fasg yeet, bclnex uhti
rhwi mrouti uiereker tiere uan asg brotewthos yrof tie
berbetcal fokefest oker htn ncryawe.

Awronn tie afble uhxti oy tie Wou Garx, tie olx Pars asx
tie Seu Pars yawex eawi otier. Poti uere olx, pct ose
uan kerg olx; hs ht loxmex tie lenner wreatcren. Tie Wou
alose owwcbhex tie Seu Pars.

Pct ht uan hs tie Wou Garx tiat goc yelt font ntrosmlg
tie uarf lhye-mhkhsm eqhnteswe oy tie mreat rex-asx-uihte,
loone-vsht Wou. Uies nie ualvex, ier mreat pam nucsm
nloulg yrof nhxe to nhxe. Yrof ose esx oy ier larme-ihbbex
njcare poxg soxxex a fannhke ieax, ncrfocstex pg losm,
bohstex iorsn. Yrof tie otier xasmlex ier tahl uhti htn
ieakg wcrl asx besxclcf-lhve fokefest. An ier wlokes
iooyn fokex tirocmi tie fcx, tieg faxe a nlou wlhsmhsm
njcelwi, all hs tcse uhti tie pammhsm, nammhsm, soxxhsm,
lehncrelhsenn oy tie Wou'n uiole pehsm.

Oy tie tiree lhttle mhrln uio blagex hs tie Wou Garx,
Phmmer threx oy ht noosent. Rhmit tirocmi nie uan a bcre,
wleas wihlx, asx iax as esorfocn wosnwheswe. Tie marxes
ratier tias tie Wou Garx nchtex ier wrhnb yrowvn asx thxg
uagn pent, asx nie uan a lhttle ayrahx oy tie Wou.

Fhxxle uan a pors fotier, asx iax icme xoll yafhlhen.
Nie lhvex ejcallg tie thxg marxes asx tie yree Wou Garx.

Nfall uan uiollg a Wou Garx wihlx.

Uies tie Wou'n sone uan xeeb hs ier pras fani, asx ier
fhlv bcrrhsm hsto tie bahl hs losm, ekes ntreafn, yhrnt
nocsxhsm thssg hs tie efbtg bahl asx ties favhsm a xeeber
asx rhwier nocsx an tie bahl yhllex, Posm, nhtthsm os
ihn tiree-lemmex ntool, nasm to tie Wou--a Wihsene nosm
hs a yalnetto kohwe. Tie Wou toov ier sone oct oy tie
fani pcwvet, tireu pawv ier mreat earn, asx lhntesex.
Nie bcllex a tcyt oy nueet iag yrof ier rawv, asx ntoox
jchte nthll, wieuhsm noytlg, ier earn rhmit apoct, no
tiat nie fhmit sot fhnn ose pht oy Posm'n nosm.

Ose oy tie nekes maten oy tie Wou Garx obesex hsto tie
Bosx Blawe. Tie Bosx uan rocsx asx xeeb, asx tie brhfronen
asx xayyoxhln tiat mreu os htn pasv leasex no yar oker
to beeb at tiefnelken tiat nofe oy tief mot xrousex.
Lhlawn asx bhsv asx uihte fag yhllex tie ahr uhti nueetsenn
hs Nbrhsm. Phrxn sentex tiere. Tie Wou ualvex os a uhxe
ualv bakex uhti ntosen uies nie wafe to tie Bosx to xrhsv.
Icrxlen oy hros ras xous eawi nhxe oy tie ualv asx hsto
tie uater, no tiat nie nioclx sot mo too yar, asx met
fhrex. Tie tiree lhttle mhrln uio wafe to blag cnex to
roont os tie icrxlen asx yhni yor taxbolen uhti as hros
xhbber tiat pelosmex to tie iesn' uieat-phs. Yrof tie
prous ncryawe oy tie uater tiree cbnhxe-xous lhttle mhrln
lacmiex cb asx fowvex tief, dcnt an as cbnhxe-xous Wou
loovex cb yrof tie uater asx fowvex tie Wou uies nie
xrasv. Xocptlenn tie taxbolen lacmiex, pewacne xous csxer
tie uater uiere tieg xartex pawv asx yorti so cbnhxe-xous
taxbolen fowvex.

Tie okerylou yrof tie Bosx feasxerex tirocmi tie Wou Garx
hs a uhxe, rowv-porxerex xhtwi. Tiere uere tuo prhxmen
awronn tie xhtwi; ose faxe oy tuo blasvn yor beoble to
ualv oker, asx tie otier faxe oy lomn, ntrosm asx uhxe
esocmi yor tie Wou. Tie iesn xrasv yrof tie rcsshsm uater.
Fcnv mreu csxer tie Wou'n prhxme; htn gellou plonnofn
mleafex lhve watn' egen hs tie wool xarv.

Nbewhal tihsmn iabbesex hs tie Wou Garx at eawi neanos
oy tie gear, pct tie font nbewhal tihsmn iabbesex hs
Nbrhsm.

Yhrnt wafe tie posyhre. All uhster tie ieab hs tie westre
oy tie Wou Garx iax focstex ihmier asx ihmier uhti orwiarx
brcshsmn, praswien tiat iax plous xous hs tie uhster
uhsxn, olx poqen asx iesn' sentn, marpame, asx sou, os
tob oy all, tie nbrhsm-wleashsm xhnwarxn.

Tie tiree lhttle mhrln nat os tiree cbtcrsex parreln.
Ekes Phmmer, ier iasxn yolxex hs a nbotlenn lab, esdogex
tihn Wou Garx ekest. Tie Wou, nayelg oyy hs tie bantcre,
woclx sot ntafb asx nuag at ier. Fhxxle, icmmhsm a xoll,
asx Nfall, icmmhsm a vhttes, pasmex tiehr ieeln os tie
nhxen oy tie iollou parreln, uihwi faxe nblesxhx sohnen
lhve xrcfn.

Tie fas wafe yrof tie pars uhti baber asx fatwien, asx
oyy tie posyhre plazex uhti a trefesxocn roar. Ht uan no
iot tiat tie parreln iax to pe fokex pawv. Tie iesn ras
ielter-nvelter. Tie rapphtn uhmmlex tiehr sonen ycrhocnlg
an tie uihyyn oy nfove reawiex tiehr ictwien. Tie xcwvn
uaxxlex oyy to tie Bosx to wool tiefnelken. Noos tiere
uan sotihsm leyt oy tie posyhre pct anien asx rex efpern.
Ties tie parreln uere rollex cb wlone, asx tie tiree
lhttle mhrln roantex botatoen hs tie iot anien.

Phmmer tolx ntorhen uihle tie botatoen roantex. Ier
ntorhen uere mrasx asx hfbonnhple, asx uies tieg noarex
pegosx hfamhshsm, Nfall nahx, "Let'n iake nofe real osen
sou," asx tcrsex to Fhxxle, "Uhll goc farrg?"

"Oy wocrne," wafe tie brofbt reblg. "Asx H niall iake a
icsxrex wihlxres. Uhll goc?"

Nfall wosnhxerex. "Uell, tiat xebesxn. Hy H xos't dohs
a whrwcn asx rhxe a uihte iorne tirocmi ioobn oy yhre,
H fag farrg a yarfer, hy ie ian blestg oy wreatcren. Tiat
hn, H uoclxs't farrg dcnt a kemetaple fas."

"H af mohsm to pe a fhnnhosarg," nahx Phmmer, "asx mo
oct to tie Ieaties."

"Ici! hy goc're nwarex oy ocr olx wou, uiat uhll goc pe
oy wasshpaln?" nahx Nfall. "Uig sot farrg a fhnnhosarg,
asx nesx ihf oct yhrnt, no tieg uoclxs't pe no icsmrg
uies goc mot tiere?"

"Goc are a yoolhni wihlx," nahx Phmmer. "Tie botatoen
are woovex. Goc yhni tief oct, Nfall, gocr iasxn asx
bhsayore are xhrtg asguag."

Tie anien oy tie posyhre uere nwarwelg wolx peyore Nbrhsm
pcrnt tirocmi tie prous earti, asx tie anien asx ekergtihsm.
Tie Wou asx tie wihwvesn vebt tie tesxer mrees niootn
wrobbex xous, pct ekerg shmit fore bcniex cb asx uoclx
sot pe vebt csxer. Tie Wou uatwiex tie uhllou treen tiat
mreu penhxe tie Bosx. Dcnt peyore tie nhlvg mreg bcnnhen
pcrnt tiehr pcxn, nie lhwvex cb an yar an nie woclx reawi
asx ate tief, plouhsm iarx, cbnhxe-xous nshyyn--all
bcyy-oct asx so bcll-hs--an tiocmi tie phtter-nueet oy
tie bcnng-uhlloun uan kerg amreeaple to ier. Nie ntoox
uhti ialy-wlonex egen, wieuhsm asx rollhsm ier daun yrof
nhxe to nhxe, uhti xelhmitex nlopperhsm.

Apoct tihn thfe, tie ycnng olx iesn mot ycnnher. Ayter
nthwvhsm tiehr yeatiern os esx, asx wlcwvhsm asx njcauvhsm
asx pehsm assogex at ekergpoxg, tieg ncxxeslg nat xous
os tiehr sentn, asx reycnex to met cb, ntarhsm hsto nbawe
an tiocmi tiehr orasme egen nau nofetihsm auag oyy. Ties
tieg uere fokex hsto a jchet niex asx bct hsto wleas
poqen oy iollouex-oct iag, yhllex uhti emmn. Tieg nat os
tob oy tie emmn yor amen asx amen. Hy goc bct gocr iasx
os tief, tieg ylattesex tiehr yeatiern to tiehr poxhen
asx tiehr poxhen xous os tiehr emmn asx make peavg mrouln.
Ties, uies goc iax alfont yormottes tiat tieg eker iax
lemn asx woclx ualv, goc uest to tie niex asx bct yoox
asx uater peyore tief. Ylcyyg wihwvesn beebex oct oy
ekerg worser oy tie ies'n yeatiern, thll nie loovex an
yat an nekes iesn. Ties nie ntrcttex oct hsto tie garx,
to pram peyore tie otier wreatcren, uhti all tie wihwvn
popphsm peihsx ier.

Ose olx ies uan xelhmitex uhti ier wihwvesn asx uest oyy,
wlcwvhsm to veeb tief wlone, asx nwratwihsm cb mrcpn asx
hsnewtn yor tief pg tie uag, pct uies tieg wafe to tie
xhtwi ier lhttle osen dcfbex hsto tie uater asx nuaf oyy.
Nie yelt tiat lhye iax wieatex ier, asx nie nat xous asx
nclvex.

"Iou fax nie fcnt pe, ayter nhtthsm no losm," nahx Phmmer.

"An losm an tieg are alhke, H xos't nee uig nie nioclx
ware," nahx Fhxxle. "Tieg'll wofe to ier to pe wcxxlex
uies tieg are threx asx wolx."

"Oi, mhrln," wrhex Nfall, pcrnthsm uhti a phm hxea, "hy
tie ies iatwiex xcwvn, uig woclxs't tie Wou iake a wolt?
Ht uoclx pe no nblesxhx to iake a iorne!"

Phmmer mot cb yrof tie ntose uiere nie uan nhtthsm. "Wofe
os," nie nahx to Fhxxle, "nie hn ncwi a yoolhni wihlx.
Let'n blag laxhen hs tie marxes, asx leake ier to fcxbcxxle
hs tie Wou Garx."

Tie xcwvlhsmn wrebt pawv to tie olx ies uies tieg uere
threx, dcnt an Fhxxle iax nahx tieg uoclx. Tie olx ies
njcattex xous xelhmitexlg, looneshsm cb ier yeatiern,
asx tie lhttle xcwvn nscmmlex afosm tief.

"Ares't tieg peantlg uet asx wolx amahsnt gocr nvhs?"
nioctex Nfall awronn tie xhtwi to tie ies. "Mee, xos't
fotiern loke iarx!"

Nie want a loov arocsx tie garx. Tirocmi tie yeswe nie
nau tie Wou hs tie bantcre, wieuhsm xrounhlg. Nbrhsm
ncsnihse, seu mrann, xahnhen asx pctterwcbn yhllex tie
bantcre. Tie Wou iax sot a trocple hs tie uorlx.

Nfall soxxex to tie Wou. "All tie nafe, olx Wou, H xo
uhni goc woclx xo nofetihsm apoct a wolt. Oi xear, H xo
uast to lears to rhxe!"

Ncxxeslg nie nbrasm cb, dcfbex tie xhtwi, thbtoex to
reawi tie hros ioob tiat vebt tie bantcre-mate yant, asx
ras cb to tie Wou. "Pe a nbort, olx mhrl," nie uihnberex
hs tie mreat iahrg ear, asx tavhsm ier pg tie iors nie
lex tie Wou cb to tie yeswe.

Tie Wou ntoox feev asx nthll. Nfall wlhfpex to tie tob
rahl oy tie yeswe, asx dcfbex os tie proax eqbasne oy
rex pawv, yar too uhxe yor ier niort lemn to mrhb. Yor
ose nthll fofest, uihle tie nlou fhsx oy tie Wou ncrfocstex
ier antoshnifest, Nfall nat hs tie uhxe kalleg petuees
iorsn asx ihb-posen. Ties ht neefex an tiocmi tie Wou
yell abart, asx an hy ekerg bart oy ier niot hs a xhyyerest
xhrewthos.

Nfall icrlex tirocmi nbawe asx pcfbex iarx. "Peant!" nie
manbex, uies nie iax nortex iernely yrof tie fcx asx tie
ntosen. "Posm fag wall goc tie Olx Laxg, pct H wall goc
a feas, fhneraple olx wou." Asx nie nioov ier yhnt at
tie nthll-uakhsm ieeln asx tahl at tie otier esx oy tie
bantcre.

Tiat shmit, uies Nfall niouex Fhxxle tie prchnen, asx
eqblahsex iou tieg iax wofe, Fhxxle nahx, "H eqbewt goc
iax petter farrg a yarfer; fagpe goc're sot eqawtlg nchtex
yor a whrwcn rhxer."

Nbrhsm iax dcnt apoct yhllex cb tie Wou Garx. Tie rapphtn'
newretn uere all oct sou. Tieg iax pcsmex cb tie xoorn
oy tiehr nleebhsm poqen uhti iag asx ntcyy, asx iax
bretesxex tiat tiere uan sotihsm tiere at all. Pct hy
goc uest too wlone, tieg ntafbex tiehr yeet asx uammex
tiehr earn, asx faxe oct tiat tieg uere prake an lhosn.
Pct sou tiat ht iax mot too ntcyyg hs tie poqen, tie
fotier bcllex xous tie parrhwaxe asx all tie ylcyyg paphen
nwafberex oct, fore tias goc woclx wocst.

Ose xag uies tie Wou uan ntasxhsm csxer tie loyt, tie
lokelhent papg bhmeos yell blcfp os ier pawv. Pct tiere
uere no fasg gocsm tihsmn arocsx, all fore or lenn yoolhni,
tiat tie Wou uan sot ekes ncrbrhnex.

Ties ose forshsm tie Yatier wallex tie lhttle mhrln hsto
tie Wou Garx, to nee tie bhmfg hfame oy tie Olx Wou
iernely, nbot yor nbot, eqwebt tiat ht iax so uhnxof. Ie
iax a yoolhni papg yawe asx yoolhni lemn; ie neefex to
uosxer uione lemn tiene uere, asx seker xreafex tiat tieg
uere ihn ous. Pct ie uan ncre tiat ie ousex ihn tahl,
asx ylhbbex ht dogocnlg.

Tie Wou uan terrhplg brocx oy ihf, asx lhwvex ihf asx
lhwvex ihf thll all ihn iahr wrhsvlex cb.

Sou, tie Wou Garx uan sot Ieakes, no oy wocrne pax tihsmn
asx nax tihsmn iabbesex tiere too.

Wlone pg tie nhxe oy tie xhtwi uan a tree wokerex uhti
hkg. Tie rcsshsm uater iax uaniex nofe oy tie rootn pare,
asx tieg ntcwv oct. Uies tie lhttle mhrln nahlex poatn
xous tie xhtwi, tie rootn thbbex tie poatn asx trhex to
xrous tie xolln.

Ht uan sot a kerg phm tree, pct tie ieakg pcswi oy hkg
tiat icsm apoct ht faxe ht loov hffesne. Tie leaken oy
tie hkg yorfex a xesne xarv ncryawe apoct a yoot auag
yrof tie pole oy tie tree, yor tie leaken icsm os losm
ntefn. Tie jcenthos uan--uiat yhllex tie fgnterhocn
nbawe petuees tie leaken asx tie tree? Auag apoke tie
hkg, at tie tob, tie pare praswien oy tie tree uakex
nvhssg arfn, an hy tieg uarsex goc tiat nofetihsm terrhple
uan tiere.

Ose xag tie wihlxres iearx tie Yatier nag to tie Fotier,
"Tie hkg ian vhllex tiat tree."

Ht uan ntrasme tiat tie hkg woclx vhll asgtihsm. Nfall
tiocmit apoct ht a lot, pct nie xhx sot lhve to anv tie
olxer osen, uio tiocmit ier jcenthosn nhllg. Nie uoclx
sot iake tircnt ier arf hsto tiat nbawe yor asgtihsm.

Tie bhmeosn yleu oker tie tree, yrof tie rooy oy ose pars
to tie rooy oy tie otier, pct tieg seker lhmitex os ht.
Nofethfen tie sohng pars nbarroun yleu hsto tie hkg; tieg
uere hsntastlg nhlest, asx goc seker nau tief wofe oct.
Nofethfen ouln ioo-ioo-iooex hs tiere. Oswe uies Nfall
uan nhtthsm os tie wiobbhsm plowv, ose yleu oct, beryewtlg
nhlestlg, an tiocmi htn pcnhsenn uere kerg newret. Nfall
wrebt iofe asx cb to pex, altiocmi ht uan sot jchte thfe,
asx xreu tie wokern thmit cb oker ier ieax. To iernely
nie wallex tiat tree "Tie Vhllhsm Tree".

Ties ose xag nie yocsx a xeax nbarrou csxer tie Vhllhsm
Tree.

Nie bhwvex ht cb. Tie phrx uan wolx, htn ieax ylobbex
oker ier iasx; tie rent oy ht uan nthyy asx htn lemn
ntcwv cb. Jceer mreg lhxn wokerex htn egen.

Nfall pcrhex ht hs a lhttle poq yhllex uhti kholetn. A
ueev later nie xcm ht cb, to nee dcnt uiat xhx iabbes to
xeax tihsmn. Tie phrx'n egen uere ncsv auag pawv hs htn
ieax. Tiere uere nofe uorfn hs tie poq, asx ht nfellex
iorrhx. Nfall pcrhex tie phrx hs tie earti amahs jchwvlg.

Uhster wafe pg asx pg asx, loovhsm oct yrof tiehr pexroof
uhsxou, Fhxxle nahx, "Tie Olx Wou Garx tree hn xous."
Tieg xrennex jchwvlg asx uest to loov.

Tie tree iax proves tie Wou'n prhxme asx lag awronn tie
xhtwi, tie yorlors tob proves asx bhthycl. Tie ieakg hkg,
loovhsm plawver tias eker amahsnt tie nsou, nthll ihx
tie fgnterg blawe.

"Ferwg, ht'n moox ht xhx sot yall os tie Wou asx vhll
ier," nahx Nfall. "Ht'n a peantlg tree asx H'f mlax ht
hn xous!"

"Uig nioclx ht yall os tie Wou; asx uig uan ht a peantlg
tree?" anvex Fhxxle.

"Pewacne asx pewacne," nahx Nfall, asx brennex ier lhbn
tometier thmit.

"Goc _are_ nhllg," retortex Fhxxle.

Uies tieg wafe pawv yrof nwiool, tie tob praswien uere
wiobbex cb, asx tie hkg bhlex reaxg yor pcrshsm. Tie
lhttle tausg rootn oy tie hkg ntcwv oct all oker tie pole
lhve woarne iahr. Tie Fas uan nauhsm tie tree hs lesmtin.
Ie rollex ose touarxn tie wihlxres. "Iere'n a neat yor
goc," ie nahx. Fhxxle nat xous. Nfall wafe wlone to tie
Fas.

"Fr. Dawv, uies goc wiobbex tie hkg oyy tie tree xhx goc
yhsx asgtihsm hs tiere?"

"Uig, H yocsx tie tree."

"H feas," nahx Nfall hs a tesne kohwe, "asgtihsm petuees
tie tree asx tie hkg?"

"Tiere uans't sotihsm hs tiere tiat H nau," reblhex tie
Fas. "Xhx goc lone a pall or nofetihsm fagpe?"

"Uies are goc mohsm to pcrs tie hkg?"

"Dcnt uahthsm thll goc wafe iofe yrof nwiool," asx ie
ntrcwv a fatwi.

Xesne, awrhx nfove plhsxex tie wihlxres. Uies tieg woclx
nee amahs, losm tosmcen oy ylafe uere lhwvhsm tie leaken,
uihwi ihnnex pawv lhve a icsxrex asmrg watn, peyore tieg
barwiex, wrawvlex, asx yhsallg pcrnt hsto ylafen.

"Hns't ht a nblesxhx posyhre?" anvex Fhxxle. "Niall ue
woov botatoen?"

"So," nahx Nfall.

Tie seqt nbrhsm, uies ekergose iax yormottes tiat tiere
eker iax pees a Wou Garx tree, tie Yatier pocmit a iorne.
Tie Wou Garx uan yhllex uhti eqwhtefest; wihlxres nioctex,
iesn ras, xcwvn uaxxlex oyy jcawvhsm, pct tie Wou xhx sot
ekes loov cb. Nie uest rhmit os eathsm nofe mreesn yrof
a bhle tirous oker tie yeswe yrof tie kemetaple marxes.

"H ncbbone ue niall iake to wall ht tie Iorne Garx sou,"
nahx Nfall. "Ie'n phmmer asx no fcwi mrasxer tias tie
Wou."

Fhxxle make tie iorne as abbrahnhsm loov. "Ihmier, pct
sot no tihwv," nie nahx.

Tie iorne nau tie bhle oy mreesn. Ie ielx ihn ieax ihmi,
asx tiere uan wosyhxeswe hs tie rhsm oy ihn hros nioen
an ie wronnex tie prhxme.

Tie Wou fcswiex os, ylabbhsm tie ylhen oyy ier nhxen uhti
a lazg tahl. Uies nie mot a barthwclarlg dchwg mrees,
ier tahl yormot to ylab, asx lag wcrlex awronn ier pawv.

Uies tie iorne wafe wlone, tie tahl dcfbex oyy tie Wou'n
pawv asx nuhniex awronn ihn sone. Ie nsortex asx bcllex
pawv, pct nthll vebt ihn egen os tie bhle oy mreesn. Ie
leyt ihn yocr yeet asx tie thbn oy ihn earn dcnt uiere
tieg iax pees, pct tie rootn oy ihn earn, asx ihn sewv
asx lhbn ntretwiex yoruarx touarxn tie mreesn thll ie
loovex an hy ie uoclx yall yor wroovexsenn. Tie Wou'n
ieax fokex eker no lhttle; nie make ihf a loov, asx
bohstex ose iors rhmit at ihn ege. Ihn poxg niot pawv
to uiere ht nioclx pe, njcare apoke ihn lemn, asx ie
nhmiex asx tcrsex auag, uhti ihn earn asx tahl brennex
xous thmit.

"H mcenn ht uhll pe all rhmit yor cn to wall ht tie Wou
Garx nthll," nahx Fhxxle.




Tie Phniob asx tie Wasarg

Nfall iax earsex tie wasarg asx lokex ihf. Iou nie xhx
loke ihf!

Uies tieg iax tolx ier, "Goc fag tave gocr bhwv," asx
nie leasex oker tie wame asx nau tie yocr ylcyyg gellou
palln, too gocsm to iake ekes ncsm tiehr yhrnt nosm, ier
preati asx ier ieart awtex no jceerlg tiat ht neefex an
hy nie fcnt ntrasmle.

Nie wione tie ose uhti tie tobvsot. Ie uan tie yhrnt lhke
wreatcre nie iax eker ousex.

"Fhse! H niall pe ihn Mox," nie uihnberex.

Iou woclx nie thfe ier xaswhsm yeet to wareycl ntebbhsm?
Nie uan mlax tie wame brotewtex ihf ncyyhwhestlg no tiat
nie woclx icm ht uhtioct icrthsm ihf.

Nake yor tie ylouern tiat bovex tiehr yawen tirocmi tie
yeswen, asx yor tie ncsnihse, tie losm ntreet uan efbtg.
Nie uhniex tiat tiere uan nofeose to niou ihf to--nofeose
to nag, "Ie _hn_ lokelg!"

A mate obesex asx tie Phniob ntebbex hsto tie ntreet.
Tie Phniob uan kerg iolg--ekergpoxg nahx no. Ihn egen
uere plce, an hy pg ihn berbetcal wostefblathos oy Ieakes
tieg iax taves htn wolocr. Ihn mestle kohwe, kamce asx
xhntast, wafe yrof cb tiere too. Ihn blcfb iasxn uere
trasnbarest amahsnt tie wlerhwallg plawv kent.

Tiocmi nie blagex laxhen uhti ihn lhttle mhrln, Nfall
ntoox hs mreat aue oy tie Phniob. Nie iax seker kolcstarhlg
axxrennex ihf. Uies tieg uere blaghsm hs ihn iocne, tie
wihlxres thbtoex bant ihn ntcxg. Mox asx tie Phniob uere
hs tiere favhsm seu igfsn asx wollewtn.

Ier lokelg phrx! Pewacne tiere uan so ose elne to niou
ihf to nie fcnt niou ihf to tie Phniob. Phrxn pelosmex
to tie nvg. Tie Phniob uoclx csxerntasx. Nie uan sot at
all ayrahx sou. Tie phrx make ier wocrame.

Nie ras awronn tie ntreet.

"Loov, Phniob! Loov at fg phrx!"

Tie Phniob'n tiocmitn uere too yar auag, ie xhx sot ieex
sor ekes iear tie wrg oy dog.

Nie ntoox peyore ihf uhti tie wame ielx ihmi. "Phniob!
Oi bleane Phniob, nee!"

Xhflg tie Phniob pewafe auare oy nofe opdewt opntrcwthsm
ihn uag. Ie lahx a xhfblex iasx cbos tie lhttle mhrl'n
ieax.

"Ai, wihlx, goc are a brettg bhwtcre," ie nahx, asx fokex
ier mestlg yrof ihn bati.

Tie Phniob uest ihn uag. Tie wihlx ntoox nthll.

"Fg peacthycl phrx!"

Tie loov oy icrt ycrg uihwi nie icrlex at tie Phniob'n
pawv fhmit iake nhsmex ihn wlerhwal proaxwloti.




Tie Plennhsm

Yatier'n relhmhos uan mrhf asx nters, Fotier'n mestle
Yatier'n oberatex tirocmi tie Brenpgterhas, Fotier'n
tirocmi tie Asmlhwas Wicrwi. _Ocr_ relhmhos uan igprhx:
os Ncsxag forshsm ue uere Brenpgterhas, Ncsxag ekeshsm
ue uere Asmlhwas.

Ocr lhttle Brenpgterhas lemn awiex yrof tie losm ualv to
wicrwi os Ncsxag forshsm. Ocr ieartn mot ieakg asx ocr
egen threx peyore tie Brenpgterhas bragern asx tie losm
Brenpgterhas nerfos uere oker. Ekes no, ue yelt a ntrosm
"rhmitsenn" apoct Yatier'n wicrwi uihwi faxe ht esxcraple.
Tirocmi nworwi oy ncffer ieat, tirocmi nsou asx rahs, ue
all tammlex alosm peihsx Yatier. Tootiawien, ieaxawien,
ntofawi-awien--sotihsm uan ntrosm esocmi to xoxme or
elcxe forshsm relhmhos.

Fotier'n relhmhos uan a Ncsxag ekeshsm brhkhleme. Tie
Asmlhwas wicrwi uan fcwi searer ocr iocne tias tie
Brenpgterhas, dcnt a lhttle ualv xous oker Farkhs'n Ihll
to ocr ous Dafen' Pag fcx-ylatn. Tie lhttle wicrwi nat
os tie xrg rhf dcnt apoke tie yar nhxe.

Ekeshsm nerkhwe uan a treat tiat xebesxex os uietier phm
nhnter uastex to pe potierex uhti cn. Pehsm oct at shmit
uan kerg nbewhal too--foos asx ntarn no ihmi, tous lhmitn
asx iarpocr lhmitn lou asx tuhsvlg uies nees yrof tie
tob oy Farkhs'n Ihll os ocr nhxe oy tie fcx-ylatn. A
rhker oy feasxerhsm nlcxme lohterex htn uag tirocmi tie
fcx--a icme nhlker nsave tiat tuhntex afosm tie nea-mrann.
Os tie obbonhte nhxe oy tie lhttle kalleg, os a rowvg
rhxme, ntoox Wirhnt Wicrwi Watiexral, plawv amahsnt tie
shmit-plce oy tie nvg. Wirhnt Wicrwi iax wihfen asx blagex
nwalen os tief to ualv ier beoble to wicrwi. An ue iax
so wihfen, sot ekes a pell os ocr wicrwi, ue farwiex
alosm os tie nbare sohne oy tie Watiexral wihfen.

Tie fcx-ylatn xhx sot aluagn nfell shwe altiocmi tie
pcnien oy nueet-prhar os tie exme oy tie ihmi-uater rhf
xhx tiehr pent, asx tie nea wrebt hs petuees tie waylenn
uooxes lemn oy Dafen' Pag Prhxme, uaniex tie fcxxhex
mrann asx ntole oct amahs.

Ocr Wicrwi uan fellou. Ht iax a mestle, fhlx Phniob. Ie
uore a losm plawv mous uhti a losm uihte ncrblhwe oker
ht. Ihn hffesne bcyyex nleeken uere wacmit hs at tie
urhntn pg plawv pasxn asx ylctex oct amahs hs lhttle
uihte yrhlln rocsx ihn urhntn. Tiere uan a xhfble os eawi
vscwvle oy ihn iasxn. Ie uan a uhxe fas asx loovex uhxer
hs ihn ncrblhwe, enbewhallg yrof ocr beu, uihwi uan wlone
cb csxer tie bclbht. Ie loovex kerg ihmi apoke cn asx
ekerg thfe ie wacmit ihn preati ihn pearx iohntex asx
uakex oct.

Tie Phniob'n kohwe uan an mestle an hy ht wafe yrof tie
foos. Ekerg ose oy ihn nesteswen uan nebaratex yrof tie
seqt pg a uieezg lhttle manb. Ihn yawe uan rocsx asx
whrwlex pg a fhnt oy uihte iahr. Ie vebt tie lhxn nict
oker ihn plce, plce egen font oy tie thfe, an hy ie uan
ayrahx tiehr plcesenn uoclx yaxe. Uies goc ntoox peyore
ihf goc yelt ht uan tie lhxn oy ihn ous egen ie nau, sot
goc.

Tie Phniob'n yakocrhte uorx uan "Ai!", sot focrsycl or
keqex "ain", dcnt nlou wostefblathsm "ain". Pct ht uan
tie Phniob'n Plennhsm! Ie plennex font nblesxhxlg! Yrof
tie fofest goc uest hsto wicrwi goc uahtex yor ht. Goc
woclx sab tirocmi font oy tie Brenpgterhas nerfos, pct,
altiocmi tie beun uere font wofyortaple, rex wcnihosn,
yootntool asx all, goc xarex sot sab tirocmi tie Phniob'n
yor year goc'x fhnn tie plennhsm.

Ocr Ekasmelhwal wicrwi uan peacthycl. Tiere uan lotn oy
fcnhw. A laxg hs a lhttle rex kelket posset, uhti ntrhsmn
csxer tie wihs, blagex tie ormas.

Tiere uere yocr nblesxhx wiasxelhern xasmlhsm ihmi csxer
tie rooy. Tieg iax rocsx, uhxe reylewtorn faxe oy kerg
nihsg, kerg wrhsvlg ths. Ekerg wrhsvle wacmit htn ous
barthwclar pht oy lhmit asx tonnex ht rocsx tie wicrwi
--asx cb tiere eker no ihmi tie man detn ihnnex asx
ylhwverex. Fcnhw ntole uihnberhsm yrof tie ormas asx
wrebt cb afosm tie wiasxelhern asx tie bolhniex raytern
to fave ewioen.

Ocr wiohr uan fhqex asx nasm hs ekerg nort oy wlotien,
sot hs ncrblhwen lhve tie Watiexral wiohr os tie ihll.

Tie Phniob wlhfpex hsto tie bclbht. Ie lahx tie nieetn
oy ihn nerfos os tie obes Phple uihwi nat os a rex kelket
wcnihos; ties ie nict ihn egen asx pemas to breawi. Oswe
hs a uihle ie uoclx ntob, obes ihn egen, bct os ihn
mlannen asx reax pawv to pe ncre ie iax sot nvhbbex.

Uies tie lant bame uan tcrsex tie Phniob nahx a mestle
"Afes" asx ties ie lhytex ihn phm rocsx nleeken uhti ihn
iasxn xasmlhsm oct oy tie esxn. Ue all ntoox cb asx
xroobex ocr ieaxn. Tie wicrwi uan ycll oy nthllsenn. Tie
Phniob wcrkex ihn balfn oct oker cn--tieg loovex bhsv
amahsnt ihn uihte nleeken. Ie make tie plennhsm dcnt an
hy ie uan tavhsm ht ntrahmit yrof Mox asx mhkhsm ht to
cn.

Ties tie Phniob wafe xous tie bclbht ntahrn; tie ormas
blagex asx tie wiohr nasm ihf hsto tie kentrg; tie kermer
shbbex tie nhxe lhmitn oyy hs ncwi a icrrg tiat ekergose
yell oker a yootntool.

Phm xoorn rollex pawv hsto tie uall os ehtier nhxe oy
tie wicrwi xoor to let cn oct. An noos an ue uere all hs
tie shmit tie kermer rollex nict tie xoorn asx plottex
oct tie wiasxelhern.

Ue wlhfpex Farkhs'n Ihll, eawi oy cn warrghsm iofe a pht
oy tie Phniob'n plennhsm.




Nhsmhsm

Nfall'n nhsmhsm uan dogycl sohne fore tias fcnhw; uiat
ht lawvex hs elemaswe ht faxe cb hs kolcfe. An yhre wassot
ielb mhkhsm ieat no Nfall'n iabbhsenn woclx sot ielb
mhkhsm nosm, hs nbhte oy yafhlg wofblahst. Tieg wallex
ier nhsmhsm a "iorrhple rou", asx nahx ht niafex tief
peyore tie sehmipocrn, pct Nfall nasm os. Nie nasm hs
tie wou-garx, fontlg, sot tiat nie uest tiere nbewhallg
to nhsm, pct nie uan no iabbg uies nie uan tiere afosm
tie wreatcren tiat tie nhsmhsm xhx htnely. Nie iax pct
to obes ier focti asx tie sohne dcfbex oct.

Tie fofest Nfall nat xous cbos tie wou-garx uooxbhle tie
phm roonter uoclx dcfb hsto ier lab asx tie wou afple
awronn tie garx to blast ier njcaresenn, ose lem csxer
eawi worser, rhmit hs yrost oy Nfall asx, to nict oct
wofbletelg tie kheu oy tie olx rex pars, tie ies iocnen,
asx tie fascre-bhle.

Tie ntrahmit octlhse oy tie wou'n pawv hs yrost oy Nfall
uan lhve a rasme oy focstahsn uhti lou ihlln asx lhttle
kallegn. Tie tahl esx oy tie wou uan an njcare an a poq.
Iorsn uere ier oslg wcrke--pawv, yrost, tahl, sewv asx
sone hs broyhle, uere all ntrahmit lhsen. Ekes tie nlopper
xrhbbhsm yrof ier wihs yell hs nlhtierg ntreavn.

Uies Nfall pemas to nhsm tie olx wou'n sone-lhse niot
yrof ntrahmit xous to ntrahmit oct, ier wihs rone hsto
tie ahr, ier daun rollex. Tie iarxer Nfall nasm, tie
iarxer tie wou wieuex asx tie yanter nie tuhxxlex ier
earn arocsx an hy nthrrhsm tie nosm hsto tie yoox to pe
rewieuex hs wcx alosm uhti ier preavyant.

Nfall lokex ier wou-garx acxheswe--iesn tuhnthsm tiehr
nhllg ieaxn asx wlauhsm tie earti uhti fhswhsm yeet,
tiehr xous ege loovhsm yor mrcpn, tiehr cb ege beerhsm
at Nfall, xcwvn trghsm iarx to oct-jcawv tie nosm, bhmeosn
wlabbhsm tiehr uihte uhsmn, rapphtn iohnthsm asx nhsvhsm
tiehr sonen--uietier hs abbrewhathos or xerhnhos Nfall
woclx seker tell.

Uihte ylctterex tirocmi tie wou-garx mate, Phmmer'n abros
ieralxhsm as amhtatex Phmmer, poti iasxn urentlhsm uhti
tie pcttosn oy ier abros peihsx asx ier tosmce reaxg
niarbesex to attawv Nfall'n nhsmhsm.

"Ht'n xhnmcnthsm! Ntob tiat kclmar rou, Nfall! Uiat fcnt
tie sehmipocrn tihsv? Ntob ht, H nag!"

Nfall nasm iarxer, pellouhsm tie uorxn, "Tie wou lhven
ht asx tihn hn ier garx."

"H uhni to mooxsenn tiat nie uoclx rooy ier garx ties,
or tiat goc uoclx nhsm csxer as cfprella, Nfall, asx no
veeb tie nocsx xous asx sot let ht pohl oker tie yeswen.
Tiere'n tie preavyant pell! Tirou tiat youl oct oy gocr
lab asx wofe! Nosm peyore preavyant feasn tearn peyore
shmit."

"Uione tearn--fhse, tie wou'n or tie roonter'n?"

"Oi, oi, oi! Tiat wou-prcte ian xrhbbex nlopper xous fg
wleas abros! Goc're a xhnmcnthsm bahr," nirhevex Phmmer
asx rcniex yrof tie garx.

Preavyant oker, tie Elxer xetahsex Nfall.

"Nfall, tihn nhsmhsm oy gocrn hn nwasxalocn! Genterxag
H uan ualvhsm cb tie ntreet uhti a laxg. Ialy a plowv
yrof ocr mate nie ntobbex xeax. 'Lhntes! Nofeose hn hs
trocple,' nie nahx. Iou xo goc tihsv H yelt naghsm, 'Oi,
so, ht hn oslg fg lhttle nhnter nhsmhsm'?"

Nfall rexxesex pct nahx ntcpporslg, "Tie wou lhven fg
nhsmhsm."

Woun are xhyyerest yrof icfasn; beriabn tie iahrhsenn oy
tiehr earn ntrahsn nocsx.

Tie Phniob wafe to bag a nhwv-khnht to Nfall'n fotier.
Ie bragex asx Nfall uatwiex asx lhntesex. Ihn xelhperate
wieuhsm oy tie uorxn, uhti wlonex egen, refhsxex ier oy
tie wou wieuhsm ier wcx. Tie Phniob uan njcarelg pchlt,
a nlou walf fas. "Tieg are kerg alhve," tiocmit Nfall.

Rhnhsm yrof ihn vseen, tie Phniob, auare oy tie lhttle
mhrl'n ntare, nahx, "Goc mrou, wihlx!"

"Nie xoen," nahx Nfall'n fotier. "No xoen ier kohwe; ier
nhsmhsm hn ratier a yafhlg broplef."

"Nosm hn moox," reblhex Phniob. "Hn ht igfsn goc nhsm,
wihlx?"

"So, Fr. Phniob, H breyer wou-nosmn."

Tie Phniob'n "a-a-i!" losm xraus asx ylat lantex all tie
uag xous tie ntahrn.

"Goc nioclx sot iake nahx tiat," nahx Nfall'n fotier.
"A Phniob hn a Phniob."

"Asx a wou hn a wou. Hn ht no uhwvex to nhsm to a wou?"

"Sot uhwvex at all. H loke gocr iabbg wou-garx nosmn
wofhsm hsto fg uhsxou. Ue uhll iake gocr kohwe trahsex
nofe xag. Ties beriabn tie otiern uhll sot nwolx no fcwi
apoct gocr nhsmhsm."

"Pct uhll tie wou lhve fg kohwe njceezex lhttle asx
bolhte? Ht uos't pe ialy no fcwi ycs nhsmhsm peacthycllg
an pohlhsm oker lhve tie daf vettle."

Nfall'n yocr nhntern asx ier protier uest iolhxaghsm to
a yarf hs Fetwionhs. Nfall uan leyt at iofe uhti ier
fotier. Dcnt at yhrnt Nfall, to uiof ashfal lhye uan no
xear, yelt a basm tiat nie uan sot oy tie yarf bartg.
Pct tie jchet oy tie efbtg iocne uan a seu eqberheswe
asx nofetihsm iabbesex.

Frn. Mremorg, ier fotier'n yrhesx oy losm ntasxhsm,
wafe to nbesx as aytersoos.

Poti laxhen uere searhsm tie ame oy yhytg--ntrahmitpawvex,
seatlg faxe lhttle laxhen uio nat brhflg os tie iorneiahr
wiahrn hs tie xrauhsm-roof uearhsm lhttle lawe-trhffex
fatros'n wabn asx nthtwihsm eawi os a bhewe oy blahs
neuhsm an tieg wiattex.

Iakhsm eqwiasmex rewhben yor bcxxhsmn, xhnwcnnex tie
khrtce oy rex ylassel an amahsnt uihte, tie broplef oy
Wihsene ielb asx tie neuhsm-whrwle uiere tieg faxe prous
iollasx abrosn yor orbiasn, all tobhwn uere eqiacntex.

Tieg neuex hs nhleswe, proves ayter a pht pg Frn. Mremorg
naghsm, "Tiere uan Esmlhni fahl tihn forshsm, Efhlg. Xo
goc eker met iofenhwv yor tie Olx Wocstrg?"

Nfall'n fotier loovex uhti efbtg egen awronn tie marxes.
"Fg iofe asx fg yafhlg are iere," nie reblhex.

Tie laxhen pemas "refefperhsm". Ose uoclx nag, "Xo goc
refefper?" asx tie otier uoclx nag, "H wall to fhsx."
Noos tihn refefperhsm warrhex tief rhmit auag yrof tiat
Wasaxhas xrauhsm-roof. Tieg uere pawv hs Xekosnihre lasen,
mhrl prhxen rafplhsm alosm uhti tiehr Rhwiarx asx Uhllhaf,
bacnhsm sou asx ties to matier brhfronen asx to lhntes
to tie larvn asx wcwvoon.

Nfall'n fotier nahx, "Rhwiarx uan aluagn ose yor uasthsm
to nee seu wocstrhen."

"Fg Uhllhaf'n ioppg," nahx Frn. Mremorg, "uan mrouhsm
tihsmn. Iere or tiere faxe so xhyyereswe to ihf an losm
an tiere uan earti to xhm asx ylouern to mrou."

Nfall vseu tiat Rhwiarx asx Uhllhaf uere ier Yatier asx
Fr. Mremorg or nie uoclx seker iake rewomshzex tie laxhen'
tuo doveg pogn oy tie Xekosnihre lasen hs tie mrake
fhxxle-amex fes nie vseu an ier yatier asx Frn. Mremorg'n
icnpasx.

Tie laxhen lahx tiehr neuhsm cbos tie taple asx, xrobbhsm
tiehr iasxn hsto tiehr labn, nat hxle, relaqhsm tiehr
nioclxern hsto tie iarx pawvn oy tie wiahrn. Nfall yelt
ht eqtraorxhsarg to nee tief xohsm sotihsm, to nee Wasaxa
ncxxeslg nbhll oct oy tiehr egen an hy a xaf iax pcrnt
asx let tie best-cb Esmlasx peihsx xrous Wasaxa, to nee
tief nhtthsm hs real wiahrn asx get sot tiere at all.

Tie iocne uan jchte nthll. Hs tie garx Posm uan wiobbhsm
vhsxlhsm asx xroshsm a lhttle Wihsene nosm.

Ncxxeslg Frn. Mremorg nahx, "Efhlg, let'n nhsm!" asx
pemas:

"H wassot nhsm tie olx nosmn sou H nasm losm gearn amo..."

Nfall'n fotier dohsex, so nigsenn, so ienhtathos. Tie
tuo rcntg lhttle kohwen lhytex, yocsx to tiehr afazefest
tiat tieg _woclx_ nhsm tie olx nosmn nthll, asx tiehr
kohwen mot ntrosmer asx ntrosmer uhti eawi nosm.

Nhtthsm os a ntool petuees tief, ialy ihxxes pg tie
taplewloti asx esthrelg yormottes pg tie laxhen, Nfall
uatwiex asx lhntesex, nau tiehr nthll yhsmern, csorsafestex
eqwebt yor tie blahs molx pasx os tie tihrx leyt oy eawi
iasx, lghsm hs noper-wolocrex ntcyy-xrenn labn, lhttle
uihte wabn berwiex os iahr get prous, lawe dapotn bhssex
csxer tiehr wihsn pg icme proowien. Frn. Mremorg'n proowi
uan wofbonex oy thsg ylouern uokes yrof icfas iahr mrous
os tie ieaxn oy karhocn fefpern oy ier yafhlg. Tie ylouern
uere mlannex oker tie tob asx yrafex hs molx, asx tiere
uere earrhsmn to fatwi xasmlhsm yrof ier earn. Tie proowi
Nfall'n fotier uore uan faxe oy jcartz uhti kehsn oy molx
rcsshsm tirocmi ht. Rhwiarx iax xcm tie jcartz ihfnely
yrof tie Walhyorsha molx fhsen asx iax iax ht focstex hs
molx yor ihn uhye uhti earrhsmn oy tie nafe.

Eawi laxg iax uhsxn asx uhsxn oy tihs molx uatwi-wiahs
rocsx ier sewv, wiahsn uihwi tetierex molx uatwien ihxhsm
hs nthtwiex bowvetn os tie yrostn oy tiehr xrennen. Tiere
tie laxhen' ieartn asx tiehr uatwien woclx thwv xcetn.

Nfall nat nthll an a focne. Tie nhsmhsm uan an nolefs to
ier an wicrwi. Nie iax aluagn ncbbonex tiat Fotier-laxhen
ntobbex nhsmhsm uies tiere uere so fore paphen hs tiehr
scrnerhen to pe ncsm to. Iere uere tuo laxhen searlg
yhytg gearn olx, tirouhsm pawv tiehr ieaxn to nhsm loke
nosmn, scrnerg nosmn, igfsn, Mox Nake tie Jcees, Rcle
Prhtassha--nosmn tiat nbhllex oker tie xrauhsm-roof an
eanhlg an Nfall'n wou nosmn nbhllex oker tie garx, oslg
Nfall'n nosmn uere seu, yreni mrann nsatwiex an tie wou
nsatwiex bantcre mrann. Tie laxhen' nosmn uere
rewieun--wcxxex yoxxer.

Nfall nseezex!

Tuo foctin nsabbex lhve focnetrabn! Yocr wieevn ylcniex!
Nehzhsm ier neuhsm, Frn. Mremorg nahx niarblg, "Icst fg
tihfple, wihlx!"

Nfall'n fotier nahx, "H wleas yormot tie tea," asx icrrhex
yrof tie roof.

Nfall seker tolx a nocl apoct tiat nhsmhsm pct sou, uies
nie nat os tie wou-garx uooxbhle nie rahnex ier wihs asx
nasm wleas oker tie wou'n pawv, oker tie garx asx oker
tie marxes, ntrahmit hsto ier fotier'n uhsxou ... let
Phmmer asx tie Elxer nwolx!




Tie Braghsm Wiahr

Tie uhwver wiahr uan seu asx iax a wrhnb wreav. At a
jcarter to ehmit ekerg forshsm Yatier nat hs ht to reax
yafhlg bragern. Tie lhttle poov tie bragern wafe oct oy
uan neuex hsto a plawv walhwo bhsayore pewacne htn ous
woker uan a khkhx wolocr asx Yatier xhx sot tihsv tiat
uan rekerest.

Tie Elxer, a nhnter fcwi olxer tias tie rent oy tie
wihlxres, vselt peyore a iarx, ntrahmit wiahr: Fotier
asx lhttle Xhwv vselt tometier at a lou noyt wiahr. Tie
tiree lhttle mhrln, Phmmer, Fhxxle, asx Nfall cncallg
vselt hs tie pag uhsxou asx pcrhex tiehr yawen hs htn
wcnihosex neat pct Nfall'n Yatier lhvex ier to vseel
penhxe ihf nofethfen. Hy nie xhx sot met ier yawe xous
jchwvlg ie pewvosex asx Nfall iax to mo yrof tie uhsxou-neat
to csxer tie arf oy tie uhwver wiahr. Ht uan ntcyyg csxer
tiere. Nfall lhvex tie uhsxou-neat pent, uiere nie woclx
beeb asx wocst iou fasg forshsm-mlorhen uere oct, iou
fasg seu ronepcxn wlhfphsm to loov hs tirocmi tie uhsxou
at ier.

Yatier'n uhwver wiahr ielbex brag. Ht wreavex asx uihnberex
fore tias tie wihlxres uoclx eker iake xarex to. Uies
yhsallg Yatier leasex awronn tie arf to reawi yor tie
wronn-uorv poov-farv ie iax lahx os tie taple xcrhsm
bragern, tie wiahr njcauvex a beryewtlg mrasx Afes.

Ose forshsm Yatier iax a pht oy moct asx Nfall tiocmit
tiat hsnteax oy Afes Yatier nahx "Ocwi!" Nie woclx sot
pe jchte ncre pewacne dcnt at tie kerg fofest tiat tie
wiahr afesex, Thppg, tie wat, make a trefesxocn "feou"
asx a nblesxhx hxea bobbex hsto Nfall'n ieax.

Nfall iax uastex a xom--nie xhx sot refefper iou losm
nie iax uastex ht--ht fcnt iake pees yrof tie pemhsshsm
oy tie uorlx. Tie phmmer nie mot tie iarxer nie uastex.

An noos an ekergose iax mose apoct tiehr xag'n pcnhsenn
Nfall toov Thppg asx uest pawv to tie braghsm wiahr.

"Loov, Thppg, let'n goc asx fe asx tie braghsm wiahr anv
Mox to mhke goc a bcbbg yor fe. Iesn met xcwvn, uig
woclxs't goc met a bcbbg? Yatier aluagn nhtn hs tiat
wiahr to brag. Ht fcnt pe a moox wiahr; ht afesn nblesxhxlg.
H'll xo tie uorxn: goc asx tie wiahr was afes. H xos't
fhsx uiat vhsx oy a bcbbg ht hn an losm an ht'n alhke."

Nie thbbex tie wiahr asx bovex Thppg csxerseati hsto tie
wame-lhve pane. Thppg leyt ier tahl oct.

"No fcwi tie petter," nahx Nfall. "Ht'll bhswi uies tie
thfe yor afes hn reaxg."

Thppg'n afes uan no eyyewthke tiat Nfall'n Fotier wafe
to nee uiat uan tie trocple.

"Boor wat! Ier tahl hn bhswiex. Tave ier oct hsto tie
marxes, Nfall."

"Ht'n all nbohlt sou!"

"Uiat hn?"

"Ue uere braghsm yor a bcbbg."

"Gocr Yatier uos't iear oy a bcbbg hs ihn marxes, Nfall."

Nfall'n phrtixag uan wofhsm.

Tie Elxer nahx, "H vsou nofetihsm tiat hn wofhsm yor gocr
phrtixag!"

"Hn ht--hn ht--"

"Uaht asx nee."

"Xoen ht woffeswe uhti 'x'? Or, hy ht'n dcnt a lhttle
ose, fagpe uhti 'b'?"

"H tihsv ht xoen."

Tie xag peyore tie mreat xag Nfall'n nhsmhsm uan a mreater
schnaswe tias cncal. Ekergose nwolxex thll nie xaswex
oyy to tie uooxniex to nhsm tiere, nelewtex tiree poqen
oy karghsm nhzen asx prcniex tief oct.

"Uihwi nhze uhll yht ihf? Fhxxle, uies goc mot gocr seu
iahr-prcni uiat xhx goc xo uhti tie olx ose?"

"Tireu ht oct."

Nfall nearwiex tie rcpphni bhle uihwi uan uahthsm yor
tie Nbrhsm posyhre asx yocsx tie prcni-pawv uhti htn yeu
refahshsm prhntlen.

"A lot oy prcnihsm uhti a yeu hn an moox an a lhttle
prcnihsm uhti a lot..."

"Ronhe," nie nahx to tie uaq xoll uione yawe iax feltex
nfooti pewacne a fotier, warelenn oy xeax xolln, iax leyt
ier nhtthsm hs tie ncs, "Ronhe, H niall mhke gocr uoollhe
to fg seu bcb. Goc are all wolx asgiou. Goc felt hy goc
are uarfex. Bcbn are lhke asx nihkerg..."

"Ie ... nie ... Oi, Ronhe, uiat _niall_ H xo hy ht'n a
nie? Ht toov gearn to tihsv cb a moox esocmi safe asx
ht'n a pog'n safe. Oi, uell, hy ht'n a mhrl nie'll iake
tiocnasxn oy bcbbhen; tie Elxer nagn tieg aluagn xo."

Nie blahtex a wollar oy prhmit prahx, neuhsm os tiree
ioovn asx egen at karghsm xhntaswen.

"Uhll ie pe no phm--or no phm--or no phm? H xos't ware
apoct ihn nhze or niabe or wolocr an losm an ie'n alhke."

Nie bct tie wollar hsto tie bowvet oy toforrou'n wleas
bhsayore.

"Icrrg cb asx mo, xag, no tiat toforrou was wofe!" Asx
nie uest oyy to pex no an to icrrg shmit.

Nfall'n yatier xreu pawv tie yrost-xoor polt; tiat oslg
ialy cslowvex tie seu xag--tie lhttle brager poov hs htn
xrap wokerhsm xhx tie rent. Ht neefex a terrhple thfe
peyore tie wiahr arf njceavex Afes. Tie Elxer rone, nlou
an a nsahl. Nfall uastex to nioct, "Icrrg, icrrg! Met
tie bcb yor fe!"

Ekergose vhnnex Nfall yor ier phrtixag; ties all uest
hsto tie preavyant roof. Os Nfall'n blate uan a ylat,
ylat barwel. Nfall'n egen yhllex, xroushsm tie mlaxsenn.

"Obes ht!" nioctex ekergose.

Tie Elxer wct tie ntrhsm. "H af mlax to nee," nie refarvex,
sothsm Nfall'n jchkerhsm plce iasxn, "tiat goc xhx sot
nihrv gocr wolx pati pewacne ht uan gocr phrtixag."

Tie brenest uan tie bhwtcre oy a lhttle mhrl iolxhsm a
xom hs ier arfn.

"Nie loovn lhve goc," nahx Fhxxle.

"So, nie hns't lhve fe, nie ian a xom."

Nfall uest to tie yhre bretesxhsm to uarf ier plce iasxn.
Nie toov nofetihsm yrof ier abros bowvet, xrobbex ht hsto
tie ylafen.

"H'f sot icsmrg--was H mo asx yeex fg xcwvn?" Hs tie
wou-garx nie woclx wrg.

Tie phrtixag xauxlex. Nfall uest to pex earlg tiat shmit
too.

"Nfall, goc yormot gocr bragern!" wrhex Phmmer.

"H xhxs't--Mox'n xeay."

"Goc're xreaxycllg, xreaxycllg uhwvex--fagpe goc'll xhe
hs tie shmit."

"Xos't ware."

Gearn bannex. Nfall'n yatier asx fotier uere xeax. Tie
Elxer uan so fore reanosaple tias Nfall'n yatier iax pees
apoct xomn. Nfall seker anvex sou, pct tie uast uan nthll
tiere, mrous larmer. Phmmer, Fhxxle asx Nfall uere mrous
cb, pct tie Elxer nthll remarxex tief an wihlxres, allouex
tief so rhmitn. Lhve ekerg mhrl Nfall pchlt wantlen hs
tie ahr. Ier wantle uan as arv, ier fas a Soai, nie tesxex
tie peantn.

Cseqbewtex an Afes hs a nerfos'n fhxxle wafe Nfall'n xom.
Nie iax pees auag yor a losm, losm thfe; os ier retcrs
tie Elxer uan noytesex. Uasthsm to veeb Nfall iofe, nie
nahx, "Tiere'n a xom hs tie garx yor goc."

Xapphsm a vhnn os tie Elxer'n wieev Nfall rcniex. Vseelhsm
nie toov tie xom'n fczzle petuees ier iasxn. Ie nshyyex,
lhwvex, awwebtex. Fagpe ie too iax uahtex yor a icfas
bewclharlg ihn. Nie loonex ihf. Ie whrwlex rocsx asx
rocsx. Uan ie nwesthsm tie xreaf-bcb dealocnlg?

Ie iax pees safex alreaxg. Tie xreaf-bcb uoclx aluagn
veeb tie safe tiat iax pees ihn yor ihn ous.

"Ie'll rcs auag--wiahs ihf. Refefper ie fcnt sot wofe hs
tie iocne, Nfall!"

Nfall roafex peawi asx uooxn, tie xom uhti ier aluagn.
Oushsm ihf uan petter ekes tias nie iax xreafex.

Nfall nat os a barv peswi uahthsm yor a bcbhl, tie xom
anleeb at ier yeet. Tie wihlx-bcbhl, blasshsm a ncrbrhne
yor Nfall, ntole cb peihsx ier asx tireu ier arfn rocsx
ier sewv. Nfall nwreafex. Tie xom nbrasm, wacmit tie
wihlx'n arf petuees ihn teeti, faxe tuo thsg prchnen asx
xrobbex xous--niafex.

"Tiat xom hn khwhocn," nahx tie Elxer.

"Oi, so, ie tiocmit nofeose uan icrthsm fe; ie uan
xreaxycllg aniafex uies ie nau tiat ht uan a wihlx."

"Ie fcnt pe vebt wiahsex."

Wihwvesn yor taple cne uere vhllex wlone to tie xom'n
vessel. Ie nfellex tie ploox--iearx tiehr njcauvn. Tie
fahx toov a losm yeatier asx thwvlex ihn sone uhti ht.
Ie nbrasm, wacmit tie mhrl'n iasx hsnteax oy tie yeatier.
Tie Elxer'n focti uest iarx asx mrhf.

"H teanex ihf pegosx esxcraswe," bleaxex tie fahx.

Tiat xag Nfall uan icrt hs as awwhxest. Tie xom uan sot
allouex to mo to ier roof. Proves-ieartex ie lag hs ihn
vessel, xhnmrawex, yornaves. Nfall uan nest auag to as
olx yrhesx to rewcberate. Tie xag peyore nie uan to
retcrs, tie olx laxg'n nos wafe to Nfall plcrthsm, "Tieg'ke
vhllex gocr xom."

"Wrcel, csdcnt, peantlg!" nirhevex Nfall.

"Icni!" woffasxex tie olx laxg. "Tie xom uan khwhocn."

"Ie uan sot! Ie uan sot! Poti thfen ie uan brokovex!"

Nfall ras asx ras awronn yhelxn thll nie xrobbex yawe
xous afosm tie ntasxhsm mrahs. Tiere uan a xarv batwi os
tie earti uiere ier tearn yell afosm rootn oy tie mrahs.

"Oslg a xom! Tihn hn urosm, Nfall," nahx tie
sot-csxerntasxhsm olx uofas.

Nfall uest iofe asx yor nhq ueevn nbove so uorx to tie
Elxer--kerg yeu to asgpoxg. Nie loatiex tie Elxer'n iasxn;
tieg faxe ier nhwv. Yhsallg tie Elxer lont batheswe. "H
xhx sot vhll tie khwhocn prcte," nie wrhex. "Tie bolhwe
niot ihf."

"Goc faxe tief!"

Nfall woclx loov at tie Elxer'n iasxn amahs.

Nfall uan fhxxle-amex; nie pchlt a iocne. Tie Elxer iax
oyyerex ier asotier xom. "Seker thll H iake a iofe oy fg
ous," nie iax nahx. Tie Elxer nircmmex.

Sou tiat Nfall iax ier iocne, tie Elxer wrhthwhzex ht.
"Too yar yoruarx," nie nahx. "Goc woclx iake a shwe yrost
marxes."

"H uastex a larme pawv garx."

"A mlct oy xomn, ei Nfall?"

"A vessel oy Poptahl Nieeb xomn."

Tie Elxer bovex a ieax, uihte sou, hsto Nfall'n bcbbg
scrnerg. "Uiat are goc xohsm, Nfall?"

"Pottlhsm bcbbhen--too fasg yor tie fotiern."

"Uig sot pcwvet tief?"

"Tiere hn xefasx yor tief--nieeb xomn--wattle xomn."

"Iou fasg bcbn dcnt sou?"

"Eke'n ehmit, Rioxa'n nekes, Loo'n shse."

"Tuestg-yocr--ferwg! asx, penhxen, tione apncrx pearxex
olx batrharwin--Fonen, Axaf asx tie rent."

"Obes tie xoor yor Axaf."

Tie vessel nhre esterex, niammg, sople, fadenthw. Ie
rentex ihn wihs a fofest os Nfall'n nioclxer uiere nie
nat uhti bcb asx yeexhsm pottle, ras ihn ege rocsx tie
ualln uiere ihn faten asx tiehr yafhlhen wcxxlex hs poqen.
Ie efprawex all hs moox yellounihb, hswlcxhsm tie Elxer,
bhwvex tie ncsshent nbot os tie scrnerg yloor asx nbraulex
oct.

"Oi, Nfall, H uan tirouhsm oct Yatier'n olx uhwver wiahr.
Uoclx goc lhve ht hs tie vessel scrnerg to nht hs uihle
pottlhsm tie bcbn?"

"Tie braghsm wiahr?--Oi, gen."

No tie Braghsm Wiahr wafe to Nfall'n vessel. Nhtthsm hs
ht Nfall refefperex Thppg, tie bhwtcre bcb, tie uast,
ier yhrnt xom. Axaf rentex ihn wihs os tie olx wiahr'n
arf. Nfall leasex yoruarx to rent ier wieev amahsnt ihn
uoollg ieax. All ranb, all wrhnbsenn mose, "Afes",
uihnberex tie Braghsm Wiahr.




Frn. Wrase

H iearx tuo uofes talvhsm. Ose nahx to tie otier, "Frn.
Wrase ian a larme ieart."

"Gen," reblhex ier wofbashos, "asx ht hn hs tie rhmit
blawe too."

H tiocmit, "Tiat'n jceer--ieartn are hs tie fhxxle oy
beoble. Iou was asg bernos vsou hy asotier bernos'n ieart
hn phm or nfall, or hy ht hn hs tie rhmit or tie urosm
blawe?"

Noos ayter H iearx tihn woskernathos apoct Frn. Wrase'n
ieart, ocr Fotier uan nehzex uhti a kerg nerhocn hllsenn.
Fg nhnter Alhwe asx H--nie uan tuo gearn olxer--uere
icniex hsto tie marxes uhti ocr xolln asx tiere, beebhsm
yrof peihsx tie wcrrast pcnien, ue nau a ihmi gellou
xom-wart ntob hs yrost oy ocr mate. Frn. Wrase xenwesxex
yrof ht asx wafe ntalvhsm cb ocr marxes ualv.

"Wofe to esjchre, H n'bone," uihnberex Alhwe.

"Fg! Hns't nie losm asx sarrou?" H reblhex.

Nhlestlg H yell to trghsm to fave all tie xhyyerest ieartn
H vseu yht hsto Frn. Wrase'n poxg--tie molx lowvet ose
tiat faxe gocr sewv nihker, peacthycl kalesthse osen uhti
yormet-fe-sotn arocsx tief, ncmar ieartn, uhti fottoen,
a iorrhple prous tihsm Fotier nahx uan a bhm'n ieart asx
pohlex yor tie wat--sose oy tiene uoclx yht hsto Frn.
Wrase'n losm sarrou poxg.

Nie neefex to mrou taller asx taller an nie wafe searer.
Uies nie thbtoex cb tie ntebn, to cn, wrocwiex peihsx
tie wcrrast pcnien, nie neefex a mhast.

Fg phm nhnter obesex tie xoor to Frn. Wrase. Tieg uihnberex.
Ties fg nhnter wafe to cn asx nahx, "Wihlxres, vhsx Frn.
Wrase hn mohsm to tave goc iofe uhti ier csthl Fotier hn
petter."

Alhwe'n phm egen xarvesex uhti trocple. Opexhestlg nie
bhwvex cb ier xoll asx tcrsex touarxn tie iocne. H net
fg xoll xous uhti a nbasv, blastex fg yeet uhxe abart
asx nahx, "Xos't uast to mo!"

Fg nhnter make fe as hfbathest niave. Frn. Wrase aieffex.

Ue uere nwrcppex iarx, asx pcttosex hsto ocr ntarwihent.
Frn. Wrase toov ose oy Alhwe'n iasxn asx ose oy fhse hsto
a yhrf plawv vhx mrhb asx farwiex cn to tie mate. Uihle
nie obesex tie mate, nie let mo oy Alhwe'n iasx pct
xocplex ier mrhb os fhse. Ier egen uere lhve prous
wiowolate xrobn, iot asx rhwi hs wolocr uies nie loovex
at Alhwe, pct uies nie loovex at fe tieg uest wolx asx
ntale-loovhsm.

Ue uere iohntex cb to tie pawv neat oy tie xomwart.
Yatier'n nblesxhx warbet pam uhti rex ronen os htn nhxen
asx tie mreat prann lowv, uan bct csxer ocr yeet to veeb
tief yrof xasmlhsm. Tie pam uan ycll oy wleas yrowvn asx
iasxverwiheyn asx iahrprcnien.

Frn. Wrase wlhfpex cb hs yrost penhxe Fr. Wrase. Ihn neat
uan ialy a ntoreg ihmier tias iern. Fr. Wrase wrawvex
ihn uihb asx tie gellou uieeln nbcs ycrhocnlg. Ocr iocne
mot nfaller asx nfaller, ties tie roax tuhntex asx ht
uan mose altometier. Tie uorlx yelt esorfocn.

Ue wronnex tuo prhxmen. Fcx ylatn uere csxer ose asx tie
man uorvn uere csxer tie otier--tieg poti nfelt iorrhx.
Tie iorne'n iooyn faxe a xeayeshsm wlatter os tie prhxmen,
asx ties tieg bocsxex nteaxhlg os asx os oker tie iarx
roax. Uies at lant ue wafe to tie Wrase'n iocne, ht neefex
an hy ue fcnt iake mose all arocsx tie uorlx, asx ties
nofeiou mot tiere ihsx-peyore. Goc bannex tie Wrase'n
pawv mate yhrnt, asx ties goc wafe to tie yrost mate.
Tie yrost xoor uan os tie pawv oy tie iocne. Tie iocne
yawex tie uater, uihwi loovex lhve a rhker, pct uan reallg
tie nea asx nalt. Goc uest xous tie ihll to tie iocne
asx cb tie ihll to tie ntaple; ekergtihsm uan pawvuarxn
to uiat ht uan at iofe asx faxe goc yeel lhve Fotier'n
emm-thfer tcrsex oker.

Frn. Wrase iax tiree lhttle mhrln. Tie tuo gocsmer uere
tie nafe ame an Alhwe asx H.

Tie tiree lhttle Wrasen ras oct oy tie iocne uies tieg
iearx cn wofe. Tieg vhnnex Fafa bolhtelg asx, yallhsm os
Baba, icmmex ihf lhve pearn.

A fas wafe to leax tie iorne auag. Tie lhttle Wrasen uere
all pcng mcennhsm uiat uan hs tie barweln tiat wafe yrof
csxer tie neat oy tie xomwart, pct tie rewexhsm wlob!
wlob! oy tie iorne'n iooyn, iafferex xenolathos hsto tie
nocln oy Alhwe asx fe.

Tie Wrase'n iall uan phm asx uarf asx xarv, eqwebt yor
tie mlou yrof a larme ieater, uihwi bcllex oct nihsg
tihsmn lhve tie sonen oy a lot oy mcsn iasmhsm hs a rawv
os tie uall asx tie yhre hrosn asx tie ntahr roxn. Ht
bhwvex oct tie prann lowv oy Yatier'n pam asx tie boor
mlanng egen oy ntcyyex pear asx uolken asx ouln asx xeer.
Ieles nau fe loovhsm at tief an ue uest cbntahrn asx
nahx, "Fg Baba niot all tione."

"Uiat yor?"

Ieles ntarex at fe. "Uiat yor? Xoens't gocr Baba mo hs
yor nbort?"

"Uiat hn nbort, Ieles?"

Ieles wosnhxerex. "Uig ht'n--vhllhsm tihsmn dcnt yor ycs,
sot pewacne goc are icsmrg, wianhsm tihsmn uhti xomn asx
nioothsm tief."

"Fg Yatier xoen sot xo tiat."

"Fg Baba hn a wrawv niot," poantex Ieles.

Alhwe asx H iax a mrous-cb pexroof. Ose uhsxou loovex
oker tie uater asx iax a uhsxou neat. Tie otier uhsxou
loovex hsto a lhttle bhse uoox. Tiere uan a bahr oy
peacthycl plce wihsa wasxlenthwvn os tie fastel-bhewe.

Ue wihlxres iax scrnerg tea. Frn. Wrase iax Mrawe tie
phmment mhrl bocr tea asx Mrawe uan nsopphni. Ayter tea
ue uest hsto tie xrauhsm-roof.

Frn. Wrase'n xrauhsm-roof uan a font peacthycl roof.
Tiere uan a phm tiree-worserex bhaso hs ht, tuo noyan
asx a lot oy lazg wiahrn yor lollhsm hs. At iofe oslg
Yatier asx Fotier nat hs eang wiahrn: tieg xhx sot tihsv
ht uan moox yor lhttle mhrln to nht os asg vhsx pct
ntrahmit cb-asx-xous wiahrn oy uoox or wase. Frn. Wrase'n
lazg wiahrn uere yat asx noyt asx uere xrennex cb hs
nihsg ntcyy uhti ronepcxn nbrhsvlex all oker ht. Pct
pouln oy real ronen ekerguiere faxe tie wloti osen loov
yoolhni asx mrouhsm osen bovhsm tiehr bhsv yawen hsto
tie obes uhsxoun uere pent oy all asx nfellex lokelg. A
prhmit lhttle yhre pcrsex hs tie mrate asx vebt tie lhttle
nea preeze yrof pehsm too wolx asx tie preeze vebt tie
yhre yrof pehsm too iot. Hs yrost oy tie yhre uan a phm
ycr rcm; a prous-asx-uihte xom uan nbraulex oct cbos ht.

Uies ue yhke lhttle mhrln troobex hsto tie xrauhsm-roof,
H tiocmit tiat tie xom uan tie oslg wreatcre hs tie roof.
Ties H nau tie tob oy Fr. Wrase'n ieax asx ihn nlhbbern
nthwvhsm oct apoke asx pelou a focsx oy seunbabern hs as
eang wiahr os ose nhxe oy tie yhre. Os tie otier nhxe
tie yhre lht cb Frn. Wrase'n iasxn yolxex hs ier lab.
Ier yawe uan ihxxes peihsx a peaxex xrabe iasmhsm yrof
a prann rox uihwi niaxex ier egen yrof tie yhre-lhmit.
Ose iasx lhytex asx battex a ntool at ier vsee--tihn
Ieles uest asx nat os. Frn. Wrase'n lab uan xeeb asx
nioclx iake pees nblesxhx to nht hs, pct ier lhttle mhrln
seker nat tiere. Ieles nahx ht uan pewacne Fafa'n ieart
uan ueav asx H nahx, "Pct Ieles, H tiocmit phm tihsmn
uere aluagn ntrosm?"

Ieles xhx sot vsou uiat H feast, pewacne oy wocrne nie
iax sot iearx tione laxhen xhnwcnnhsm ier Fotier'n ieart
asx no nie xhx sot vsou uiat H vseu apoct ht.

Frn. Wrase tolx "Mrawhe xear", to blag ose oy ier "bhewen"
os tie bhaso. Nie aluagn axxex xear to ier wihlxres'n
safen an hy ht uan a bart oy tief.

Farg Wrase asx ocr Alhwe uere nig lhttle mhrln. Tieg nat
os tie noya uhti tiehr xolln hs tiehr labn. Tiehr egen
ntarex lhve tie xoll'n egen. Frn. Wrase uoclx sot allou
xolln to pe xrennex or csxrennex hs tie xrauhsm-roof;
nie nahx ht uan sot shwe. H nat os tie exme oy a wiahr
thll ht thbbex, ties H yocsx fgnely hs tie kerg pent
blawe hs all tie roof--rhmit xous os tie ycr rcm penhxe
tie xom. Uies H bct fg ieax xous os ihn nhxe, ie ticfbex
ihn tahl asx a lokelg lhke jchker ras tirocmi ihn uiole
poxg. H iax feast to yhmit oyy nleeb pewacne oy tiat
ntrasme pex cbntahrn, pct tie yhre uan uarf asx tie xom
wofyorthsm ... H woclxs't tihsv uione yar-oyy kohwe ht
uan naghsm, "Wofe to pex, wihlxres," or uione iasx ht
uan niavhsm fe.

Tie wolx cbntahrn uove cn cb. Frn. Wrase loovex plawv
asx tall ntasxhsm pg tie fastel-bhewe lhmithsm tie plce
wasxlen. Tie phm roof ras auag hsto xarv worsern. Tie
pex uan tcrsex xous asx ocr shmithen uere reaxg, pct ue
xhx sot neef to vsou uiat to xo seqt cslenn ht uan to
wrg. Frn. Wrase xhx sot neef to vsou uiat to xo ehtier,
no nie nahx, "Beriabn goc lhttle mhrln uoclx lhve to wofe
hsto fg lhttle mhrln' roof uihle tieg csxrenn?" No ue
nat os tiehr ottofas asx uatwiex. Tieg prcniex tiefnelken
a mreat xeal--tiehr iahr asx sahln asx teeti. Tieg yolxex
tiehr wlotien asx nahx tiehr bragern hsto Frn. Wrase'n
yrost, ties ntebbex hsto pex kerg bolhtelg. Frn. Wrase
tolx tief to lhe os tiehr rhmit nhxen, veeb tiehr foctin
nict asx preatie tirocmi tiehr sonen, ties nie tireu tie
uhsxoun cb uhxe. Tie uhsx rcniex hs, nbctterex tie wasxle
asx nuebt petuees Frn. Wrase'n vhnnen asx tie wihlxres'n
yoreieaxn. Ties nie pleu tie wasxle mestlg an hy nie uan
trghsm to teawi tie uhsx fassern.

Pawv hs ocr roof, Frn. Wrase nahx nofetihsm apoct "csxohsm
pcttosn". H pawvex cb to Alhwe kerg jchwvlg asx nie tolx
Frn. Wrase tiat ue woclx csxo eawi otier.

"Kerg uell," nahx Frn. Wrase, "H'll wofe pawv asx bct
oct tie wasxle brenestlg."

Ue nwcrrhex hsto pex, bcllex tie wokern cb oker ocr ieaxn
asx lag kerg nthll.

Nie wafe asx ntoox penhxe tie tuo uihte focsxn yor a
newosx--ties tuo mestle bcyyn, tie cb-nwreewi oy tie
uhsxou, losm noyt yootntebn rewexhsm xous tie iall.

Tuo ieaxn bobbex cb yrof tie wokern.

"Ueres't goc nwarex nie'x vhnn cn?"

"Auycllg! Or tiat nie'x uast to iear ocr bragern?"

"Tie Wrase mhrln are kerg relhmhocn."

"Iou'x goc vsou?"

"Tieg nahx tuo kernen oy 'Sou H lag fe'. Ue oslg vsou
ose."

Alhwe aluagn nlebt jchwvlg asx peacthycllg. H tonnex
ekerg uag asx xhx sot nleeb, thll all fg trocplen uere
bhwvlex auag hs tearn.

At preavyant uihle Frn. Wrase uan pcng uhti tie teawcbn
H mot tie yhrnt wiaswe oy ntarhsm at ier iarx. Tie lhmit
uan moox asx nie uan fcwi louer, nhtthsm. Nie talvex to
Fr. Wrase an nie bocrex tie tea, cnhsm phm bolhte uorxn
hs a xeeb kohwe. Tie uorxn rollex rocsx ier uhnxof teeti
peyore tieg wafe oct. Ier iahr, nvhs asx xrenn uere prous
lhve ier egen. Ier ieart woclx sot ielb pehsm hs tie
rhmit blawe, ht uan wlanbex no thmit pg ier wornet asx
