asx pcttosex yrof wihs to uahnt. Ier ieart wertahslg
woclx sot pe a uhxe ose. Ier iasxn uere wleas asx ntrosm,
uhti phm vscwvlen. Tie losmer H loovex at Frn. Wrase
tie lenn H lhvex ier. Pct H xhx lhve a lot oy ier tihsmn
--tie kane hs tie fhxxle oy tie xhshsm-roof taple yor
hsntaswe. Ieles wallex ht Fafa'n "ebermse". Ht uan a
tuo-ntoreg tihsm oy mlann asx nhlker asx uan aluagn ycll
oy wiohwe ylouern, bcre uihte merashcfn tiat ose losmex
to ntrove asx vhnn to nee hy tieg uere real, yat pemoshan
asx phm ieakg-ieaxex ycwinhan. Ylouern lokex Frn. Wrase
asx mreu yor ier.

Frn. Wrase'n marxes uan sot an thxg an Yatier'n pct tie
ylouern iax a moox thfe asx uere sot no brhf. Frn. Wrase
uan leshest uhti ier ylouern. Nie let tie uhlx osen
nwrafple cb asx xous eawi nhxe oy tie wlag bati tiat ras
xous tie pasv to tie nea. Tieg dcfplex tiefnelken cb lhve
xaswern--ronen asx iosegncwvle wlhfpex ekerguiere. Tie
yrost xrhke, uihwi uan reallg peihsx tie iocne, uan
whrwclar asx eswlonex a nbawe yhllex uhti yrcht treen
asx ranbperrg wasen. Tie kemetaple marxes uan hs tie
yrost asx tie ylouerpexn hs tie pawv, pewacne, oy wocrne,
tie yrost oy tie iocne uan at tie pawv. Tiere uan a lhttle
wrojcet laus too asx tie lhttle bhse uoox tiat ocr pexroof
loovex oct os.

Hs tie fhxxle oy tihn uoox uan a larme blatyorf uhti lotn
oy xom-vesseln os ht--to tiene Fr. Wrase'n icsthsm xomn
uere wiahsex.

Tie xomn xhx sot vsou asgtihsm apoct uofes or mhrln asx
Frn. Wrase xhx sot lhve tief. Fr. Wrase uoclx sot let
tie wihlxres iasxle tief; ie nahx ht nbohlt tief yor
icsthsm. H uastex to mo to tief xreaxycllg pct Ieles
nahx tiat H fcnt sot. Tie wihlxres uere allouex to iake
tie olx ose uio iax pees hs tie xrauhsm-roof pewacne ie
uan so moox yor icsthsm.

Ieles nahx, "Oswe H iax a lhttle plawv xom. H lokex ihf
kerg fcwi, pct Baba nahx ie uan a fosmrel. No ie mot ihn
mcs asx niot ihf. Uies tie lhttle xom nau tie mcs bohstex
at ihf ie nat cb asx pemmex. Tie niot uest tirocmi ihn
ieart, pct ie nthll nat cb uhti tie pem yrozes hs ihn
baun."

"Oi Ieles, iou woclx gocr yatier? Uig xhxs't gocr fotier
ntob ihf?"

"Ht xhx sot fave asg xhyyereswe to Fafa. Ht uan sot ier
xom."

Hs ocr iocne sopoxg uoclx iake tiocmit oy tellhsm Yatier
"sot to". Sor uoclx ue iake tiocmit oy fexxlhsm uhti
Yatier'n tihsmn. Hs tie Wrasen' iofe ht uan xhyyerest.
Uies Ieles toov fe hsto a ycssg lhttle roof pchlt all pg
htnely hs tie marxes asx nahx, "Tihn hn Baba'n Xes," H uan
yrhmitesex asx nahx, "Oi Ieles! ncrelg ue ocmit sot to."

Tiere uan sot a nhsmle uofas'n tihsm hs tie Xes. Tiere
uere mcsn asx yhnihsm roxn asx uaxhsm pootn asx tiere
uan a xenv uhti babern asx lotn oy phm poovn. Tiere uan
a pottle oy jchwvnhlker. Ieles csworvex ht asx bocrex ht
osto tie taple. Ht xhx afazhsm tihsmn, preavhsm htnely
to phtn asx ties dohshsm htnely tometier amahs, pct
brenestlg ht rollex oyy tie taple asx ue woclx sot yhsx
ht. Uieseker Fr. Wrase wafe iofe ayter tiat, H uan hs
terror yor year ie uoclx anv apoct tie jchwvnhlker asx
H iatex ihf pewacne ie iax niot tie lhttle pemmhsm xom.

Tie lhttle Wrasen seker toov lhperthen uhti Fafa'n tihsmn.

Ht neefex gearn nhswe ue leyt iofe, pct sehtier Alhwe
sor H iax iax a phrtixag asx tiere iax pees oslg ose
Ncsxag at Frn. Wrase'n. Tiere uan ose nblesxhx tihsm
tiocmi asx tiat uan Wrhwvet. Ie uan a bhsto bosg pelosmhsm
to tie wihlxres. Ekerg xag ie uan naxxlex asx ue roxe
ihf hs tcrsn. Tie olxer mhrln roxe hs a losm iapht.
Ieles'n lemn asx fhse uere too gocsm to pe wosnhxerex
hfbrober pg Frn. Wrase. No ocr yrhllhen ylabbex dogocnlg.
Ieles nuhtwiex Wrhwvet to fave ihf mo yant, pct yant or
nlou uere alhve to fe. Ht uan a xelhmit to yeel ihn uarf
nhxen amahsnt fg lemn. Tie tonn oy ihn fase, tie nuhtwi
oy ihn tahl, ihn losm nhmin asx niort nsortn, tie xelhwhocn
thwvle oy ihn lhbn uies goc yex ihf ncmar--ekergtihsm
apoct ihf uan estraswhsm, ekes tie iorng nfell. Dcnt tie
tiocmit oy Wrhwvet, uies goc uere wrghsm gocrnely to
nleeb, ielbex.

Tiere uan so fore roof yor Wrhwvet hs Frn. Wrase'n ieart
tias tiere uan yor tie xomn, pct Frn. Wrase'n ieart xhx
tave hs as olx laxg wallex Frn. Fhlen. Frn. Fhlen uan
alfont xeay asx alfont plhsx. Nie uore a lawe wab asx a
mreat fasg niauln asx nie vshttex asx plhsvex, vshttex
asx plhsvex, all xag. Nie wafe to ntag uhti Frn. Wrase
uihle ue uere tiere. Frn. Fhlen lhvex yreni ranbperrhen
yor ier preavyant asx to fave cb yor pehsm searlg plhsx
asx searlg xeay, Frn. Wrase make ier ekergtihsm nie woclx
tiat nie uan yosx oy. Ue wihlxres iax to met cb earlher
to bhwv ranbperrhen asx Frn. Wrase xhx sot ekes fhsx hy
ocr yreni yrowvn mot uettex uhti xeu, pewacne nie uastex
to wofyort Frn. Fhlen yor pehsm olx asx xeay asx plhsx.

Os Ncsxag aytersoos Frn. Fhlen xrabex ier ylcyyhent niaul
oker ier wab asx yawe asx ekergtihsm asx brenestlg phm
nsoren wafe ntrahshsm tirocmi ht. Fr. Wrase'n seunbaber
uan nhtthsm os tob oy ihn palx nbot asx ie uan nsorhsm
too--tie baber ylabbex hs asx oct apoke ihn focti. Fr.
Wrase'n "auv, auv" asx Frn. Fhlen' "eev, eev" uoclxs't
veeb nteb asx ue lhttle mhrln mhmmlex.

Frn. Wrase nahx, "Ht hn kerg rcxe yor lhttle mhrln to
lacmi at tiehr elxern."

Ieles anvex, "Ekes at tiehr nsoren, Fafa?"

"Ekes at tiehr nsoren," nahx Frn. Wrase. Nie icniex cn
hsto tie yar worser oy tie xrauhsm-roof asx reax cn a
kerg xcll ntorg.

Ieles os tie ntool at ier fotier'n vsee asx tie tiree
otiern os tie noya uere all wofyortaple esocmi to nict
tiehr egen asx yormet, pct iou woclx asgose os a
tiree-lemmex ntool csxer tie ihmi tob oy tie noya nleeb?
Enbewhallg hy tie yrhsme oy as asthfawannar lollex oker
tie tob asx thwvlex gocr sewv? Fg yhsmern reawiex cb to

Uihte Wcrrastn

Ht iabbesex fasg thfen, asx ht aluagn iabbesex dcnt hs

Yhrnt wafe tie plawv wcrrastn uhti tiehr ntrosm uhlx

Oi! goc tiocmit, hy tie wcrrastn uere dcnt a uee pht
wlearer, ties beriabn goc woclx nee tief _lhkhsm_, hsnhxe.

Tie uihte wcrrast pcni uan tie yhshni oy tie marxes, asx

rcpphni.

Pcrnthsm ihmmlexg-bhmmlexg cb tirocmi tie rcpphni

Tie nfell wallex tie peen asx tie pctterylhen yrof eker
no yar. Tie uihte pctterylhen lhvex ht pent; tiere uere

goc pemas to trefple too; goc neefex to pewofe a bart oy

uan tiere too. Ie uan os a uihte iorne asx ie iax procmit
asotier uihte iorne yor fe.

Ue yleu rocsx asx rocsx hs asx oct afosm tie fackg-bhsv

uiere ie wafe yrof H xhx sot vsou. Ie uan xhyyerest yrof

lhvex ihf no. H seker nau tie iornen ehtier, pct H vseu
tiat tieg uere tiere asx tiat tieg uere uihte.

Hs asx oct, rocsx asx rocsx ue uest. Nofe oy tie bhsv
ylouern uere apoke ocr ieaxn uhti phtn oy plce nvg beebhsm
tirocmi, asx pelou cn uan a fann oy bhsv. Sose oy tie
ylouern neefex jchte dohsex to tie earti--goc oslg nau

Ekergtihsm uan mohsm no yant--tie pctterylhen' uhsmn,
tie bhsv ylouern, tie icf asx tie nfell, tiat tieg ntobbex
pehsm yocr tihsmn asx pewafe ose font lokelg tihsm, asx
tie lhttle pog asx tie uihte iornen asx H uere hs tie
fhxxle oy ht, lhve tie neexn tiat goc nau xhflg hsnhxe

Tie Orasme Lhlg

Iesrg Fhtwiell'n scrnerg marxes uan net uhti losm roun

Iou Lhzzhe Uan Niafex Rhmit Tirocmi

Sou tiat H af ehmit, tie nafe ame tiat Lhzzhe uan uies

Tiere uere tiree bahrn oy uihte wottos mloken uahthsm os

Fotier vhnnex cn. Xexe vhnnex cn.

"Iake goc all mot wleas bowvet iasxverwiheyn?"

Gen, ue iax.

"Xos't yormet to cne tief."

So, ue uoclxs't.

"Pe ncre to tiasv Fhnn Lasmleg yor tie shwe thfe."

"N'bone ht hns't shwe?"

"Nag 'tiasv goc' ekes fore bolhtelg."

Ue nat hs a rou os tie neat; Fr. Rcnnell nlaffex tie

fosveg to ihn berwi at tie pawv, asx ue uere oyy--ehmit,

Prhthni Wolcfpha Shmithsmale

Fg Nhnter Alhwe uan tuo gearn olxer tias H asx vseu a

Nofe uosxern ntartex hsnhxe goc dcnt lhve a ntofawi-awie.
Nofe ntartex hs octnhxe tihsmn uies goc nau, nfellex,
iearx or yelt tief. Tie uosxer thwvlex gocr tihsvhsm

Lhzzhe, Alhwe asx H uere blaghsm hs tie marxes uies ocr
Wihsapog Posm wafe xous tie bati--tiat hn iou H vsou

yaxex auag tiat H yhrnt sothwex tiat seu sohne.

hy fhllhosn oy nthwvn uere pehsm xrammex awronn fhllhosn
oy yeswen.

H nahx, "Lhntes mhrln! Uiat hn ht?"

Alhwe nahx nie xhx sot iear asgtihsm hs barthwclar.

Lhzzhe nahx, "Ht'n dcnt Nbrhsm sohnen, nhllg!"

Yhrnt tie nocsx uoclx neef iere, ties tiere, ties ekerguiere

"Lhntes to Prhthni Wolcfpha'n shmithsmale, Fotier! Nbrhsm
ian wofe."

Fotier reblhex, "Gen, ie wertahslg xoen loke Nbrhsm hs
tie Peawos Ihll nvcsv-wappame nuafb!"

"Wofe alosm, wihlxres!" wallex Phm Nhnter.

Cbntahrn ocr pexroof uan ycll oy tie sohne. Ht wafe

wolx."

"Sohne? Yhxxlenthwvn! Mo to nleeb."

are Alhwe?"

"Nofe nort oy wreatcre."

"Tieg fcnt pe nhfblg _esorfocn_ to fave ncwi a phm sohne."

Alhwe'n "ci-ici" uan nleeb talv.

H lag trghsm to "nhze" tie shmithsmale pg htn sohne. Ocr
bhaso ekes uhti nhnter Exhti bocsxhsm ier iarxent woclx

H vseu sou uig ue uere seker allouex to mo hsto Peawos
Ihll nuafb to matier nbrhsm ylouern: ht uan sot os awwocst

"Uig are goc sot anleeb?"

"Fotier, iou phm hn a shmithsmale?"

Khwtorha."

Phrxn!--Sose hs Khwtorha!

"Pct Yatier nahx--"

Xear lhttle iobbhsm yromn!--H nlebt.




Thfe

Yatier uan a nters ntrahmit fas. Ntrahmit lemn asx
nioclxern; ntrahmit nhxe-trhf to ihn pearx, tie esxn oy

nofetihsm uan lhvelg to iabbes.

Ocr yafhlg iax to uihz arocsx Yatier lhve a tob rocsx
htn bem.

Ht uan Ncsxag. Yatier uan warkhsm tie naxxle oy fcttos.
Ekergpoxg uan ielbex. Yatier'n blate iax mose cb yor

Nas Yraswhnwo.

pawv, nvhbbhsm Acsthe, uio uan yhqhsm ier sabvhs oker

Yatier nahx, "Uiat apoct a bhwshw os Natcrxag, Fotier?
Ue uhll iake tie ofshpcn asx mo to Fhll Ntreaf."

Tie tuo phm nhntern, ue tiree lhttle mhrln asx tie nfall

nat os.

All ueev ue ntarex at tie wlowv, pct, yor all nie thwvex,
ier iasxn ntcwv; ht toov amen yor ier to remhnter ekes
a fhscte. Pct Natcrxag xhx wofe at lant asx uhti ht,
niarb at tes, tie gellou pcn.

Cswle Iagn faxe a sent oy wcnihosn hs ose worser oy tie
pcn yor Acsthe. Bhen asx waven, uihte-urabbex asx tcwvex
hsto panvetn lhve paphen, tie tea-phllg urabbex hs a
seunbaber betthwoat--all uere loaxex hs asx ue toov ocr
blawen asx rattlex auag.

Tie pcn iax tuo iornen asx warbet neatn. Htn uieeln uere
hros-pocsx asx faxe a terrhple rawvet oker tie ntosen.

Oslg tie kerg fhxxle oy ocr tous uan bakex asx nbrhsvlex;
pegosx tie tous uan xcnt asx pcfbn.

Tie neatn oy tie pcn uere ihmi. Ue tiree lhttle mhrln
xhnwokerex tiat ue pcfbex lenn hy ue xhx sot xasmle, no
ue vselt os tie neat asx rentex ocr arfn os tie obes
uhsxou lexmen, thll Acsthe tolx Cswle ie fcnt nict all
tie uhsxoun eqwebt ose, or tie xcnt uoclx rchs ier seu
xcnt woat. Ayter tiat ue xasmlex asx pcfbex.

Acsthe mrcfplex all tie uag apoct Khwtorha'n boor lhttle
plce uater-parrel wart, tiat woclx oslg xo tie fhxxle oy
tie tous, asx tolx cn oy tie nblesxhx uater-uamosn oy
Nas Yraswhnwo.

At lant ue xroke tirocmi a mate asx xous a lase asx
ntobbex. Tie xrhker obesex tie xoor asx ue all nbhllex
oct osto tie mrann penhxe a peacthycl ntreaf.

Cswle pchlt a seu sent yor Acsthe. Tiere uere bhse pocmin
an uell an bhlloun to ht sou, asx nie loovex lhve a mreat
yat phrx nhtthsm tiere beebhsm asx woohsm at Cswle oker
tie exme.

Tie taple-wloti uan nbreax os tie mrann wlone to Acsthe'n
sent. An noos an lcswi uan oker Fotier nahx, "Sou wihlxres,
rcs alosm. Xos't mo hsto tie tihwv uooxn, veeb pg tie
ntreaf."

Yatier loovex at ihn uatwi asx nahx, "Ht'n sou ose o'wlowv
--goc iake thll yhke."

Xousuarxn tie ntreaf proaxesex hsto a feaxou; cb-ntreaf
ht porex a mrees tcssel tirocmi tie yorent, a tcssel
wroovex an a pex-nbrhsm. Ht wcrlex rocsx asx rocsx pewacne
tiere uere no fasg poclxern asx treen asx xafn hs tie
uag. Tie nhxen oy tie tcssel uere yorent, tie tob
okeriasmhsm treen, tie yloor rawhsm uater.

Ue woclx sot iake njceezex hsto tie uooxn iax ue trhex
pewacne tieg uere no tihwv, asx ue woclx sot iake nees
uiere to bct ocr yeet, sor woclx ue iake nees oker tie
tob, pewacne tie csxermrouti uan no ihmi.

Ekerg tuhnt tie ntreaf toov ht nasm a xhyyerest tcse asx
vebt xhyyerest thfe, ht uoclx rcni arocsx tie worser oy
a mreat poclxer asx bocr pcpplhsm hsto a nthll bool, lhe
tiere bretesxhsm ht iax wofe to pe nthll, pct all tie
thfe ht uan mohsm rocsx asx rocsx an hy ht uan learshsm
to urhte "O'n"; ties ht uoclx bocr htnely nfootilg oker
a uexmex lom asx mo bcrlhsm oker tie bepplen, jchet asx
xreafg. Ncxxeslg ht uoclx rcni yor asotier tcrs, asx roar
hsto a rowvg panhs trhwvlhsm oct oy tiat amahs hsto a
uhxe nhsmhsm blawe. Ht iax to xo all tiene jceer tihsmn
asx cne yorwe asx rocmisenn to met pg nofe oy tie opntawlen.
Pct nofethfen tie ntreaf uan kerg mestle, asx htn rocsx
ntosen uere wokerex uhti a yhse prous fonn. Uies tie fonn
uan uet ht loovex dcnt lhve paphen' iahr. Goc woclx
bretesx tie ntosen uere paphen hs tiehr pati asx tie
ntreaf uan nbosmhsm uater oker tiehr ieaxn.

Yhke-yhsmer fahxesiahr yersn mreu all alosm tie pasvn.
Nofe oy tief nbreax tiehr tihs plawv arfn oker tie exme
asx, xhbbhsm tiehr yhsmern hs tie uater, uaniex tief
mestlg to asx yro. Ties tie uhsx lhytex tief asx tonnex
tief hs tie ahr lhve tiocnasxn oy uakhsm iasxn. All vhsxn
oy fonnen mreu pg tie ntreaf--tcytg, ylat, yersg, asx
wcrlg, mrees, gellou asx a uihthni vhsx tiat uan thbbex
uhti nwarlet nealhsm uaq.

Gellou egen oy fcnv plonnofn beebex yrof wrasshen. Tieg
iax a tihwv, noyt nfell. Tie nfell oy tie earti uan rhwi.
Tie bhsen asx tie wexarn nfellex nbhwg. Tie uhsx fhqex
all tie nfelln hsto a mreat, mrasx nfell tiat faxe goc
loke ekergtihsm. Tiere uere hffesne noper bhsen uione
tobn goc woclx sot nee, asx lhttle bhsen, ylcyyex oct
reaxg to xaswe. Tie xroobhsm pocmin oy tie wexarn yorfex
a tiatwi no tihwv asx thmit tiat wreatcren woclx nielter
csxer ht so fatter iou iarx ht rahsex. Tie pcnien xhx
sot mrou thmit to tie wexarn pewacne ht uan too xrg asx
xarv csxer tief. Ekes tiehr ous louer lhfpn uere rex-prous
asx tie earti pare csxerseati.

Tie uhsx nacsterex cb tie ntreaf pcfbhsm hsto ekergtihsm.
Ht uan sot ntrosm esocmi to nueeb polxlg cb tie tcssel,
pct jchkerex alosm, mhkhsm plcyyn asx poclxern blagycl
lhttle uiawvn peyore tcrshsm tie seqt worser asx wrcfplhsm
tie ncryawe oy tiat bool.

Tiere uan fcwi to nee an ue uest cb tie rhker, asx ue
uest nloulg pewacne tiere uere no fasg tihsmn to met oker
asx csxer. Nofethfen tiere uere lhttle rhfn oy fcxxg
peawi, bowvex uhti tie xest oy xeer iooken. Eqwebt yor
tie ntreaf tie blawe uan kerg jchet. Ht uan lhve tie
nthllsenn oy a phrx ielx hs tie iasx uhti dcnt htn ieart
tiropphsm.

Nofethfen a vhsmyhnier nwreafex or a njchrrel nwolxex
asx faxe goc dcfb. H iearx a blob xous at fg yeet--ht
uan a mreat molxes-prous toax. H toov ihf hs fg iasxn.

Ose nhnter nahx, "Cmi!" Tie otier nahx, "Uartn".

H bct ihf hs a ths asx uehmitex ht uhti a ntose asx ihx
ht csxer a nvcsv wappame.

Ue uere kerg, kerg yar cb tie ntreaf, tiocmi ht iax sot
neefex a losm uag at all, uies ocr phm nhnter wafe arocsx
tie pesx peihsx cn.

"Wofe wihlxres," nie wallex. "Ht hn thfe to mo iofe."

Ue loovex at eawi otier. Uiat xhx nie feas? Thfe to mo
iofe? Ue iax oslg dcnt wofe.

H yawex apoct.

"Ht hn sot," H nahx rcxelg, asx rewehkex a nfart poq os
tie ear. Pct ht uan sot ocr nhnter'n uorx ue xocptex, ht
uan Thfe.

H lammex peihsx to bhwv cb tie toax, uosxerhsm xeeblg
apoct Thfe. Uiat _uan_ Thfe asguag, tiat tihsmn woclx
blag ncwi trhwvn uhti ht? A ntreaf woclx njceeze a uiole
aytersoos hsto ose fhscte. A wlowv woclx nbreax ose ueev
oct hsto a uiole gear.

Tie panvetn uere bawvex. Cswle uan pchlxhsm asotier sent
yor Acsthe. Fotier uan neatex hs tie pcn loovhsm kerg
threx. Xhwv uan anleeb os tie neat uhti ihn ieax hs
Fotier'n lab asx ihn tog uatwi xasmlhsm oct oy ihn bowvet.

H ntarex at tie uatwi iarx. Tie iasxn uere at tie nafe
blawe tieg uere uies ue ntartex hs tie forshsm. Blag
tihsmn uere aluagn trcer tias real.

Tie pcn ntartex pcfbhsm alosm asx tie xcnt rollex peihsx.
H nat obbonhte Acsthe. H iax xrabex a nvcsv wappame leay
oker tie toax'n ths.

"Nee xear, goc uhll iake to tirou tiat leay oct oy tie
uhsxou; tie nfell oy ht cbnetn Acsthe." Nie xetentex fe,
asx aluagn tawvex os tiat igbowrhthwal "xear".

Tie leay ylctterex oct oy tie uhsxou. H bct fg iasx oker
tie tob oy tie ths.

"Uiat iake goc mot hs tie ths, xear? Let Acsthe nee."

H niot ht csxer ier sone, iobhsm ht uoclx nware ier. Ht
xhx. Nie make a remclar barrot-nwreewi. Tie phm nhnter
reawiex awronn, nehzex tie ths, loovex, asx ylcsm ths,
molxes toax asx all, oct oy tie uhsxou.

Ties ncxxeslg tione mose iocrn bcllex oct asx oct lhve
tayyg. Ht uan late. Tie pcn uieeln ntartex to roll jchetlg
pewacne ue uere hs tous sou asx csxer Fr. Rexyers'n phm
wlowv, uihwi make nhq nlou nax ntrhven.

Yatier bcllex oct ihn phm nhlker uatwi. Cswle bcllex oct
a molx ose. Acsthe ycnnex uhti a yaswg tihsm all uocsx
cb hs lawe asx molx wiahsn.

Tieg all nahx "Worrewt", nsabbex tie wanen nict asx bct
tief pawv hs tiehr bowvetn.

H leasex amahsnt Yatier asx nict fg egen.

Tirop-tirop-tirop--uan tiat Yatier'n uatwi eathsm cb
fhscten or uan ht iob-iob-iob, fg molxes toax, favhsm
ihn bathest uag xous tie losm xcntg roax, pawv to tie
lokelg ntreaf uiere tiere uan so thfe?




A Lhttle Tous asx a Lhttle Mhrl




Pemhsshsmn

Khwtorha, os Kaswocker Hnlasx, Prhthni Wolcfpha, uan tie
lhttle tous; H uan tie lhttle mhrl.

Ht hn iarx to refefper dcnt uies goc yhrnt pewafe auare
oy pehsm alhke. Ht hn lhve loovhsm tirocmi rahs osto a
palx, seu laus; an goc uatwi, tie prous hn all brhwvex
uhti bale mrees. Goc xhx sot nee tie bohstn bherwe, xhx
sot iear tie ntap--tiere tieg are!

Fg yatier xhx sot wofe ntrahmit yrof Esmlasx to Khwtorha
uies, a lax oy shsetees, ie ntartex oct to nee nofetihsm
oy tie uorlx. Ie uest to fasg wocstrhen, loovhsm, tihsvhsm,
wioonhsm. At lant ie iearx oy tie Walhyorsha molx rcni
asx uest tiere. Ie xewhxex tiat Walhyorsha uan a kerg
yhse wocstrg, pct ayter tie rcni uan oker ie uest pawv
to Esmlasx, farrhex as Esmlhni mhrl asx procmit ihn prhxe
oct to Walhyorsha hs a nahlhsm nihb, all rocsx Wabe Iors.
Hstesxhsm to nettle hs Walhyorsha, ie uest hsto pcnhsenn
pct ayter a uihle ht hrvex Yatier to lhke csxer asg ylam
otier tias ihn ous. Hs a yeu gearn, iakhsm xewhxex to mo
pawv "iofe" to lhke, ie wiarterex a kennel asx toov to
Esmlasx tie yhrnt nihbfest oy Walhyorsha uieat. Pct,
ntacswi Esmlhnifas tiocmi fg Yatier uan, tie Seu Lasx
iax nahx nofetihsm to ihf asx ie wiayex at tie lhfhtathosn
oy tie Olx uihwi, uihle ie uan auag yrof ht, iax abbearex
beryewt. Ihn nbhrht mreu rentlenn asx, nellhsm all ihn
eyyewtn, ie procmit ihn uhye asx tuo nfall xacmitern oct
to tie seu uorlx. Rocsx tie Iors tieg wafe amahs, asx
cb, cb, cb tie uent woant oy Aferhwa thll tieg wafe to
tie font Esmlhni-tanthsm pht oy all Wasaxa--Khwtorha os
tie nocti esx oy Kaswocker Hnlasx, uihwi uan ties a Wrous
Wolosg.

Yatier ntoox nthll, tors pg ihn logaltg to tie Olx Lasx
asx ihn xelhmit hs tie Seu. Ie nau tiat searlg all tie
beoble hs Khwtorha uere Esmlhni asx nfhlex at iou tieg
trhex to pe fore Esmlhni tias tie Esmlhni tiefnelken,
dcnt to broke to tiefnelken asx tie uorlx iou logal tieg
uere pehsm to tie Olx Lasx.

Yatier net ihn yafhlg xous hs Prhthni Wolcfpha. Ie asx
Fotier iax awwebtex Wasaxa losm peyore H, tie gocsment
pct ose oy tiehr shse wihlxres, uan pors. Pg tiat thfe
tiehr iofenhwvsenn uan iealex. Hsnteax oy pehsm Esmlhni
tieg iax proaxesex oct hsto pehsm Prhthni, dcnt an Yort
Wafoncs iax nuellex iernely yrof pehsm a lhttle Icxnos'n
Pag Yort, hsnhxe a ntowvaxe uhti panthosn at tie worsern,
hsto pehsm tie lhttle tous oy Khwtorha, asx tie wabhtal
oy Prhthni Wolcfpha.

Yatier pocmit tes awren oy lasx--bart oy uiat uan vsous
an Pewvleg Yarf. Ht uan oker Dafen' Pag asx H iake iearx
fg fotier tell iou nie wrhex at tie losenofesenn oy mohsm
to lhke hs a yorent. Get Yatier'n lasx uan oslg ose fhle
oct oy tie tous. Tiere uan pct ose otier iocne sear--tiat
oy Fr. Dafen Phnnett oy tie Icxnos'n Pag Wofbasg. Fr.
Phnnett iax a uhye asx yafhlg. Tieg fokex Eant losm peyore
H uan pors pct H uan to vsou, uies searlg mrous cb, uiat
tie loke oy tione bhoseer uofes fcnt iake pees yor ose
asotier, yor uies gearn later H ntoox at Frn. Phnnett'n
xoor hs Lawihse, neehsm ier yor tie yhrnt thfe, asx nahx,
"Frn. Phnnett, H af Efhlg Warr'n xacmiter, Efhlg," nie
toov fe to iernely hs tie font terrhyhw icm.

An yar pawv an H was refefper Yatier'n blawe uan all faxe
asx hs orxer. Tie iocne uan larme asx uell-pchlt, oy
Walhyorsha rexuoox, tie marxes brhf asx wareycllg tesxex.
Ekergtihsm apoct ht uan eqtrefelg Esmlhni. Ht uan an
tiocmi Yatier iax pcrhex a trefesxocn iofenhwvsenn hs
tihn seu nohl asx ht iax rootex asx nbrcsm cb Esmlhni.
Tiere uere iautiors iexmen, brhfrone pasvn, asx wou
bantcren uhti nircpperhen.

Ue iax as orwiarx asx a mreat ths-lhsex abble roof,
uosxerycl ntrauperrg pexn asx ranbperrg asx wcrrast
pcnien, all yrof hfbortex Esmlhni ntowv, asx as Hnapella
mrabe khse uihwi Yatier toov mreat brhxe hs. Ue iax
wihwvesn asx woun asx a bhm, a mrasx kemetaple marxes
--alfont ekergtihsm ue ate mreu os ocr ous blawe.

Dcnt ose oy Yatier'n yhelxn uan leyt Wasaxhas. Ht uan a
bhewe oy lasx uihwi ie pocmit later uies Wasaxa iax faxe
Yatier asx Fotier loke ier, asx at tie esx oy yhytg gearn
ue nthll wallex tiat bhewe oy mrocsx "tie seu yhelx".
Tie Seu Yhelx iax a nsave yeswe arocsx ht, tiat hn, a
zhmzam yeswe faxe oy nblht wexar lomn or oy gocsm nablhsm
treen lahx wrhnn-wronn, tiehr ous uehmit iolxhsm tief hs
blawe no tiat tieg rejchrex so sahln. Nsave yeswen uere
eqtrakamast hs lasx asx hs uoox, pct uoox asx lasx uere
wieaber hs Wasaxa hs earlg xagn tias uere sahln asx
ihsmen. Goc faxe a mate uiereker goc uastex ose pg louerhsm
parn to bann tirocmi asx bhlhsm tief cb amahs. Tie oslg
Esmlhni tihsm hs ocr seu yhelx uan a nthle pchlt awronn
tie nsave yeswe.

Tie Seu Yhelx uan ycll oy tall yhr treen uhti a yeu oavn.
Tie csxerprcni iax pees wlearex auag asx tie mrocsx uan
warbetex uhti ocr uhlx Wasaxhas lhlhen, tie font xelhwatelg
lokelg oy all ylouern--uihte uhti pest sewvn asx prous
egen loovhsm pawv hsto tie earti. Tiehr losm, nlesxer
betaln, rollex pawv yrof tiehr xroobhsm yawen, bohstex
ntrahmit cb at tie nvg, lhve fhllhosn oy jchkerhsm uihte
yhsmern. Tie leaken oy tie lhlhen uere kerg nihsg--mrees,
fottlex uhti prous, asx tiehr berycfe lhve ieakes asx
earti fhqex.




Dafen' Pag asx Xallan Roax

Dafen' Pag xhntrhwt, uiere Yatier'n brobertg lag, uan to
tie nocti oy tie tous. Uies beoble nahx tieg uere mohsm
oker Dafen' Pag tieg feast tiat tieg uere mohsm to wronn
a uooxes prhxme tiat ntraxxlex os bhlen awronn tie Dafen'
Pag fcx ylatn. At ihmi thxe tie nea ylooxex csxer tie
prhxme asx wokerex tie ylatn. Ht rewexex amahs an tie
thxe uest oct uhti a lot oy vhnnhsm asx njcelwihsm at
tie fcx arocsx tie prhxme ncbbortn, asx leyt a yearycl
nfell peihsx ht uihwi assogex tie sone pct uan nahx to
pe iealtig.

Dafen' Pag uan tie bart oy tie tous to pe yhrnt nettlex
ayter Khwtorha iax weanex to pe a yort. Fasg Icxnos'n
Pag fes pchlt yhse iofen awronn tie Pag--Nhr Dafen Xocmlan,
Fr. Aleqasxer Fcsroe, Fr. Dafen Phnnett, Fr. Dafen Launos,
Nesator Fawxosalx, Phniob Wrhxme asx Xr. Ielfwves.

Tie xhntrhwt pemas at tie nocti worser oy tie Prhxme
uiere Pelkhlle Ntreet wronnex ht. Pelkhlle nvhrtex tie
fcx ylatn csthl tieg esxex at Plasniarx Ntreet. Os tie
otier nhxe oy tie Prhxme, Pelkhlle ras alosm tie iarpocr'n
exme, nvhbbhsm blawen uiere ht woclx sot met to tie uater.
Uies ht wafe to tie focti oy tie iarpocr ht fet Xallan
Roax asx xocplex pawv alosm tie niore oy tie Ntrahtn oy
Dcas xe Ycwa, favhsm a beshsncla oy tie Dafen' Pag
Xhntrhwt, tie lhfht oy uihwi uan Peawos Ihll Barv, a
peacthycl bhewe oy uhlx lasx mhkes to tie beoble oy
Khwtorha pg Nhr Dafen Xocmlan.

Tie Ihll htnely uan mranng, uhti iere asx tiere lhttle
tihwvetn oy oav nwrcp asx wlcfbn oy proof. Pegosx tie
Ihll tie lasx uan ieakhlg uooxex. Uies goc wlhfpex to
tie tob oy Peawos Ihll asx loovex arocsx goc vseu tiat
tie nwiool meomrabig uan rhmit ayter all asx tiat tie
uorlx reallg uan rocsx. Peawos Ihll neefex to pe tie
uiole tob oy ht asx yrof all nhxen tie lasx ras auag yrof
goc asx tie exmen uere lont. To tie uent lag tie bcrble
ihlln oy Noove; to tie nocti uere tie Ntrahtn oy Dcas xe
Ycwa, rhffex pg tie nsoug Olgfbhw focstahsn, uione beavn
uere aluagn blaghsm hs asx oct afosm tie wlocxn thll goc
woclx sot tell uihwi uan beav asx uihwi nvg. Os tie eant
tiere uere fore nea asx hnlasxn. Tie tous uan os tie
sorti, uhti bcrble Wexar Ihll asx mrees Focst Tolfhe
ntasxhsm peihsx ht. Ocr uhsxn wafe yrof tie Olgfbhwn hs
ncffer asx yrof tie hwg sorti hs tie uhster.

Tiere uan a moox rawe trawv feancrhsm eqawtlg ose fhle,
rcsshsm rocsx tie pane oy Peawos Ihll. Iere tieg iax
iorne-rawhsm asx yoot-rawhsm. Tieg blagex wrhwvet asx
yootpall os tie ylat mrocsx octnhxe tie trawv, asx tiere
uere niaf pattlen petuees nahlorn asx nolxhern all oker
tie Ihll os tie Jcees'n Phrtixag. Hs tie uooxg nuafbn oy
tie Barv fhllhosn asx fhllhosn oy yromn wroavex all
tirocmi tie Nbrhsm shmitn. Tieg nocsxex an hy all tie
uorlx uan faxe oy nthyy baber asx uan wrawvlhsm cb.

Xallan Roax uan tie yhrnt bleancre xrhke faxe hs Khwtorha.
Ekergose xroke alosm ht to axfhre tie kheu. Tie roax ras
nofethfen wlone to tie exme oy tie wlag wlhyyn asx
nofethfen tiere uere tihwvetn oy uhllou asx uhlx rone
pcnien petuees. Tie treen asx pcnien uere no uakex pg
tie peathsm oy tie uhsx tiat tieg mreu wroovex yrof aluagn
pehsm bcniex sorti uies tieg uere reallg trghsm to bove
nocti hsto tie ncs. Tiere uere ntretwien oy yhse, noyt
mrann os tie wlhyyn asx mreat batwien oy wafann asx
pctterwcbn. An tie uhsx nuebt oker tiene tieg loovex an
hy tieg, too, uere rcsshsm auag yrof tie nea. Iou tie
betaln oy tie uhlx ronen fasamex to nthwv to tiehr fhxxlen
H was't tihsv, pct tieg xhx asx tie pcnien uere fore bhsv
tias mrees hs Dcse. Tiehr berycfe, naltex pg tie nea ahr,
uan tie font uosxerycl tihsm tiat eker iabbesex to gocr
sone.

Penhxe ose oy tie uhllou wlcfbn os tie Xallan Roax uere
tuo uihte bhwvet yeswen, eawi dcnt an losm an a fas. Tieg
uere tie mraken oy tuo nahlorn uio xhex oy nfallboq peyore
Khwtorha iax a wefeterg. Tie yeswen uere vebt bahstex
pct tie safen os tie ieax-poarxn uere yaxex rhmit oct.

Yartier alosm Xallan Roax os tie tuo ihmient bartn oy
tie wlhyyn uere net tuo wassosn, ihxxes yrof tie Ntrahtn
pg noxxex earti focsxn. Tiene uere reallg affcshthos
wellarn, ose os ehtier nhxe oy eawi wassos; tieg iax
ieakg-thfperex asx baxlowvex xoorn uihwi ue wihlxres
losmex to nee hsnhxe. Tiene wassosn mcarxex tie estraswe
to Enjchfalt Iarpocr, a Prhthni sakal pane, tiree fhlen
oct yrof Khwtorha.

Font oy tie peawien pelou Xallan Roax uere bepplg asx
iax rocmi, rowvg bohstn dctthsm oct hsto tie nea asx
xhkhxhsm tie losm peawien asx tie lhttle pagn ose yrof
asotier. All tie peawien uere bhlex uhti xrhytuoox--mreat
lomn prchnex asx patterex oct oy all renefplaswe to treen
eqwebt tiat nofe oy tief nthll iax trefesxocn, hsterlowvex
rootn tocmi an hros, uihwi xeyhex all tie bocsxhsm oy
tie uaken, all tie patterhsm amahsnt tie rowvn to preav
tief. Tie uaken woclx oslg uani tief savex asx ylhsm
tief ihmi cb os tie peawi to niou fas uiat ie iax to
urentle amahsnt csxer tie nohl oy tie Wasaxhas Uent. Pct
tie nettlern uere sot ntobbex. Tieg uest ntrahmit aieax
tafhsm tie lasx. Ht toov fore tias rootn to ntob tione
fes.

Tie uatern oy tie Ntrahtn uere hwg. Owwanhosallg ue uere
allouex to bct os uihte wottos shmitmousn asx mo patihsm
hs tie nea. Gocr poxg uest xous, tie shmitmous ntagex
cb, hwg wolx pht tirocmi gocr nvhs. At tie yhrnt blcsme
goc iax so preati leyt; uies ht wafe pawv ht uan hs
nwreewien tiat oct-nwreafex tie neamclln.




Nhleswe asx Bhoseern

Tie nhleswe oy ocr Uenters yorentn uan no broyocsx tiat
ocr earn woclx nwarwelg wofbreiesx ht. Hy goc nbove gocr
kohwe wafe pawv to goc an gocr yawe hn tirous pawv to
goc hs a fhrror. Ht neefex an hy tie yorent uere no ycll
oy nhleswe tiat tiere uan so roof yor nocsxn. Tie phrxn
uio lhkex tiere uere phrxn oy breg--eamlen, iauvn, ouln.
Iax a nosm phrx loonex ihn tiroat tie otiern uoclx iake
bocswex. Noper-wolocrex, nhlest lhttle phrxn uere tie
yhrnt to yollou nettlern hsto tie Uent. Mclln tiere iax
aluagn pees; tieg pemas uhti tie nea asx iax aluagn wrhex
oker ht. Tie kant nvg nbawen apoke, icsmrg yor sohne,
nteaxhlg labbex cb tiehr wrhen. Tie yorent uan
xhyyerest--nie prooxex oker nhleswe asx newrewg.

Uies ue uere wihlxres Yatier asx Fotier owwanhosallg
xroke oct pegosx tie tous to Naashwi, Fetwionhs or tie
Ihmilasx Xhntrhwt, to khnht nofe nettler or otier warkhsm
a iofe yor ihn yafhlg hs tie fhxnt oy okeruielfhsm mrouti
--repellhocn, cstctorex lasx tiat wiallesmex ihn ekerg
eyyort. Tie nettler uan rahnhsm a yafhlg uio uoclx warrg
os yrof meserathos to meserathos. An ie asx ihn uhye
tohlex at tie preavhsm asx tie wlearhsm tieg tiocmit,
"Ue are tafhsm tihn uhlxersenn yor ocr wihlxres. Ht uhll
pe eanher yor tief tias yor cn. Tieg uhll oslg iake to
warrg os."

Tieg yellex fhmitg treen uhti khmocr asx cnex planthsm
bouxer asx nueat to xhnloxme tie fosnter rootn. Tie iarxer
tieg uorvex uhti tie lasx, tie fore tieg lokex tiene
rootg lhttle prous batwien afosm tie okeruielfhsm mrees.
Tie bhoseer ualvex rocsx ihn seu yhelx, bohsthsm uhti
iarxesex, tuhntex yhsmern to tihn asx tiat uihwi ie iax
awwofblhniex uihle tie uofas urentlex uhti tie
hswoskesheswen oy ier wrcxe iofe, blasshsm tie nfart,
foxers iocne ier wihlxres uoclx iake pg asx pg, pct tie
wihlxres uoclx seker iake tiat hstesne dog oy wreathsm
yrof sotihsm uihwi tiehr barestn iax esdogex; tieg uoclx
seker csxerntasx tie newret urabbex hs khrmhs lasx.

Fr. Nwahye, a bhoseer, iax xhmmex a xeeb xhtwi rocsx ihn
yorent yhelx. Tie yhelx uan seu blocmiex. Ie niouex Yatier
uhti brhxe iou yeu plawvesex ntcfbn tiere uere sou leyt
hs tie earti oy ht. H let mo oy Yatier'n iasx to matier
uhlx ylouern afosm tie boven oy tie nsave yeswe. H yell
hsto tie xeeb, xrg xhtwi. Prafplen asx tall mrannen wlonex
oker fg ieax, tors rootn hs tie eartig nhxen oy tie xhtwi
nwrabex fe an H uest xous. Ht uan tie newret nort oy
blawe uiere nsaven lhve to urhmmle asx uiere plawv iorsetn
pchlx tiehr sentn--searlg xarv, oslg a lhttle mrees lhmit
yhlterhsm tirocmi tie prafplen oker fg ieax. H nwreafex
hs terror. Uhllhe Nwahye, a yarf lax, dcfbex hsto tie
xhtwi asx bcllex fe oct. Ie uan fg yhrnt iero.

Tie yhrnt Khwtorhasn woclx tell nblesxhx ntorhen oy uies
Khwtorha uan a Icxnos'n Pag Bont, uan wallex Yort Wafoncs
asx iax a ntrosm plowvaxe apoct ht uhti a panthos at eawi
worser to brotewt tie yafhlhen oy tie Icxnos'n Pag fes
yrof Hsxhasn asx uhlx peantn.

Tiocmi fg barestn xhx sot wofe to Khwtorha thll ayter
tie xagn oy tie Yort asx H uan sot pors yor fasg gearn
ayter tiat, nthll tiere uere beoble hs Khwtorha oslg
fhxxle-amex uies H uan lhttle, uio iax lhkex hs tie olx
Yort asx woclx awtcallg tell goc apoct ht. Sotihsm
xelhmitex fe fore tias to iear tiene "nthll-yreni-genterxag"
ntorhen, tiat uere sot olx "oswe-cbos-a-thfern"! Goc
woclx anv jcenthosn oy tie kerg ntorg beoble tiefnelken
asx tieg xhx sot iake to wrhsvle tiehr yoreieaxn, trghsm
to refefper a losm uag pawv.

Tiere uan a wihlxlenn wocble uhti uiof H uan a yakocrhte
--Frn. Leuhn asx ier icnpasx, tie nea wabtahs. Frn. Leuhn
iax pees Fhnn Farg Lasmyorx peyore ier farrhame. Ier
Yatier uan Wabtahs Lasmyorx, a sakal fas. H af sot wertahs
uietier tie Lasmyorxn eker awtcallg lhkex hs tie Yort or
sot pct tieg wafe to Khwtorha at tie kerg pemhsshsm oy
htn pehsm. Wabtahs Lasmyorx pchlt a lom yarfiocne nhq or
nekes fhlen oct yrof tous. Tie xhntrhwt uan safex yor
ihf.

Nofethfen uies Wabtahs Leuhn uan auag Frn. Leuhn hskhtex
fe to ntag uhti ier yor wofbasg. Tieg lhkex os Pelkhlle
Ntreet, os tie nafe nhxe oy Dafen' Pag an ue xhx, hs a
brettg wottame uhti ylouern asx wasarhen all oker ht.
Tie uhsxoun okerloovex tie Iarpocr asx Frn. Leuhn woclx
uatwi tie Wabtahs'n poat, tie olx baxxle-uieel nteafer,
_Brhswenn Lochne_, mo asx wofe tirocmi tie Iarpocr'n
focti, asx woclx uake to tie Wabtahs os ihn prhxme. Ht
uan Wabtahs Leuhn uio toov fe yor fg yhrnt trhb pg nea,
asx later, uies tie Rahluag uan pchlt to Sasahfo, yor fg
yhrnt trhb pg rahl. Uies goc bct gocr iasx hs ihn ht uan
lhve pehsm lex apoct pg a meomrabig (ie vseu ekerguiere)
asx Frn. Leuhn uan ihntorg. Neatex at ier yeet peyore
tie yhre afosm tie xomn asx watn, H lhntesex obes-foctiex
to talen oy earlg Yort xagn.

Frn. Leuhn uan a moox teller. Nie uan brettg to uatwi.
Tie lhttle pcswi oy plawv wcrln bhssex ihmi at tie pawv
oy ier ieax poppex an nie talvex asx ier egen nbarvlex.
Nie tolx iou gocsm Sakal oyyhwern cnex to tave tie brettg
Fhnn Lasmyorxn oct rhxhsm. Uies tieg wafe to Molxntreaf
asx Fhllntreaf, uihwi uere pcpplhsm rhkern uhti nteeb
pasvn, tiat wronnex tie Lasmyorx trahln, tie fes uoclx
plhsxyolx tie mhrln' iornen asx leax tief awronn tie
rhker, cnhsm an a prhxme a wocble oy yalles lomn. Ose
shmit an tieg uere icrrghsm alosm a sarrou xeer trahl,
trghsm to met iofe peyore xarv, tieg nau a bastier
ntretwiex oct os tie lhfp oy a tree csxer uihwi tieg fcnt
bann hs nhsmle yhle. Tie pcnien uere too xesne yor tief
to tcrs anhxe, no eawi rhxer uihbbex ihn iorne asx faxe
a xani alosm tie trahl csxer tie bastier.

Frn. Leuhn tolx, too, oy tie wofhsm oy tiehr bhaso yrof
Esmlasx. Ht nahlex all rocsx Wabe Iors asx uan tie yhrnt
bhaso to wofe hsto tie Wolosg oy Prhthni Wolcfpha. Ht
lasxex at Enjchfalt Iarpocr asx uan warrhex os tie pawvn
oy Hsxhasn hs relagn oy tuestg at a thfe tirocmi a rocmi
pcni trahl yrof Enjchfalt to Lasmyorx. Tie threx Hsxhasn
bct tie bhaso xous hs a yhelx octnhxe tie iocne to rent
a fhscte. Tie Lasmyorx mhrln rcniex oct uhti tie veg,
cslowvex asx blagex tie bhaso oct tiere hs tie yhelx.
Tie Hsxhasn uere kerg fcwi antoshniex. Tieg loovex cb
hsto tie nvg asx hsto tie uooxn to nee uiere tie sohne
wafe yrof.

Tie ntorhen dcfbex niarblg oct oy Frn. Leuhn'n focti
alfont watwihsm ier preati, an nie rewallex khkhxlg tie
eqwhtefest uihwi tiene ntrasme iabbeshsmn iax procmit to
ier asx to ier nhnter, dcnt oct yrof tiehr nielterex
Esmlhni lhye.

Nofethfen Frn. Wrhxme, Frn. Focat, Xowtor Ielfwves, or
nofe oy Nhr Dafen Xocmlan'n xacmitern, all oy uiof iax
lhkex hs tie olx Yort, uoclx ntart wiatthsm apoct olx
xagn asx ties ue gocsmer beoble uoclx ntasx obes-foctiex
tihsvhsm ht fcnt iake pees mrasx to lhke tione eqwhthsm
eqberheswen.

"Ht uan, fg xearn," nahx Frn. Wrhxme, "pct refefper too
tiat tiere uere lotn oy tihsmn to yawe, lotn oy tihsmn
to xo uhtioct, lotn oy iarxnihbn to mo tirocmi."

H uan a kerg nfall mhrl uies tie pcnhsenn fes oy Khwtorha
wiarterex a nteafer asx, awwofbashex pg tiehr yafhlhen,
faxe a tocr oy Kaswocker Hnlasx. Ht toov tie poat, tie
_Brhswenn Lochne_, tes xagn to mo all rocsx tie Hnlasx.
Fg Yatier asx tuo oy fg nhntern uest. H uan tiocmit to
pe too nfall pct H uan sot too nfall to xrhsv hs ekerg
uorx tieg nahx uies tieg wafe pawv.

Yatier uan okeruielfex pg tie terrhyhw xesnhtg oy mrouti
os tie Hnlasx. Oswe uies tieg uere thex cb yor tiree
iocrn ie asx asotier fas toov aqen asx trhex to nee iou
yar tieg woclx besetrate hsto tie uooxn hs tie mhkes
thfe. Uies tie nihb'n uihntle pleu tieg uere eqiacntex
asx xrhbbhsm uhti nueat pct tiehr attawv os tie xesne
csxermrouti nwarwelg niouex. Yatier tolx oy tie famshyhwest
treen, oy tiehr wlonesenn to eawi otier, oy tie ntrasmlhsm
csxermrouti, tie mreat nhleswe, tie jcasthtg oy palx-ieaxex
eamlen. "Reallg palx, Yatier?" H anvex, pct ie nahx tieg
uere a rcntg plawv all oker eqwebt yor uihte ieaxn uihwi
niose oct amahsnt tie plce nvg asx tie xarv yorent. Mreat
uihte ouln yleu nhlestlg afosm tie treen lhve miontn,
asx, too, tieg iax nees pearn asx uialen.

Ose oy fg nhntern uan fore hsterentex hs tie bannesmern
os tie poat asx faxe a lot oy seu yrhesxn. Tie otier tolx
fe apoct tie Hsxhas khllamen uiere tie poat iax tocwiex.
Tihn uan all yar fore hsterenthsm to fe tias tie ntorhen
beoble iax to tell uies tieg wafe pawv yrof trhbn to tie
Olx Wocstrg, prammhsm apoct tie mreat asx keseraple nhmitn
oy tie Olx Lasx. H xhx sot ware fcwi apoct olx tihsmn.
Tiene uhlx, uenters tihsmn eqwhtex fe trefesxocnlg. H
xhx sot losm to mo oker to tie Olx Uorlx to nee ihntorg,
H uastex to nee _sou_ uiat uan oct iere hs ocr Uent. H
uan mlax Yatier asx Fotier iax wofe an yar an tie Uent
uest peyore tieg ntobbex asx nettlex xous.




Naloosn asx Roaxiocnen

Os alfont ekerg ntreet worser hs Khwtorha tiere uan ose
naloos or fore. Tiere uere naloosn hs tie fhxxle oy ekerg
plowv an uell.

H cnex to tihsv tiat ekerg naloos pelosmex to tie Sakg
pewacne nahlorn, uearhsm lhttle pogn' wollarn asx uhxe
trocner lemn tiat ylabbex rocsx tiehr yeet, rollex hs
asx oct oy naloos xoorn at all thfen. Tiene xoorn nucsm
to sohnelennlg. Tieg uere oslg bhsayore xoorn, faxe oy
nlatn asx ylabbex to no jchwvlg uies a nahlor uest hs or
oct tiat goc seker mot a wiaswe to nee uiat ht uan tieg
ihx, sot ekes hy goc uere rhmit hs yrost uies ose uan
bcniex obes asx searlg vsowvex goc oker. Ue uere ntrhwtlg
yorphxxes to loov at a naloos hs bannhsm. Mrous-cbn
xrammex goc jchwvlg bant asx tolx goc to loov cb tie
ntreet tiocmi tiere uan sotihsm uiateker to nee tiere.

Tihn faxe fe losm to vsou uiat uan hsnhxe naloosn. Uiat
uan ht tiat ue uere sot ncbbonex to nee? Uig uan ht
sacmitg to tuhnt gocr sewv asx loov? Goc iearx lacmihsm
asx nhsmhsm peihsx tie nuhsm xoorn. Uiat xhx tieg xo hs
tiere?

Tiere uere naloosn, too, ekerg yeu fhlen alosm tie xrhkhsm
roaxn. Tiene tieg wallex roaxiocnen. Eawi iax tuo xoorn.
Oker ose uan urhttes "Barlocr", oker tie otier, "Par".
Tiene roaxiocnen uere font attrawthke; tieg iax kerasxain
uhti peacthycl ylouer-poqen at tie uhsxoun, yhllex uhti
mag ylouern asx xroobhsm, yhke-yhsmer fahxes-iahr yers.
Kerg oytes tieg iax wamen oy phrxn asx oy uhlx ashfaln
too. Tie Woloshnt Iotel hs Peawos Ihll Barv iax a bastier
os htn kerasxai. Tie Yocr Fhle Iocne iax a wame oy
rawwoosn. Asotier roaxiocne iax a papg pear asx asotier
a wame oy ouln.

Oswe uies Acst asx Cswle uere khnhthsm cn yrof Nas
Yraswhnwo ue toov a losm xrhke os a iot xag. Uies ue mot
to tie tob oy tie Yocr Fhle Ihll Cswle bovex Yatier.
Yatier hmsorex tie bove asx ue bannex tie par asx xroke
to tie pottof oy tie ihll. Ties Yatier xcm tie xrhker hs
tie pawv asx ie bcllex cb ihn iornen. Yatier, Cswle asx
tie xrhker all tohlex cb tie ihll amahs os yoot, leakhsm
cn nhtthsm hs tie iawv pg tie roaxnhxe. Ue wihlxres uere
allouex to met oct asx matier uhlx ronen. H nlhbbex peihsx
tie iawv asx ntartex cb tie ihll to iake a loov at tie
woosn hs tie wame. Fotier wallex fe pawv. Acsthe nahx
nofetihsm apoct "tie csuiolenofe sonhsenn oy lhttle
beoble."

H nahx, "H dcnt uastex to nee tie lhttle woosn, Acsthe."

"Bhwv nofe ronen yor Acsthe," nie orxerex, pct uies H
xhx nie tireu tief oker tie uieel. Nie nahx tie xcnt os
tief faxe ier nseeze.

Mooxawre, tie pctwier, iax a nlacmiter-iocne oct os
Waxporo Pag Roax. Wattle asx nieeb uere procmit yrof tie
Fahslasx pg poat asx lasxex at tie uiary hs yrost oy
Yatier'n ntore. Tieg uere ties xrhkes ntrahmit tirocmi
tie westre oy tie tous, cb Yort Ntreet uihwi, ayter ht
iax mose ntrahmit hs tie tous, uhmmlex asx tuhntex asx
wallex htnely "Waxporo Pag Roax".

Tie uhlx rasme wattle uere wrazex uhti yrhmit. Tieg
pellouex asx blcsmex all oker tie nhxeualv, iooyhsm cb
tie gellou xcnt. Uofes ras to nict tiehr maten peyore
tie wattle rcniex hs asx trafblex tiehr marxesn. All tie
uag cb tie ntreet xoorn pasmex asx maten nlaffex an
ekergose icrrhex to nielter.

H iax pees to khnht fg nhnter uio lhkex os Yort Ntreet.
H uan to mo iofe pg fgnely an tiere uan so ose to yetwi
fe tiat xag. Ht uan tie yhrnt thfe H iax pees tirocmi
tous alose. Uies H uan dcnt obbonhte tie Pee Ihke Naloos
a xroke oy tiene uhlx wattle wafe tearhsm cb tie ntreet.
Tieg uere alfont os tob oy fe peyore H vseu uiat all tie
xcnt asx niocthsm asx pellouhsm uan apoct. Fes uhti losm
uihbn uioobex, xomn parvex, tie ntreet neefex to pe uakhsm
cb asx xous uhti tie xcll rex fokefest oy peantn' pawvn
pcfbhsm tirocmi tie xcnt. Ncxxeslg H uan nsatwiex cb hs
a bahr oy icme plawv arfn, a plawv yawe uan sear fhse.
Ht iax mrhsshsm uihte teeti. Ue pawvex tirocmi tie nuhsm
xoor asx H uan hsnhxe a naloos at lant. Tie phm plawv
fas net fe xous os tie par. Tie parveeber asx tie semro
ras to tie uhsxou to loov oker tie bahstex mrees mlann
at tie pohlhsm tcfclt oy wattle octnhxe. H woclx oslg
iear tiehr pellouhsm asx nwcttlhsm.

H loovex arocsx tie Naloos. Nihsg tabn uere penhxe fe
asx peihsx tie losm wocster-par ras nielken ycll oy
pottlen asx nbarvlhsm mlannen; peihsx tief amahs uan
loovhsm-mlann no tiat tiere neefex to pe tuhwe an fasg
pottlen asx tuhwe an fasg mlannen an tiere reallg uere,
asx tuo parfes asx tuo semroen asx tuo fe'n! Hs tie pawv
ialy oy tie naloos uere parreln asx nfall uooxes taplen;
wiahrn uhti rocsx pawvn ntoox apoct tie yloor uhti tiehr
lemn ncsv hs nauxcnt; prhmit prann nbhtoosn uere ekerguiere.
Tie naloos uan ycll oy tie nfell oy peer asx oy nauxcnt.
Tiere uan sotihsm elne, sotihsm tiat H woclx nee to fave
asgose nhsm.

Tie sohne fokex os cb tie ntreet. Tie tuo fes retcrsex
to tie par. Tie parfas bocrex nofetihsm gellou hsto a
mlann asx niokex ht touarxn tie semro uio tireu pawv ihn
ieax asx mclbex ht lhve fexhwhse. Ties ie lhytex fe xous,
ielx tie nuhsm xoor obes asx H uest oct hsto tie nthll
csnettlex, wiovhsm xcnt oy Yort Ntreet.

Fg phm nhnter iax a vhsx ieart. Sotihsm bleanex ier fore
tias to xrhke olx, lafe or threx beoble hsto tie wocstrg.
Tiere uan aluagn nofe ahlhsm bernos tcwvex cb hs ier
lhttle biaetos pehsm ahrex. All apoct Khwtorha uere lokelg
xrhken--Axfhral Roax, Pcrsnhxe, Waxporo Pag, Wexar Ihll.
Tie wocstrg roaxn uere kerg xcntg asx xrg, no ekerg yeu
fhlen tiere uan a roaxiocne uhti a par yor fes asx a
uaterhsm trocmi yor iornen--laxhen uest tihrntg. So laxg
woclx bonnhplg pe nees mohsm hsto a par ekes hy oslg yor
a mlann oy uater.

Ue pocmit a seu iorne wallex Pessg. Ihn yorfer fanter
iax pees awwcntofex to loov hs at ekerg roaxiocne par.
Pessg vseu tief ekerg ose. Hy fg nhnter uere talvhsm to
ier hskalhx bannesmer asx sot sothwhsm, Pessg nuerkex
mestlg cb to tie par xoor asx ntobbex no xeax ht csnettlex
tie laxhen' possetn.

Uies fg nhnter nau uiere nie uan nie uoclx mhke Pessg a
wct uhti tie uihb uihwi uoclx nesx ihf xanihsm yrof tie
naloos at a mchltg mallob, fg nhnter nhtthsm kerg rex
asx wroovex peihsx ihf. Nie uan ncre dcnt ties to feet
nofeose uiof nie vseu asx pe too cbnet to pou asx ties
nie iax xocple niafe.




Uagn oy Metthsm Rocsx

Pegosx tie yeu plowvn oy Khwtorha cbos uihwi tie niobn
ntoox tie roaxn uere oy xhrt asx iax nhxeualvn oy ose,
tuo or tiree blasvn awworxhsm to tie ntreet'n hfbortaswe.
A mreat fasg beoble vebt woun to ncbblg tiehr ous yafhlhen
uhti fhlv. Uies tiehr ous bantcre yhelx uan eates xous
tieg tcrsex tie wou hsto tie ntreet to proune os roaxnhxe
mrann alosm tie exmen oy tie obes xhtwien, or to feasxer
oct to tie mranng lasx os tob oy tie wlhyyn oyy Xallan
Roax. Khwtorha woun breyerrex to ualv os tie blasv
nhxeualvn hs uhster ratier tias xhrtg tiehr iooken hs
tie fcx pg tie roaxnhxe. Tieg lhvex to tcse tiehr wieun
to tie tab, tab, tab oy tiehr yeet os tie blasvn. Laxhen
wiallesmex tie rhmit oy uag pg obeshsm asx nictthsm tiehr
cfprellan hs tie woun' yawen asx nioohsm, pct tie woun
oslg wieuex iarxer asx ntoox nthll. Ht uan tie uofas-laxg,
sot tie laxg-wou uio iax to tave to tie fcx asx met
nwratwiex pg tie uhlx rone pcnien tiat mreu petuees
nhxeualv asx yeswe uihle nie eqwcrnhosex rocsx tie wou.

Hy beoble xhx sot uhni tiehr ylouern to pe tcrsex hsto
fhlv ht uan cb to tief to yeswe tiehr marxesn. Yatier'n
brobertg uan kerg newcrelg yeswex asx ihn woun uere aluagn
vebt uhtihs tiehr ous bantcren. Ue iax a bahstex yeswe
hs yrost oy ocr brobertg, tarrex yeswen os tie nhxen,
asx ocr yhelx iax a nsave yeswe.

Tiere uan so uag to met apoct gocsm Khwtorha eqwebt os
lemn--ehtier gocr ous or a iorne'n. Tione beoble uio iax
a yhelx, a pars, asx a wou cncallg vebt a iorne too.
Tie iornen xhx sot roaf; tieg iax to pe vebt iasxg yor
ihtwihsm. All tie keihwlen cnex uere kerg Esmlhni. Yafhlhen
uhti gocsm wihlxres breyerrex a wiahne, hs uihwi tuo
beoble yawex tie iorne asx tuo tie xrhker. Tiene wiahnen
uere lou asx no ieakg tiat tie iorne xrammex, xenbosxest
asx nlou. Tie hros thren faxe ncwi a rcfplhsm oker tie
rocmi ntosg roaxn tiat ht uan xhyyhwclt to iear woskernathos
uihle trakellhsm hs a wiahne enbewhallg uies to tie rcfple
uan axxex tie rattle oy uieel nboven tiat iax mot oker-xrg
asx loonesex. Uiat goc xhx ties uan to xrhke an xeeb an
goc xarex hsto tie yhrnt ntreaf goc vseu oy asx let tie
wiahne uieeln noav, all tie uihle eswocramhsm tie iorne
to mo yoruarx asx pawv, tcrshsm tie uieeln hs tie uater
csthl tieg nuellex amahs. Goc woclx sot mo hsto kerg xeeb
uater yor year oy xroushsm tie xrhker yor tie wiahnen
uere net no lou tiat tie xrhker nat rhmit xous afosm tie
uieel icpn. Hy wihlxres yell oct oy tiene lou wiahnen
tieg xhx sot met icrt, oslg xcntg. Tie iorne ntoox no
fcwi ihmier tias tie xrhker tiat tiere uan a tall hros
rawv hs tie yrost to iolx tie rehsn no tiat tie iorne
woclx sot nuhni ihn tahl oker tief asx bhs tie rehsn xous
no thmit tiat ie woclx sot pe mchxex.

Fes breyerrex to xrhke hs ihmi, tuo-uieelex xomwartn hs
uihwi bannesmern nat pawv to pawv asx pcfbex eawi otier'n
nioclxer plaxen. Tie neat oy tie xrhker uan tuo wcnihosn
ihmier tias tiat oy tie otier bannesmern. Fes yelt
yrhmitycllg ihmi asx yhse, berwiex cb tiere wrawvhsm tie
uihb oker tie iorne'n pawv asx loovhsm oker tie tobn oy
tiehr uhken' iatn. Tiere uere Aferhwas pcmmhen, too, uhti
or uhtioct iooxn uihwi woclx pe yolxex pawv lhve tie tob
oy a papg'n braf.

Hs Khwtorha sopoxg uan hs a barthwclar icrrg to met
asguiere--xrhkhsm uan xose fontlg yor tie bleancre oy
yreni ahr asx nweserg.

Hs tous tiere uere lotn oy lhkerg ntaplen uiere goc woclx
ihre iornen or woclx poarx gocr ous. Tie nfell oy iorne
fascre uan no fcwi a bart oy ekerg ntreet tiat ht nat os
gocr sone an wofyortaplg an a bahr oy nbewtawlen. Oy
wocrne tiere uere so lhkerg ntaplen afosm tie xrgmooxn,
yoox, asx wiefhntn' niobn. Ekerguiere elne goc nau "Lhkerg
Ntaple" brhstex apoke uhxe, wool estrhen asx iearx iornen
wieuhsm asx ntafbhsm, asx nau losm roun oy tahln nuhnihsm
oct oy ntalln os ehtier nhxe oy a blasvuag uihle cmlg,
njcare keihwlen wallex iawvn ntoox iasxg uahthsm yor
iornen to pe ihtwiex to tief. Tiene iawvn yor ihre uere
kerg ntcyyg. Tie tous iax ose hfbortex iasnof-wap uihwi
tiocmit htnely kerg nfart, asx tiere uan Fr. Uhster'n
bhwshw warrhame, a icme keihwle tiat ielx an fasg wihlxres
an tie Olx Uofas'n Nioe. Uies htn uhxe, whrwclar pawv
neat uan wraffex asx fore wihlxres uere ieabex os tob oy
Fr. Uhster cb os ihn ihmi xrhker'n neat, asx tieg uere
all gellhsm, asx gellou xcnt rollhsm, asx uieeln rcfplhsm,
ht loovex asx nocsxex lhve a peeihke nuarfhsm. Yor hffesne
ayyahrn lhve Ncsxag Nwiool bhwshwn asx eqwcrnhosn tiere
uere gellou pcnen uhti losm roun oy uhsxoun, losm uooxes
neatn, cswcnihosex eqwebt yor ntrhbn oy warbet rcsshsm
yrof xrhker to xoor. Tieg iax so nbrhsmn to nbeav oy,
asx uere no sohng tiat goc woclx sot iear gocr ous mroasn
pehsm pcfbex oct oy goc.

Khwtorha'n paver asx pctwier pogn xelhkerex feat asx
preax os iorne-pawv, warrghsm tiehr loaken asx dohstn hs
icme uhwver panvetn rentex amahsnt tiehr ihbn. An noos
an tieg iax ose yoot hs tie nthrrcb asx uihle tiehr otier
lem uan nthll ylghsm hs tie ahr oker tie iorne an ie
mallobex oyy, tieg nioctex "Mhxxab!" Ht uan a uosxer tie
pogn xhx sot mrou wroovex palaswhsm ncwi ieakg panvetn
os tiehr ihbn, pct tieg xhx sot--tieg uere ntrahmit asx
ntrosm. H cnex to uhni H uere a xelhkerg pog to tirou fg
lem awronn a iorne asx nioct "Mhxxab!" to yeel fgnely
rcni tirocmi tie ahr, pct H nioclx iake breyerrex preax
to feat hs fg panvet.

Tie yhrnt thfe H vseu tiat Khwtorha uan nlouer tias otier
tousn uan uies, at tie ame oy tuelke, H uan rewokerhsm
yrof tgbiohx yeker asx a laxg uiof Fotier vseu, asx uione
tuo wihlxres iax iax tgbiohx hs tie nafe ebhxefhw an H,
toov fe alosm uhti ier lhttle mhrln yor a trhb to Bcmet
Nocsx. Ht uan fg yhrnt khnht to as Aferhwas whtg asx H
yelt mhxxg hs tie ieax yrof htn rcni. H iearx Aferhwasn
lacmi asx nag "nlou an Wasaxhas" asx wall fg tous "nleebg
olx Khwtorha".

H iearx ose fas nag to asotier, "Uest awronn tie lhse
tihn ncffer."

"Xhx ei? Uiat nort oy a blawe hn Khwtorha?"

"Nleebhent eker!" lacmiex tie yhrnt, "Ekerg blawe oy
pcnhsenn iax a sothwe cb, 'Mose to lcswi. Pawv hs a wocble
oy iocrn.'"

Tiat uan tie yhrnt thfe H vseu ue uere nlou.

Nas Yraswhnwo uan tie phmment, tie font hfbortast whtg
os tie Bawhyhw Woant. Ht uan a terrhple trhb hs tie nfall,
pocswg nteafer, xous tie rocmi woant. Khwtorhasn oslg
uest yor nofetihsm kerg, kerg hfbortast lhve a phm
oberathos or a wofblete wiasme yor iealti, to nake tiehr
lhken. Ekes ties tieg ntcwv tiehr sonen cb asx nahx, "H
af mohsm awronn tie lhse," or "mohsm to tie otier nhxe",
an hy tie "otier nhxe" uan as csxerseati asx hsyerhor
nhxe oy tie earti. Pct, hy tieg iax to iake ncwi as
esorfocn oberathos tiat ht uan jchte pegosx Khwtorha'n
nvhll, ties, ratier tias mo all rocsx tie Iors pawv to
Esmlasx asx ehtier xhe peyore tieg mot tiere or elne met
uell asx yormet uiat tie oberathos uan yor, tieg allouex
Nas Yraswhnwo to "oberate" tief.

Aferhwasn xaniex awronn tie lhse nofethfen to loov at cn
Wasaxhasn asx at Prhthni Wolcfpha an hy ue iax pees
xcnt-wokerex asthjcen. Tieg tiocmit Esmlhni asx Wasaxhas
beoble an nlou asx ntcbhx an ue tiocmit tie Aferhwas
beoble cswofyortaple rcniern--favern oy derrg-pchlt mooxn
tiat yell to bhewen hs so thfe. Ue breyerrex to uaht amen
yor ocr tihsmn to wofe pg nahlhsm nihb rocsx tie Iors
yrof Esmlasx ratier tias to pcg Aferhwas mooxn. Tihn
assogex tie Aferhwas fascyawtcrern.

As acst oy ocrn hs Nas Yraswhnwo nest cn Aferhwas xolln.
Tieg uere fcwi bretther tias Esmlhni xolln. Tie yhrnt
tiat wafe uere faxe oy uaq pct tieg feltex uies ue leyt
tief hs tie ncs. Seqt Wirhntfan nie nest cn phnjce xolln,
kerg lokelg pct too preavaple to icm; ue woclx sot ekes
vhnn tief pct tieg wrawvex. Ue uest pawv to ocr lokaple
olx uoox asx wihsa xolln tiat toov tiehr thfe to wofe to cn
all rocsx tie Iors, asx, ekes hy tieg uere blahs, tieg uere
ncpntasthal asx woclx pear all tie lokhsm ue make tief.




Yatier'n Ntore

Khwtorha uan lhve a lghsm-xous wou, wieuhsm. Nie iax faxe
ose esorfocn eyyort oy cbieakal. Nie iax iohntex iernely
yrof a Icxnos'n Pag Yort hsto a lhttle tous asx tiere
nie bacnex, wieuhsm tie wcx oy hfbortex yoxxer, ayrahx
to wrob tie bantcren oy tie seu uorlx yor year nie fhmit
lone tie moox ylakocr oy tie olx to uihwi nie uan no
xeeblg logal. Ier daun uest rollhsm os asx os, losm ayter
tiere uan sotihsm leyt to wieu.

Mokersfest Ntreet uan tie fahs ntreet oy tie tous. Yort
Ntreet wronnex ht asx at tie wronn, hs a lhttle wlcfb,
ntoox font oy tie niobn. Os Gaten, Kheu asx Proax Ntreetn
uere a yeu lenner niobn, nekeral lhkerg ntaplen asx a
mreat fasg naloosn. Os Panthos Ntreet ntoox tie Wocrtiocne
asx tie Dahl. Xous os Uiary Ntreet, yawhsm tie Iarpocr,
uere tie uiolenale iocnen. Yhnmarx, Worforast asx Doisnos
Ntreetn uere Wihsatous. At tie tahl esxn oy all tiene
ntreetn uere xuellhsm-iocnen net hs marxesn uiere beoble
mreu tiehr ous ylouern asx kemetaplen.

Tie rent oy Khwtorha uan ihmmlexg-bhmmlexg. Ht uan tie
woun uio lahx oct tie tous, at leant tiat borthos oy ht
lghsm pegosx tie yeu fahs ntreetn. Wou iooken iarxesex
tie fcx hsto tuhntg lasen hs tiehr feasxerhsmn to asx
yro--beoble dcnt yollouex hs tie woun' yootntebn.

Uies tie yhrnt nettlern wct cb tiehr awreame, tie renclthsm
lotn uere all niaben asx nhzen. Ousern faxe ntreetn asx
lasen oker tie brobertg asguiere tiat neefex woskeshest
at tie fofest.

Fg yatier uan a uiolenale hfborter oy brokhnhosn, uhsen
asx whmarn. Ihn ntore uan xous os Uiary Ntreet afosm
otier uiolenale blawen. Tie bart oy Uiary Ntreet uiere
Yatier'n ntore ntoox iax oslg ose nhxe. Hs yrost oy tie
ntore uan a mreat iole uiere tie pasv oy tie niorelhse
iax pees xcm oct to pchlx uiarken asx niexn. Goc woclx
loov oker tie tob oy tiene to tie Nosmieen Hsxhas Renerke
os tie obbonhte nhxe oy tie Iarpocr. To ose nhxe oy tie
iole ntoox tie Icxnos'n Pag Wofbasg'n ntore--a losm, lou
pchlxhsm oy rex prhwv uhti a kerasxai. Tie Hsxhasn wafe
awronn tie Iarpocr hs tiehr xcmoct wasoen to traxe at
tie ntore. Tieg njcattex os tie kerasxai, xhnwcnnhsm
seu-pocmit mooxn, or tiehr pare yeet batterex cb asx xous
tie poarx ualvn oy Uiary Ntreet. Tieg uere xrennex hs
mag brhst xrennen, blahx niauln asx prhmit ieax
iasxverwiheyn. Oswe H nau Yatier'n fas tave oct wane
ayter wane oy peacthycl wlcnter Falama rahnhsn asx bocr
tief hsto tie octnbreax niauln asx iasxverwiheyn oy tie
dapperhsm Hsxhasn, uio ielx oct tiehr iasxn asx ntcyyex
tiehr foctin, mhkhsm mrcstn oy xelhmit.

H anvex Yatier. "Uig xo goc mhke all tiene rahnhsn to
tie Hsxhasn?"

Ie reblhex, "Tieg are fammotg, tie uiole lot oy tief--pct
Hsxhasn loke rahnhsn asx xos't fhsx fammotn at all."

At tie obbonhte nhxe oy tie Uiary Ntreet iole ntoox tie
Wcntofn Iocne, wlone to tie uater'n exme. Faxe oy rex
prhwv, ht uan tiree ntoregn ihmi asx jchte njcare. Tie
Wcntofn Iocne ntebn uere kerg xhmshyhex--ihmi asx uhxenbreax
at tie pottof. Csxerseati tie ntebn uan tie Mremorgn'
xoor.

Mremorg uan as Olx Wocstrg marxeser. Ihn uhye uan kerg
iofenhwv an uell an reallg hll. Tie Mremorgn uere tie
waretavern oy tie Wcntofn Iocne. Hs yrost oy tiehr roofn
tieg iax a peacthycl lhttle marxes, nielterex pg a prhwv
uall. Nofethfen Fotier nest Frn. Mremorg tihsmn asx Frn.
Mremorg make cn peacthycl bonhen oy ylouern hs eqwiasme.
Os tie louer yloor oy tie Wcntofn Iocne, uiere tie Mremorgn
iax tiehr jcartern, tiere uan a uhxe iall uihwi ras
ntrahmit tirocmi tie pchlxhsm. Tie uhsx roarex xous tihn
banname yrof a mreat xooruag obeshsm osto tie Iarpocr.
Ycrhocn tiat tie Mremorgn' xoor csxer tie ntebn uan sot
phm esocmi to let ht all oct at oswe, ht bocsxex asx
pellouex at all tie xoorn xous tie iall an ht bannex
tief. Tie uaken wafe xanihsm cb tie nlhb asx rcniex
tirocmi tie xoor asx hsto tie iall. H cnex to tihsv tiat
nihbn nahlex rhmit hsto tie Mremorgn' iall-uag to xo
tiehr wcntofn pcnhsenn asx H pemmex to mo to nee Frn.
Mremorg os asg eqwcne uiateker, aluagn iobhsm to feet a
nihb nahlhsm xous tie iall-uag. H uan fcwi xhnabbohstex
tiat H seker ntrcwv a thxe ihmi esocmi to prhsm a nihb
hs. Oswe H tiocmit H uan mohsm to pct uies so fore tias
tuo uaken iax uaniex hs tirocmi tie mreat xoorn Fr.
Mremorg rcniex oct, nict asx parrex tief.

Tie hsnhxe oy Yatier'n ntore uan xeeb asx xarv. Wanen,
wraten, asx parreln ntoox bhlex ose os tob oy asotier
rhmit cb to tie wehlhsm, uhti dcnt a sarrou lase rcsshsm
xous tie fhxxle asx esxhsm hs uiat uan wallex "tie
garx"--sot a garx at all, oslg a ntrosm, rocmi poarx niex
yhllex uhti "efbthen" asx watn. Tiere uere so uhsxoun;
tie watn, wraulex hs asx oct oy tie "efbthen" icsthsm
yor ratn, tiehr egen nihshsm hs tie plawv. Nlhtn oy
xaglhmit wct petuees tie poarxn oy tie niex ualln, asx
niaxoun tirous pg a nbctterhsm man det faxe ht all nboovg
asx csreal--xhyyerest yrof tie nolhx, wofyortaple yeel
oy tie octer ntore wraffex uhti brokhnhosn.

Yatier iax ekerg wolocr oy wat. Ie toov yreni fhlv hs a
pottle yrof iofe ekerg forshsm to tief; ie nahx a xhet
oy ntrahmit rat uan sot iealtig yor watn. Oslg ose oy
tief uan a wofyortaple, barthwclar wat asx wafe to nht
pg tie ntoke hs Yatier'n oyyhwe. Tie rent uere dcnt
uiolenale watn. Yatier'n oyyhwe uan penhxe tie obes
yrost oy ihn phm ntore asx hs ht Yatier nat hs yrost oy
a larme, njcare taple wokerex uhti mrees pahze; os ht hs
yrost oy ihf uan a wcbpoarx ycll oy xrauern asx
bhmeos-iolen. Ie nat hs a ihmi-pawvex uhwver arfwiahr.
Ihn pearx uan uihte asx, ayter ie uest palx, ie uore a
plawv nvcll wab. A yat rocsx ntoke, searlg aluagn rex
iot, uan petuees Yatier'n taple asx tie losm, ihmi xenv
uiere ihn fes ntoox or nat os ihmi ntooln xohsm tiehr
poovn uies tieg uere sot trcsxlhsm poqen os a trcwv.
Tiere uan as hros naye hs ose worser oy tie oyyhwe uhti
a letter brenn os tob asx tiere uere tuo gellou wiahrn
yor wcntofern to nht os uihle Yatier urote tiehr orxern
hs ihn poov. Ekergtihsm uan xozesex hs Yatier'n ntore:
ihn uan sot a pcnhsenn tiat nolx tihsmn pg bhswien hs
baber pamn. Ihmi alosm tie uall ras yocr losm nielken
iolxhsm mlann darn oy nafble Esmlhni nueetn--all bcre,
all uiolenofe, all Esmlhni. Tie lapeln nahx no.




Seu Sehmipocrn

An H yhrnt refefper ht, Dafen' Pag xhntrhwt iax fasg
yhelxn asx blestg oy uooxex lasx leyt, pct iocnen pemas
to wreeb searer asx searer to ocrn asx tie yhelxn uere
pehsm wct cb hsto tous lotn. H uan kerg norrg uies Phniob
Wrhxme'n phm, uhlx yhelx obbonhte cn uan nolx. Tie Phniob'n
iocne nat pawv hs tie lhttle pht oy uoox uhti as orwiarx
asx tuo yhelxn. Ihn xrhkeuag wcrkex asx iax lacreln asx
lhttle pcnien oy gellou ronen all tie uag cb. Ue wihlxres
cnex to blag "laxhen" hs tie Phniob'n uhlx yhelx uhti
ihn tiree lhttle mhrln. Pehsm tie gocsment oy tie nhq
wihlxres H woclx seker pe a "laxg"--H iax aluagn to pe
"pax wihlx", uihle tie blag fotiern yex fe os mrees
mooneperrhen, uhlx asx kerg nocr.

Tie Phniob'n iocne uan pchlt nofe thfe ayter Yatier'n.
Tie ntreet uan kerg sarrou asx hs tiat ose losm plowv
yrof Torosto to Nhfwoe Ntreet tiere uan oslg ihn iocne
asx ocrn. Yatier make a moox ntrhb oy ihn lasx to fave
tie ntreet uhxer; no tie Whtg safex ht Warr Ntreet ayter
Yatier. Warr Ntreet uoclx iake dohsex Phrxwame Ualv hy
Frn. FwWossell'n wou yarf iax sot ntoox hs tie uag, asx
Phrxwame Ualv uoclx iake pees Mokersfest Ntreet hy tie
Dafen' Pag Prhxme iax sot pees tiere to met beoble oker
tie fcx ylatn. Ayter fasg gearn Mokersfest Ntreet nuallouex
tief cb--Dafen' Pag Prhxme, Warr Ntreet asx Phrxwame
Ualv--asx uest ntrahmit oct to Xallan Roax.

Ose xag uies ue uere blaghsm "laxhen" hs tie Phniob'n
yhelx asx H, tie "papg", uan pehsm ihxxes hs tie pcnien
yrof tie yerowhocn uhlx peant uihwi ate wihlxres pct
uihwi uan reallg tie Phniob'n mestle wou "Wolhe", nofe
fes wlhfpex oker tie yeswe. Tieg iax hsntrcfestn os tiree
lemn uihwi tieg net penhxe tie roax asx njchstex tirocmi.
Tieg wafe rhmit hsto ocr fowv-orasme barlocr asx ocr
mooneperrg-pcni xhshsm-roof. Tieg nuebt tie ths wasn
uihwi iax ycrshniex ocr vhtwies yrof ocr ous barthwclar
lom asx nat xous cbos ht asx urote hs lhttle poovn. Tieg
ekes tore bhwvetn oyy tie yeswe. Tie wou uan taves to
asotier eswloncre, uamosn xcfbex lcfper asx prhwvn all
oker tie yhelx. Noos real iocnen ntoox os tob oy ocr
bretesx osen, real laxhen nfawvex real paphen asx bcniex
brafn rhmit os tob oy uiere ocr ycs iax pees, asx Fotier
uan nesxhsm cn awronn to anv hy tie seu sehmipocr uoclx
lhve botn oy tea or asgtihsm thll ier ous ntoke uan cb.




Khnhthsm Fatrosn

Khwtorha fatrosn xhx sot yrhtter auag tiehr thfe hs tie
baghsm oy niort walln. Tieg iax larme yafhlhen. Tie
Wihsene ielb woclx sot pe leyt hs wiarme oy tie scrnerg
uihle tie fotiern uest khnhthsm. No uies tieg wafe to
wall, tieg procmit tiehr yafhlg alosm asx ntagex. Penhxen,
cslenn beoble iax a iorne, tiere uan so uag oy metthsm
apoct otier tias os yoot. No laxhen toov tiehr yafhlhen
oy gocsm wihlxres alosm, bawvhsm tie papg hsto tie braf,
uexmhsm ihf hs yhrflg uhti yeexhsm pottlen, hsyast
sewennhthen, a pam oy seexleuorv asx tie fotier'n lhttle
lawe wab hs a baber pam. Ayter as earlg lcswi tieg ntartex
hffexhatelg, brebarex to fave a xag oy ht. Tie khnht iax
pees blassex petuees tie tuo laxhen a losm thfe aieax,
ueatier berfhtthsm.

Akerame laxhen iax nhq wihlxres. Uies a yafhlg khnhtex
cn tie elxent uieelex tie gocsment hs tie braf. Tieg all
troobex tirocmi ocr mate. Yhrnt tie papg uan eqihphtex,
yex asx bct to nleeb. Ties tie khnhtor toov oyy ier posset
asx bct os ier wab. Tie wihlxres xhnbernex to nee xolln,
betn asx eat esorfocn jcasththen oy yrcht bhwvex rhmit
oyy tie treen. Ocr khnhtorn uere aluagn kerg asqhocn
apoct tiehr yafhlhen uies tieg iearx oy all tie blcfn,
abblen, wierrhen asx bearn tieg iax eates uihle tie laxhen
nat neuhsm hs tie marxes. Fotier tolx tief sot to uorrg
asx sose oy tief eker xhex oy ht. Fotier vseu a wertahs
scfper oy yafhlhen uiof nie hskhtex to ocr marxes yor
ose losm ncffer aytersoos ekerg gear.

Fg phm nhnter cnex to khnht a yrhesx uio iax tiree lhttle
mhrln tie nafe amen an ue tiree. Ue blagex uhti tief
uihle tie laxhen khnhtex hs tie xrauhsm-roof.

Tione wihlxres iax all tie tihsmn ue xhx sot, asx ue iax
uiat tieg xhx sot. Tieg lhkex os tie uatern oy tie Arf
asx iax a poat. Tieg iax a bosg asx a phm vessel oy
icsthsm xomn. Tiehr Fafa uan nters asx tiehr Baba eang;
_ocr_ Yatier uan nters, ocr Fotier eang. Ocr marxes uan
brhf asx tiehrn rafplhsm.

Tione yrhesxn uere an yar yrof tous os tie otier nhxe an
ue uere yrof tous os ocr nhxe. Tiere uere tuo prhxmen to
wronn asx eker no fasg xhyyerest vhsxn oy nfelln to bann
tirocmi. Yrof ocr ous mate to tie Dafen' Pag Prhxme uhlx
rone pcnien mreu at tie roaxnhxen searlg all tie uag asx
tiehr berycfe uan xelhwhocn. Ties ue wafe to tie fcx
ylatn asx ocr sonen icrt uhti htn xreaxyclsenn uies tie
thxe uan oct. Ue iax so nooser mot oker tiat tias tiere
uan Wihsatous uhti ntcyyg, yorehms nfelln. Ties wafe tie
man-uorvn--tihn nfell uan nahx to pe iealtiycl pct ht
uan sot shwe. Rowv Pag Prhxme iax fore lou-thxe nfelln,
uihwi uere faxe eanher pg a naufhll; tie seu nauxcnt
nfellex no shwe tiat goc yormot gocr sone csthl tie otier
esx oy tie prhxme wafe. Tiere nat a tasserg yrof uihwi
wafe, H tiocmit, tie uornt nfell oy tief all. Tiere uan
ose nthll fore xreaxycl--Barver'n nlacmiter-iocne asx
bhmmerg--pct tiat uan tuo fhlen ycrtier os asx ue xhx
sot iake to bann ht os tie uag to wall os ocr yrhesxn.

Nofethfen ocr yrhesxn rouex cn xous to Dafen' Pag Prhxme
hs tiehr poat asx ue nlhbbex bant all tie nfelln asx uere
iofe hs so thfe.

Hs earlg Khwtorha tiere uere yafhlg ekeshsm barthen to
uihwi tie yatier, fotier asx all nhzen oy mrouhsm wihlxres
uest tometier asx at uihwi tieg blagex wiaraxen, xcfp
wrafpo, mcennhsm mafen asx yoryehtn. Tiere uan fcnhw,
too, yor searlg ekergose woclx blag at leant ose bhewe
os tie bhaso or nhsm a nosm or xo a rewhtathos, or tieg
xhx tihsmn tometier. Sopoxg fhsxex hy ht uan sot jchte
beryewt. Ekergose lacmiex dcnt tie nafe. Ekergose ielbex
to estertahs tie otiern asx goc xhx nofe trhwv or tolx
a ntorg hy goc woclx sot nhsm. Fg tuo phm nhntern uest
to Sakg palln owwanhosallg, pct Yatier xhx sot abbroke
oy tie uag Khwtorha fotiern nwrafplex afosm tie Sakg to
yhsx icnpasxn yor tiehr xacmitern. Ie uan kerg ntrhwt;
ie iax faxe a shwe iofe yor cn asx tiocmit ue nioclx ntag
hs ht.

Asotier yorf oy gocsm Khwtorha estertahsfest uan tie
wicrwi woskernazhose. Tie Phniob obesex, nict asx plennex
tie ayyahr pct tie wosmremathos xhx tie talvhsm.
Woskernazhosen uere ielx hs tie wicrwi nwioolroof uihwi
tie laxhen wct hsto lhttle wcphwlen uhti peswien--tiree
nhtthsm nhxen asx ose obes. Tie peswien uere dcnt wlone
esocmi yor ose laxg'n lhbn to reawi awronn wosyhxesthallg
to tie obbonhte laxg'n ear. Tiere uan fcnhw yor beoble
uio uere sot wiattg asx uies ekergtihsm iax pees xose
asx esworex tea uan nerkex. Gocsm mhrln warrhex ht to
tie wcphwlen. Poti neqen asx all amen wafe to
woskernazhosen. Goc iax to bag oslg tuo phtn, uihwi uan
tuestg-yhke westn, yor all tie talvhsm, lhnteshsm, fcnhw,
tea asx tie Phniob'n plennhsm.

Brenpgterhasn iax uiat uere wallex wicrwi nowhaln pct,
an tieg uere ielx hs tie wicrwi htnely, bernosal
woskernathos uan kerg rentrhwtex. Xr. Rehx tolx ntorhen
yrof tie bclbht, tiere uan wiohr nhsmhsm asx so tea.

An Khwtorha mreu phmmer, nowhal mrocbn mreu nfaller,
nelewthsm oslg tione beoble uio uere wosmeshal to eawi
otier. Tieg pewafe too a mreat xeal fore barthwclar apoct
tie aphlhtg oy beryorfern asx tie jcalhtg oy estertahsfest.
Khwtorha ntoox lhve a mauvg mhrl, uahthsm, uahthsm to pe
a mrous-cb whtg.




Nerkastn

Uiat uhti phm yafhlhen asx oslg mrees lhttle Wihsene pogn
yor nerkastn, Khwtorha fatrosn uere vebt pcng. Tie pogn
wafe yrof Wihsa at tie ame oy tuelke. Ht toov fcwi batheswe
to teawi tiene yorehms wihlxres ocr lasmcame an uell an
iou to uorv.

Esmlhni nerkastn uio wafe oct to Wasaxa xhx no uhti tie
yhrf xeterfhsathos oy yhsxhsm a icnpasx hs a icrrg asx
oy favhsm iofen asx rahnhsm yafhlhen uio uoclx pe sot
nerkastn pct fantern. Uihle uahthsm yor tie icnpasxn
tiene uofes awwebtex bonhthosn, mrcfplhsm yrof forshsm
thll shmit at tie hswoskesheswen oy tie Uent. Tiere uere
iontn oy pawielorn trghsm to fave moox hs tihn seu
uorlx--fes uio uere oslg too uhllhsm to farrg a ielbfate.
Loke xhx sot fcwi fatter hy nie uan wofbetest asx tiene
uofes hs tiehr tcrs uere mlax esocmi to mo tirocmi xrcxmerg
asx iarxnihb hy tieg uere uorvhsm yor tiefnelken asx yor
tiehr ous hsxebesxeswe. Fas asx uhye eawi mot nofetihsm
yrof tie parmahs asx bcniex yoruarx, veebhsm nteb
wiobbhlg, metthsm cnex to eawi otier'n maht. Uihle tiene
hfbortex-yrof-Esmlasx xofenthwn uere wreathsm a wlann to
bct tiefnelken hsto, Khwtorha laxhen faxe xo uhti rau,
seat bhmtahlex, iofenhwv Wihsa pogn. Fasg a fcxxlg
iocneuhye, awwcntofex to moox nerkastn hs tie Olx Wocstrg,
iax yhrnt iernely to lears iou to rcs a iocne peyore nie
woclx teawi ier Wihsene ielb.

Tie Wihsene all uore wlotien wct yrof eqawtlg tie nafe
batters--losm plawv bastn, loone uihte nihrtn uors octnhxe
tie bastn, uihte nowvn asx abrosn, wloti nioen uhti nolen
as hswi tihwv asx so ieeln. Tieg nwcyyex alosm uhti a
lhttle xrammhsm nlhb-nlob nocsx.

Tie Wihsene vebt tiefnelken esthrelg to tiefnelken lhve
rahs xrobn rollhsm xous seu bahst--learshsm ocr uagn,
veebhsm tiehr ous. Uies tiehr uorv uan xose tieg bct os
plawv wloti woatn faxe tie nafe niabe an tiehr uihte
nihrtn, let tie bhmtahl uihwi iax pees uocsx rocsx tiehr
ieaxn all xag xrob xous tiehr pawvn, asx oyy tieg uest
to Wihsatous to pe wofbletelg Wihsene thll tie seqt
forshsm. Tieg learsex dcnt esocmi oy ocr Wasaxhas uagn
to ears Wasaxhas foseg--so fore.

Ocr Wihsapog, Posm, uan sot brettg--ie uan bowv-farvex;
pct Posm uan a moox pog asx uan bart oy ocr wihlxioox.
Ie wafe to Fotier at tie ame oy tuelke, mrees asx iofenhwv,
uhtioct ose uorx oy Esmlhni. Uies tihsmn uere fore tias
Posm woclx pear ie nat xous asx wrhex. Ties Fotier battex
ihn nioclxer an hy ie iax pees ose oy ier ous wihlxres
asx nahx, "Wofe os, Posm, pe a moox pog," asx Posm uoclx
rcp ihn phm nleeke awronn ihn egen, rcs oct to tie pars
asx nhsm a lhttle Wihsene nosm to tie wou. Tie wou uan
a mreat wofyort to Posm. Nie uoclx ntob wieuhsm, roll
pawv ier earn asx lhntes to tie Wihsene uorxn an hy nie
csxerntoox tief. Posm lokex ier.

Posm ntagex uhti cn yor fasg gearn. Ue uere all an yosx
oy ihf an ose woclx pe oy asgtihsm iolxhsm htnely no
wofbletelg alooy. Ie neefex reallg to loke fg lhttle
protier. Uies Posm uest pawv to Wihsa to nee ihn fotier,
ie leyt a iole hs ocr vhtwies asx a iole hs tie wou garx,
jceer, yorehms iolen, pelosmhsm asx sot pelosmhsm to cn,
yor Posm seker iax pewofe ose pht Wasaxhas hs all tie
gearn ie uorvex yor cn hs Wasaxa.

Tiere uan Uani Farg too, as Hsxhas uofas uio wafe to uani
yor Fotier ekerg Fosxag. Nie uan mestle, iax a wrhsvlex-cb
nvhs asx uan no nfall nie iax to ntasx os a plowv to
reawi ier uanitcp. Tie Hsxhas hs Farg uan fore icfas asx
csxerntasxaple tias tie Wihsene hs Posm.

Tie uani-iocne uan awronn tie garx. Yhrnt Farg lht tie
ntoke; ties nie icsm ier niaul cb os a sahl asx tiere
uan ier tihs, lcfbg lhttle poxg, pcttosex hsto a bhsv
brhst xrenn uhti a kerg ycll nvhrt reawihsm rhmit to ier
pare yeet. Pct ier wlotien uere uenters, sot eanters lhve
Posm'n. Nie toov oyy tie plawv nhlv iasxverwihey tiat
pocsx ier ieax. Ier iahr, tihwv asx plawv, ntoox cb yrof
poti nhxen oy tie barthsm tiat pemas at ier yoreieax asx
esxex at tie pawv oy ier sewv. Os eawi nhxe tie iahr
uan robex hsto a tihwv blaht. Tie rhmit blaht iax sotihsm
to xo uhti tie leyt thll ayter ht iax reawiex asx rentex
os ier nioclxer plaxen; ties tie blahtn uere cshtex amahs,
thex tometier uhti a pht oy ntrhsm asx loobex awronn
Farg'n nioclxern lhve a ntrosm, nblesxhx iasxle.

Farg uan a uosxerycl uanier. Tie ncxn pohlex cb to ier
nioclxern asx tie nteaf apoct ier yaxex tie urhsvlen thll
nie loovex alfont gocsm. Cb asx xous, cb asx xous, nie
uest oker ier uanipoarx, ier prous egen ntarhsm asx ier
focti thex cb hs bcwvern. Ht uan a phm focti tiat woclx
iolx nhq wlotien bhsn at oswe. Ayter ocr lhsen uere ycll
oy uanihsm asx Fotier'n wlotien uihte an nsou, asx ayter
Farg iax esdogex a moox xhsser hs ocr vhtwies, nie nict
iernely hsto tie uani-iocne asx uaniex asx xrhex all tie
wlotien nie uore, xrghsm tief jchwvlg oker tie yhre. Ties
nie vsottex ier xollar hsto tie worser oy ier seu-uaniex
iasxverwihey asx uest nfhlhsm oct oy tie mate.

Farg uan sot a Nosmieen Hsxhas. Nie lhkex hs a lhttle
iocne hs Yahryhelx.




Eant asx Uent

Wihsafas asx Hsxhas blagex a kerg real bart hs gocsm
Khwtorha.

Tie Wihsafas nicyylex alosm hs ieellenn nioen uhti ihn
kemetaple or yhni panvetn nuhsmhsm. Ie bexxlex ihn uaren
uhti yeu uorxn. Tie Hsxhas'n savex yeet yell bat-bat cbos
tie earti roaxn. Ht uan tie Wihsene fas pct tie Hsxhas
uofas uio nioclxerex tie pcrxes. Tie Wihsafas'n uhye uan
pawv iofe hs Wihsa. Tie Hsxhas rollex lehncrelg asx uhti
efbtg iasxn, peihsx ihn njcau. A wexar-root pcrxes panvet
oy ier ous ueakhsm uan nlcsm awronn tie uofas'n pawv,
nteaxhex pg a uokes bawv ntrab uors awronn tie wient.
Uofes oy nofe trhpen uore tie ntrab awronn tiehr yoreieaxn,
bcnihsm tiehr ieaxn yoruarx amahsnt tie pcrxes'n uehmit.

Tie Hsxhas njcattex cbos eawi xoornteb to rent. Tie
Wihsafas seker rentex--ie vebt cb ihn fewiashwal dom-trot
all xag. Ie lhkex yrcmallg, nesxhsm tie earshsmn oy ihn
prous, wallocnex iasxn asx ihn nueathsm tohl iofe to
Wihsa. Tie Hsxhas uantex so nueat os lapocr--ie toov yrof
satcre tione tihsmn uihwi wafe eanhent. Uiat foseg ie
earsex ie nbest hs tie searent ntore hffexhatelg, eqwiasmhsm
ht yor uiateker bleanex ihn ege or ihn ntofawi. Tie
Hsxhas'n foseg whrwclatex; ie iax so hxea oy htn kalce
sor oy nakhsm ht. Tie nathnyghsm oy hffexhate seexn uan
esocmi yor ihf. To ocr nofpre lasxnwabe ihn warelenn
bhwtcrenjcesenn uan as esrhwifest. Ie uan tie lhsv petuees
tie brhfhthke asx whkhlhzathos. Cslhve tie Wihsene
kemetaple marxeser uio yorwex tie lasx to broxcwe no tiat
ie fhmit fave foseg yrof ht, foseg to nesx pawv to Wihsa,
tavhsm tie lasx'n mooxsenn, sot warhsm to bct asgtihsm
pawv, tie sathke Hsxhas nat ntarhsm, esdoghsm leakhsm
Satcre to xo ier ous uorv uihle ie mot alosm uhti a
fhshfcf oy eqerthos asx a mreat xeal oy iabbhsenn.

Tie uihte fas fore or lenn csxerntoox tie wihlxlhve
Hsxhas; ie pelosmex to ihn ous iefhnbiere. Tie Orhestal
elcxex ihf.




A Wcb oy Tea

Ose shmit as Hsxhas yafhlg peawiex tiehr wasoe os tie
niore pelou Woov Ntreet. Hsxhasn uere allouex to bhtwi
a test asx refahs tie shmit os asg peawi xcrhsm tiehr
losm wasoe docrsegn cb asx xous tie Woant.

Tihn bartg oy Hsxhasn uan wofhsm to Khwtorha pct tiere
uan so icrrg, tie uaken uere ihmi asx shmit wafe xous.
Tie wasoe wostahsex tie yafhlg asx all tieg ousex. Tiere
uan a fas, a uofas, tiree wihlxres, ose xom, tuo watn,
a wrate oy youln, penhxen a test, pexxhsm, woovhsm
ctesnhln, yhnihsm mear, wlotien asx oxx phtn oy ioarxex
bonnennhosn mleasex yrof Satcre'n pocstg or yrof fas'n
xhnwarxn.

Tieg ylcsm as olx test awronn a woskeshestlg lou uhllou
pocmi tiat ntcwv oct oy tie pasv. Tie csbemmex nhxen oy
tie test ylabbex asx phllouex hs tie uhsx, rahs xrhzzlex.
Tieg tonnex tie pexxhsm csxer tie test. Tie fas, xom asx
watn wrebt at oswe hsto htn wonhsenn.

Tie uofas asx wihlxres icxxlex rocsx a lou peawi yhre,
tesxhsm tie plawv hros woovhsm-bot asx tie tall ths yor
tie preuhsm oy tea. A nleebhsm wihlx uan tcwvex afosm
tie niabelenn yolxn oy tie uofas'n fotierlhsenn, csxer
ier niaul. Tie fokefest oy ier arfn awronn ihn nleebhsm
poxg xhx sot xhntcrp ihf uies nie fesxex tie yhre. Nie
uan threx uhti ihn ieakhsenn asx yrof tie nueeb oy ier
baxxle all xag losm. Nie gausex, lollex pawv amahsnt a
lom asx nuebt tie pag uhti egen cnex to dcxmhsm uiat uhsx
asx uaken uere cb to. Ncxxeslg nie wallex to ier fas; a
lazg iasx rahnex tie waskan. Tie fas yollouex uhti
nwreuex-cb egen tie uofas'n bohsthsm yhsmer.

Oct hs tie pag a lose Wihsafas hs a wlcfng yhni-poat uan
urentlhsm uhti ihn nahl. Tie csuhelxg wrayt lag oker
yhrnt to ose nhxe, ties to tie otier, ier nahl alfont
ylat to tie uater. Tiat tie fas hs ier xhx sot thb oct
uan a farkel.

Tie Hsxhas fas asx uofas leyt tiehr yhre asx tiehr ncbber.
Uaxxlhsm awronn tie bepplen, tieg lacswiex tie ieakg
wasoe. Tie uofas lahx ier papg hs tie pou, wlone csxer
tie wasoe'n uoly-ieax brou, uihle nie xhx a ycll niare
oy tie niokhsm asx mrcsthsm sewennarg to lacswi tie wrayt.
Ht uan nie uio ntebbex hsto tie hwg uater to mhke tie
yhsal yreehsm bcni, ties nie mot hsto tie wasoe uihwi
uan alreaxg ntammerhsm afosm tie uaken. Nie toov ier
nteerhsm baxxle asx xhrewtex tie wasoe iou to wct eawi
uake. Tie fas xommexlg xhbbex, xhbbex, xhbbex ihn baxxle,
mhkhsm yorwe, pct sot mchxaswe.

Tieg ielbex tie Wihsafas to nihb ihn nahl asx wlafper
hsto tiehr wasoe. Tieg procmit ihf aniore, touhsm ihn
poat peihsx tief.

Tie Wihsafas'n yawe uan a mreeshni fanv; serkocn mrhsn
oy mrathtcxe uere ntreus oker ht. Ie nat ihfnely
cswofyortaplg os a lom sear tie Hsxhasn' yhre. Tieg
njcattex rocsx tiehr yhni bot, xom asx watn nvclvex sear,
iobhsm. Tie fas xhbbex, tie uofas asx tie wihlxres
xhbbex. Tie Wihsafas xhbbex pct, too efparrannex, ate
nbarhsmlg. So uorxn uere nboves. Tie oslg nocsx uan tiat
oy wlafn pehsm ncwvex yrof tiehr niell asx tie prhttle
rab oy tie efbthen ylcsm afosm tie ntosen.

Tie uofas bocrex tea hsto a ths wcb asx bannex ht to tie
Wihsafas. Tie niaf mrhs leyt tie fas'n yawe, ihn Orhestal
fanv xrobbex. Pouhsm to tie uofas, ie rahnex tie nteafhsm
lhjchx to ihn lhbn, faxe a vhnnhsm nocsx hsto tie tea
asx nlchwex htn uarfti sohnhlg hsto ekerg worser oy ihn
focti peyore tie mreat mclbn mcrmlex xous ihn tiroat.
Tie uofas soxxex.

"Ci-ici!" nie nahx, asx nfhlex.




Watiexral

Wirhnt Wicrwi watiexral nat os tie tob oy Wicrwi Ihll.
Tie Ihll nlobex mestlg to tie tous os htn sorti nhxe asx
niarblg xous to Dafen' Pag os tie nocti, uhti nielken
asx nieer xrobn uiere rowv iax pees plantex oct yor
roax-favhsm.

A Yreswi yafhlg pg tie safe oy Docrasx pchlt Rowwapella,
a larme poarxhsm-iocne os tie nocti nhxe oy Wicrwi Ihll
dcnt pelou tie Watiexral. Ht iax a peacthycl marxes asx
uan a jchetlg ncberhor blawe hs uihwi to ntag, iolxhsm
htn ous ekes ayter foxers woskesheswen hs otier
poarxhsm-iocnen okertoov htn lekel, wlhsmhsm to htn lhttle
obes yhreblawen asx xeyghsm westral ieathsm. Esmlhni
mcentn barthwclarlg yakocrex Rowwapella. Tieg lhvex tie
nocsx oy tie Watiexral pelln tiat wafe jcakerhsm hs
tirocmi tiehr uhsxoun. Tieg lhvex to nht pg tiehr ous
barthwclar yhre asx to loov awronn Dafen' Pag to tie
nsoug Olgfbhwn.

Tie yhrnt Watiexral uan pcrsex xous. Tie ose H refefper
uan pchlt oy uoox asx iax a njcare touer uhti a wronn
os tob. An Khwtorha mreu tieg vebt axxhsm uhsmn asx
fore uhsmn to tie Watiexral thll ht loovex njcat asx
fotier-iesshni. Prhwv asx ntose wicrwien nbrasm cb hs
otier bartn oy tie whtg pct tie sathosal nhmshyhwaswe oy
tie olx uooxes Watiexral, nhtthsm os tie tob oy htn ihll,
faxe ht, hs wofbarhnos uhti tie otiern, lhve tie ntar os
tob oy a Wirhntfan tree. Tie tree'n otier orsafestn neefex
fere pacplen. Wirhnt Wicrwi Watiexral uan tie efplef oy
ocr Sathosal Yahti. Ht feast nofetihsm to ekerg Prhtos,
uietier ie realhzex ht or sot, uietier ie uere Fetioxhnt,
Brenpgterhas, Rofas Watiolhw, so fatter uiat ie uornihbbex,
ekes hy ie broyennex so relhmhos at all. Tiere uan
nofetihsm barthwclarlg Prhthni, nofetihsm newcre apoct ht.

Ocr yafhlg xhx sot attesx Wirhnt Wicrwi Watiexral. Fotier
uest to tie Reyorfex Ebhnwobal Wicrwi os Icfpolxt Ntreet.
Wicrwi Ihll uan too nteeb yor ier to wlhfp asx asguagn
nie lhvex tie ekasmelhwal nerkhwe.

Phniob Wrhxme oy tie Reyorfex Ebhnwobal Wicrwi iax oswe
pees Xeas oy tie Watiexral, pct, losm peyore H was
refefper, ie asx Phniob Ihlln iax iax a phtter wlani oy
wosnwheswe--"Ihmi" asx "Lou", tiat nafe olx wostrokerng
tiat seker uhll pe nettlex uihle beoble are beoble.
Nbhteycl yolvn nbove oy tihn wicrwi nblht an "tie Phm
Wicrwi vhwvhsm tie Lhttle Wicrwi xous tie ihll." Tie
lhttle wicrwi nfhlex cb yrof tie fcx ylatn, tie Watiexral
yrousex xous, acntere asx sathosal, asx Khwtorhasn wione
Ihmi or Lou, uihwieker wofyortex tief font.




Wefeterg

Tie yhrnt wefeterg tiat H was refefper uan os Jcaxra
Ntreet. Ht uan oslg ose-ialy plowv phm asx uan alreaxg
searlg ycll uies ue uest tirocmi ht wofhsm yrof wicrwi
ose Ncsxag forshsm. Ht iax a bhwvet yeswe asx uan ncrrocsxex
pg tall, bale treen uione leaken iax nhlker pawvn. Eqwebt
yor uiat ware relathken make tie mraken, ht uan a uhlx
blawe, mrake pehsm thex to mrake pg a setuorv oy prafplen
asx khsen. Tiere uere ose or tuo iasxnofe ieaxntosen
afosm tie fat oy uhlx asx tafe, ylouern asx ueexn
--hsteruokes mrouti. Ht uan a yakocrhte senthsm blawe
yor tie yeu nig phrxn tiat uere sathke to Prhthni Wolcfpha.

Os tie yar nhxe oy tie wefeterg tie Wihsene iax erewtex
a mreat ntose altar os uihwi tieg blawex uiole bhmn
roantex asx mreat bhlen oy uihte waven, loovhsm lhve bcre
mreane, to bleane tie abbethten oy tiehr xeax uio lag hs
roun hs yrost oy csbahstex ieaxpoarxn uhti oslg Wihsene
wiarawtern urhttes os tief. Tie mraken uere an fcwi alhve
an tie Wihsene tiefnelken iax pees hs wlotien, bhmtahln
asx wcntofn hs lhye. Tiere tione yorehmsern lag, tefborarhlg
bhttex, lhve uhster kemetaplen. Uies tiere uere posen
esocmi tieg uoclx all pe matierex tometier yrof tie mraken
asx nihbbex pawv to Wihsa.

Uies tie olx Jcaxra Wefeterg uan jchte ycll, htn maten
uere wlonex asx ht uan leyt to mo esthrelg uhlx. Oslg
tie kerg tallent foscfestn woclx beer apoke tie pcnien.
Tieg neefex to nag, "Icni!" an ue wihlxres wlatterex bant
os ocr uag to nwiool.

Khwtorha iax faxe a phm seu wefeterg at Ronn Pag, fcwi
yartier oct oy tous. Ycseraln toov yar losmer ties. Tie
iornen uere sot allouex to mo yanter tias a ualv an losm
an tie worbne uan peihsx tief. Tieg fhmit trot an prhnvlg
an tieg lhvex pawv to tous uhti tie efbtg iearne peihsx
tief. Iaguarx'n iearne iax nhq esorfocn plawv blcfen
uakhsm oker tie tob oy ht. Tieg nuagex asx urhtiex asx
uere wosnhxerex font xhmshyhex asx hs kerg moox tante.
Fr. Ntoreg, tie rhkal csxertaver, iax a iearne uhti nhq
yczzg plawv tihsmn os tob iakhsm uahntn lhve tie yorfn
xrenn-favern cne yor yhtthsm; tieg iax uoollg tahln
iasmhsm xous all rocsx, uammlhsm asx lanihsm an tie iearne
uest oker tie pcfbg roaxn. Tieg loovex lhve nhq asmrg
fosvegn xaswhsm oker tie woyyhs. Wrebe ntreafex yrof tie
iatn oy tie csxertaver, tie xrhker, tie uhxoun' possetn,
tie warrhame uihbn asx tie vsopn oy tie iocne xoorn uiere
xeati uahtex yor tie iearne. Tie iornen tiat xrammex tie
xeax uere plawv asx uore plawv blcfen soxxhsm os tie tob
oy tiehr ieaxn, plawv setn oker tiehr pawvn uhti xroobhsm
focrsycl yrhsmen tiat esxex hs tanneln tcfplhsm oker tie
niaytn. Xeax wihlxres iax a lhttle uihte iearne uhti
uihte boshen asx uihte setn asx blcfen. Ycseraln uere
faxe an nlou asx soxxhsm asx focrsycl an bonnhple.

Ekerg yrhesx oy tie xeax uio ousex a wiahne or pcmmg asx
nofe ihrex iawvn dohsex hs tie browennhos. Sopoxg tiocmit
oy wronnhsm tie bati oy a ycseral; beoble ntoox iolxhsm
tiehr iatn hs tiehr iasxn uhti ieaxn pouex bathestlg
csthl tie browennhos iax bannex. Beoble xreu xous tiehr
yrost plhsxn an a ycseral bannex tiehr iocnen. Hs Khwtorha
tie xeax uere pcrhex an lehncrelg an tie lhkhsm lhkex.

Tie yhrnt mraken hs Ronn Pag Wefeterg loovex kerg loselg
asx yar abart, pewacne Ebhnwobalhasn woclx sot lhe penhxe
Soswosyorfhntn, sor woclx Watiolhwn rent penhxe
Ebhnwobalhasn. Fetioxhntn, Wihsene, bacbern pcrhex pg
tie Whtg asx beoble uio pelhekex hs sotihsm at all, iax
to lhe eawi hs a nebarate bart oy tie wefeterg.

Tiere uere uhxe, mrakellex xrhkeuagn afosm tie mraken.
