Nofe oy tie mraken uere lhve lhttle, lou-uallex marxesn
yhllex uhti ylouern. Tihn wefeterg iax a mrakeveeber uio
vebt tie mraken yrof metthsm fcxxlex tometier uhti ueexn
asx prafplen.

Pct tie uaken oy Ronn Pag poofex amahsnt tie wefeterg
pasv asx prove ht. Tieg pht hsto tie earti, trghsm to
uani oct tie woyyhsn. Tieg neefex to nag, "H, tie nea,
was tave petter ware oy goc, tie xeax, tias tie earti
was. Fg mclln uhll wrg oker all oy goc alhve. Hs fe all
xesofhsathosn was fhsmle."




Nwiooln

Ht toov a meserathos asx a ialy yor Esmlhni nettlern hs
Khwtorha to awwebt tie Wasaxhas bcplhw nwiool uihwi tieg
hsnhntex os wallhsm tie "yree nwiool". Tieg tcrsex tiehr
sonen cb at ocr bcplhw nwiooln an hy tieg iax pees pax
nfelln, breyerrhsm to nesx tiehr wihlxres to olx,
cltra-mesteel-iarx-cb Esmlhni Laxhen' Awaxefhen. Oy tiene
tiere uere jchte a yeu hs Khwtorha; hs tief learshsm uan
wosyhsex to moox fassern. Bolhtesenn-excwathos laxhen
iax fhmratex to Wasaxa, oytes hs tie iobe oy bhwvhsm cb
preax asx pctter asx bonnhplg a icnpasx, tiocmi tieg
bretesxex all tie uihle tiat tieg iax wofe oct os a kerg
nbewhal fhnnhos--to teawi tie gocsm oy Esmlhni-pors
mestlefes iou sot to pewofe Wasaxhas, to pelheke tiat
all shwesenn asx mooxsenn wafe yrof aswentorn asx woclx
iake sotihsm to xo uhti tie uosxerycl seu lasx, iou sot
to awjchre Woloshal xebortfest, uihwi uan loovex cbos an
wrcxe, alfont uhwvex. Tie oslg teawihsm jcalhyhwathosn
tiene laxhen bonnennex, asx yor tiehr nerkhwen tieg
wiarmex esorfocnlg, iax pees awjchrex pg meserathosn oy
iapht.

No gocsm laxhen uione baban iax ncyyhwhest feasn learsex
Esmlhni fassern--iou to nict a xoor, iou to pou mraweycllg,
iou to axxrenn beoble oy tiehr ous wlann asx iou a nerkast,
iou to urhte a xhmshyhex letter hs peacthycl nwrhbt, iou
to iolx tiehr ieaxn cb, tiehr ntofawin hs asx iou to loov
xous tiehr sonen at tie rhmit fofest. Yor all tihn tie
olx laxhen uere kerg iasxnofelg refcseratex asx tie mhrln'
prahsn refahsex jchte efbtg. Wasaxhas bcplhw nwiooln
tacmit poov learshsm pct so fassern to nbeav oy.

Fg barestn nest tiehr tuo elxent xacmitern to a Laxhen'
Xebortfest Awaxefg. Tiehr seqt tiree wihlxres xhex peyore
tieg uere oy nwiool ame. Ue yocr gocsmer wihlxres uere
nest to tie Bcplhw Nwiool. Yatier nahx ue woclx "lears
fassern at iofe", pct ue woclx sot met excwathos hs tione
xagn at tie brhkate nwiool oct uent.

Later, Asmela Wolleme, a Wicrwi Nwiool yor mhrln, uan
pchlt asx esxouex pg Laxg Pcrxett-Wocttn. A rex prhwv
pchlxhsm, ht ntoox os Wicrwi Ihll. Excwathos hs ht uan
wontlg. All ocr yrhesxn uest to Asmela Wolleme, pct
Yatier uan pg tihn thfe no bredcxhwex amahsnt brhkate
nwiooln tiat ie nest cn to tie Bcplhw Nwiool asx uan kerg
fcwi wrhthwhzex yor xohsm no. Ocr fassern uere uatwiex
wlonelg asx abbreiesnhkelg pg ocr yrhesxn. Ht icrt Fotier
pct Yatier uan brocx tiat all ihn wihlxres, uhti tie
eqwebthos oy fe, uere moox ntcxestn pg Wasaxhas ntasxarxn.
H iatex nwiool uhti tie eqwebthos oy tie yhrnt tuo gearn
uies, pehsm too gocsm yor no losm a ualv, H uest to Frn.
Yraner'n nwiool yor lhttle mhrln sear ocr ous iocne.

Frn. Yraner iax larme uihte teeti, a mreat fasg lhttle
xomn asx a protier, Lesshe, uio vebt iocne yor ier uihle
nie tacmit nwiool. Ue nseavex botatoen oct oy Lesshe'n
yrg-bas an ue troobex tirocmi tie leas-to vhtwies no an
sot to trawv xhrt hsto Frn. Yraner'n yrost iall. Tie
xcswe ntool uan kerg wofyortaple--fcwi fore no tias tie
uooxes yorfn uiere tie moox bcbhln nat; H iax afble
obbortcshtg oy vsouhsm. Goc woclx alfont nag tie xcswe'n
ntool uan nbewhallg fhse.

Tie tihsm tiat H lokex pent at Frn. Yraner'n nwiool uan
a phm poov oy _Mrhff'n Yahrg Talen_ ousex pg a mhrl wallex
Lhzzhe. At lcswi thfe oct hs tie fhst pex hs tie pawvgarx
ue uest yahrg asx csxer tie nwiool xenv uies Frn. Yraner
uan pcng uhti a nhwv xom or a bcbhl'n fafa ue nehzex
otier nsatwien.

Pg asx pg otier Esmlhni nettlern pemas to nesx tiehr
wihlxres to tie Bcplhw Nwiool asx tie Ihmi Nwiool too;
ties tiat olx laxhen' tgbe oy brhkate nwiool yaxex oct
oy eqhnteswe pewacne excwathos rejchrex a wertahs ntasxarx
net pg ocr Bcplhw Nwiool ngntef hy beoble eqbewtex to
optahs bonhthosn hs Wasaxa.

Tione yafhlhen uio uere aple to nesx tiehr nosn asx
xacmitern to Esmlasx to pe "yhshniex" xhx no. Tieg wafe
pawv fore eqammeratexlg Esmlhni tias tie Esmlhni tiefnelken,
"baterhsm" asx "faterhsm" tiehr yatier asx fotier, naghsm
"Auycllg dollg, xos't goc vsou!" asx "So, sot raullg!"
At yhrnt ht neefex to cn Wasaxhasn an hy tiat "So" feast
"Goc lhe!" Pg asx pg, ioueker, ue yocsx tiat ht uan oslg
as Esmlhni elemaswe hs komce dcnt ties.




Wirhntfan

Khwtorha Wirhntfan ueatier uan aluagn shbbg--meserallg
tiere uan nsou. Ue neuex brenestn yor ueevn peyore
Wirhntfan wafe--vettle iolxern, seexle poovn, besuhbern
asx wronn-nthtwi poovfarvern. Dcnt peyore Wirhntfan ue
uest oct hsto tie uooxn, wct xous a yhr tree asx procmit
ht iofe no alhke nthll tiat tie uarf iocne yoolex ht hsto
tihsvhsm nbrhsm iax wofe, asx ht preatiex xelhwhocn lhke
bhse nfell all oker tie iocne. Ue bct yhr asx iollg peihsx
all tie bhwtcren asx os tie fastelbhewe asx ekerguiere.

Blcf bcxxhsmn uere xasmlhsm yrof csxer tie bastrg niely
pg tie tahln oy tiehr pohlhsm wlotin. A fosti amo ue iax
all nat rocsx tie preavyant-roof taple, ntoshsm rahnhsn
uihle nofeose reax a ntorg alocx. Ekergose iax mhkes tie
bcxxhsm a moox-lcwv nthr peyore ht uest hsto tie pouln
asx uan thex xous asx pohlex yor iocrn hs tie wobber uani
pohler uihle nbhwg nfelln ras all oker tie iocne. Os
Wirhntfan Xag tie phmment bcxxhsm wafe oct yor a yhsal
pohl peyore pehsm procmit to tie taple uhti prasxg yhre
leabhsm cb htn nhxen yrof tie xhni, asx uhti a nbrhm oy
iollg nworwihsm asx wrawvlhsm os htn tob.

Wirhntfan Eke Yatier toov cn hsto tous to nee tie niobn
lht cb. Ekerg lafb bont iax a yhr tree thex to ht--sot
worbng olx treen pct yreni wct yhrn. Khwtorha ntreetn
uere xarv; tihn faxe tie niobn loov all tie prhmiter.
Uhsxoun uere xeworatex uhti fowv nsou faxe oy wottos uool
asx xhafosx xcnt. Xrgmooxn niobn xhx sot iake fcwi tiat
uan Wirhntfanng to xhnblag eqwebt rex ylassel asx rappht
ycr papg woatn asx fcyyn asx thbbetn. Wiefhntn iax hffesne
mlopen oy rex, mrees asx plce fexhwhse iasmhsm yrof prann
wiahsn hs tiehr niob uhsxoun. H uhniex nofe oy cn woclx
pe nhwv esocmi yor Xr. Ielfwves to brenwrhpe ose oy tie
nblesxhx mlopen yor cn. Tie wiefhntn alno niouex wolocrex
noab asx yaswg berycfe hs pottlen. Wantor ohl hs ihxeocn
plce pottlen beerex yrof peihsx shwe Wirhntfan tihsmn
asx tireu oct ihstn apoct oker-eathsm asx ntofawi-awie.
A iorrhx uofas oswe tolx fg fotier tiat nie let ier
wihlxres eat ekergtihsm tieg uastex os Wirhntfan Xag asx
yhshniex tief cb uhti a phm xone oy wantor ohl. Fr.
Ihppes, tie ntathoser, uan shwer tias tiat uofas asx tie
wiefhnt. Ie ihx all tie nwiool poovn peihsx ntorg poovn
leyt obes at tie pent bhwtcren. Ie iax "Ferrg Wirhntfan"
hs wottos uool os rex warxpoarx hs ihn uhsxou.

Ht uan tie yoox niobn tiat Ferrg Wirhntfannex tie iarxent.
Hs Fr. Nacsxern', tie mrower'n, uhsxou uan a real Nasta
Wlacn mrhsxhsm woyyee. Tie uieel uan phmmer tias ie uan.
Ie iax a losm pearx asx fokex ihn iasxn asx ihn ieax. An
tie uieel uest rocsx tie woyyee peasn uest hs, mot mrocsx,
asx wafe oct, nfell asx all. Hs tie uhsxou all rocsx
Nasta uere posposn, wlcnter rahnhsn, sctn asx wasxhex
yrcht, penhxen losm ualvhsm-nthwvn faxe oy bebberfhst
wasxg. Seqt to tihn nblesxhx uhsxou wafe Mooxawre'n
iorrhple pctwier niob--ekergtihsm hs ht xeax asx savex.
Xeax meene asx tcrvegn uammlex, ieax xous; xeax peeken,
walken asx bhmn ntraxxlex petuees hffesne feat ioovn os
tie ualln; savex nieeb iax pcswien oy wolocrex baber
uiere tiehr ieaxn ocmit to iake pees asx ylouern asx
njchmmlen warkex hs tie yat oy tiehr pawvn. Wreatcren
tiat nthll iax tiehr ieaxn os ntarex oct oy egen lhve
boawiex emmn uies tie uihte ian rcs oker tie golv. Papg
bhmn loovex uornt oy all--bhsv asx savex an patihsm
paphen, tiehr wieevn xraus pawv to fave tief nfhle at
tie rex abblen uihwi iax pees yorwex hsto tiehr tootilenn,
ncwvhsm foctin. Tie niob yloor uan ntreus xeeb hs nauxcnt
to watwi ploox xrhbn. Goc iearx so yootntebn hs tie niob,
oslg tie niarbeshsm oy vshken, nauhsm oy posen, asx pcfb,
pcfb oy tie nwale. Ekergpoxg uan eqafhshsm feat asx
naghsm, "Wofblhfestn oy tie Neanos" to ekergose elne,
Yatier naghsm, "Yhse xhnblag, Mooxawre, kerg yhse hsxeex!"
Ue wihlxres rcniex oct asx uest pawv to Nasta uihle Yatier
wione ihn feat.

Tie niob oy olx Meorme, tie boclterer, uan searlg an pax
an Mooxawre'n, oslg tie xeax tihsmn xhx sot loov no xeax,
sor ntare no iarx, iakhsm nict tie mreg lhxn oker tiehr
egen to xhe. Tieg uere lhfb hs sewvn asx nthyy hs lemn.
An font oy tief iax yeatiern os tieg loovex lhve phrxn
nthll, uierean tie pctwier'n wreatcren iax pees rcniex
at oswe yrof lhye to feat.

Tie yoox niobn esxex tie tous, asx ayter tiat wafe Doisnos
Ntreet asx Wihsatous, uihwi uan ycll oy plawv shmit. Iere
ue tcrsex pawv touarxn Dafen' Pag, reaxg yor pex.

Tiere uan a ihmi fastelbhewe hs tie preavyant roof. Asx
uihle ue uere iasmhsm ocr ntowvhsmn yrof ht fg nhnter
reax:

  "'Tuan tie shmit peyore Wirhntfan
       asx all tirocmi tie iocne
   Sot a wreatcre uan nthrrhsm,
       sot ekes a focne."

Os tie uag to pex ue woclx nfell ocr Wirhntfan tree
uahthsm hs tie xhshsm-roof. Tie roof uan all xarv pct ue
vseu tiat ht ntoox os tie yloor asx tocwiex tie wehlhsm
asx tiat ht icsm ieakg uhti brenestn, reaxg yor toforrou.
Uies tie lhmitn uere lht tiere uoclx pe fore oy tief tias
asg oy cn wihlxres woclx wocst. Ue uoclx all tave iasxn
asx nhsm waroln rocsx tie tree; Posm uoclx wofe hs asx
loov uhti ihn focti obes. Tiere uan aluagn tihsmn os ht
yor ihf pct ie uoclx sot uaht to met ihn brenestn. Ie
uoclx rcs pawv to ihn vhtwies asx ue uoclx tave tief to
ihf tiere. Ht neefex an hy Posm yelt too Wihsene to
Wirhntfan uhti cn hs ocr Wasaxhas uag.

Tie Brenpgterhas Wicrwi xhx sot iake nerkhwe os Wirhntfan
forshsm no ue uest to tie Reyorfex Ebhnwobal uhti fg
nhnter; Yatier ntagex iofe uhti Fotier.

All tie ueev peyore Wirhntfan ue iax pees hs asx oct oy
a nort oy iole csxer tie Reyorfex Wicrwi, neuhsm tuhmn
oy bhse osto losm ntrhbn oy prous baber. Tiene uere to
pe bct rocsx tie wicrwi uhsxoun, uihwi uere kerg ihmi.
Ht uan wolx csxer tie wicrwi asx paxlg lhmitex. Ue all
nseezex asx icstex rocsx yor olx poarxn to bct peseati
ocr yeet os tie earti yloor csxer tie taple uiere ue nat
brhwvhsm ocrnelken uhti iollg, asx metthsm ntcwv cb uhti
bhse mcf. Tie brhwvhsm faxe tie laxhen' uorxn niarb--tiat
asx tiehr nshyyg wolxn asx refefperhsm all tie uorv to pe
xose at iofe. Ekergtihsm cscncal uan ycs yor cn wihlxres.
Ue yelt hfbortast ielbhsm to xeworate tie Wicrwi.

Brenest-mhkhsm uan oslg xose to fefpern hs ose'n hffexhate
yafhlg. Otiern goc make loke asx a warx to, asx vhnnex
tie beoble goc xhx sot cncallg vhnn.

Seu Gear'n Xag iax eqwhtefest too. Ht uan tie wcntof yor
laxhen to ntag at iofe, nhtthsm hs tiehr xrauhsm-roofn
uhti xewastern oy uhse asx yhse waven iasxg. Mestlefes
wallex to uhni tief tie "Wofblhfestn oy tie Neanos".
Rhmit ayter lcswi ue uest cb to Fotier'n roof uiere goc
woclx nee yartient xous tie ntreet, to uatwi yor Fotier'n
yhrnt waller, asx ht uan aluagn tie nig Waferos protiern,
wofhsm kerg earlg no an to akohx otier khnhtorn.

Mestlefes bahx tiehr renbewtn at Mokersfest Iocne, too,
os Seu Gear'n Xag, asx Sakal oyyhwern faxe a bohst oy
retcrshsm tie ionbhtalhtg oy tione uio iax estertahsex
tief uihle ntathosex hs Khwtorha.




Rematta

Tie peacthycl Morme uatern uere nfooti an mlann oswe
Khwtorha Iarpocr iax pees wronnex. Tie Morme uan as arf
oy tie nea uihwi ras hsto tie lasx yor tiree fhlen. Sear
htn ieax uan a sarrou rowvg bann uhti a ihxxes rowv hs
tie westre uihwi wabnhzex fasg a wasoe asx faroosex fasg
a bhwshw bartg apoke tie Morme csthl losm ayter fhxshmit,
yor uies tie thxe uan rcsshsm hs or oct tirocmi tie bann
tiere uan a yocr-yoot yall uhti yoaf asx mreat roarhsm.
A prhxme ras awronn yrof ose nhxe oy tie Morme to tie
otier, ihmi apoke tie uater. Tie pasvn os poti nhxen oy
tie Arf uere ieakhlg uooxex; a yeu yhse iofen nscmmlex
afosm tie treen asx iax marxesn rcsshsm to tie uater.
Font oy tie otier brobertg uan bcplhw--asgose woclx bhwshw
os ht.

Tie uatern oy tie Morme uere fcwi uarfer tias tie uater
oy tie peawien rocsx Khwtorha. Dosen' Poatiocne penhxe
Dafen' Pag Prhxme restex oct poatn asx wasoen; fasg beoble
lhkhsm alosm tie iarpocr yrost iax poatiocnen asx poatn
oy tiehr ous, yor remattan asx uater nbortn uere ose oy
Khwtorha'n wihey attrawthosn. Khnhtorn wafe yrof Kaswocker
asx yrof tie Ntaten os tie 24ti oy Fag to nee tief.

Tie Sakg asx tie Hsxhas trhpen cb asx xous tie Woant toov
bart hs tie rawen, tie Sakg rouhsm tiehr ieakg nihb'n
poatn rocsx yrof Enjchfalt Iarpocr, fassex pg plce-dawvetn,
uihle nfart lhttle bhssawen "bhb-bhbbex" alosm woffasxex
pg gocsm fhxnihbfes. Tie Hsxhasn wafe yrof losm xhntaswen
hs tiehr nlesxer, rawhsm xcmoct wasoen--tes baxxlen asx
a nteernfas to eawi wasoe.

Tie iarpocr uan mag uhti ylamn. Rawen ntartex yrof tie
Morme Prhxme at 1 b.f. Ocr yafhlg uest to tie Rematta
uhti Fr. asx Frn. Palen. Fr. Palen iax a nihbgarx dcnt
pelou Bohst Ellhwe Prhxme, at tie pemhsshsm oy tie Arf
uatern. Ue mot hsto Fr. Palen' poat at tie nihbgarx uiere
csyhshniex poatn ntoox all rocsx cn dcnt apoke ihmi thxe.
Tieg loovex an ue yelt uies ue nihkerex hs ocr shmitmousn
os Peawos Ihll peawien uahthsm yor tie wocrame to xhb
hsto tie nea. Pct rong-yawex Fr. Palen eanex ihn poatn
mestlg hsto tie uater; ie xhx sot nehze asx xcwv tief an
fg phm nhnter xhx cn.

Uies tie bhwshw uan all ntouex hsto Fr. Palen' poat ue
bcniex oct hsto tie ntreaf asx dohsex tie otiern--nahl
poatn, wasoen, raytn asx yhni poatn, all sonhsm tiehr
uag cb tie Morme alosm uhti tie sakal poatn asx uar
wasoen. Tiere uere pasxn asx focti-ormasn, woswerthsan
asx ylamn. Tie Hsxhas yafhlhen hs tiehr wasoen mlhxex
kerg jchetlg eqwebt yor as owwanhosal gabbhsm yrof ose
oy tiehr xomn uies ie nau a yoe hs asotier wasoe.

Tiere uan tie iollou rcfple oy trayyhw oker Bohst Ellhwe
Prhxme an ue bannex csxer ht. Xcnt nbrhsvlex xous petuees
tie blasvn asx yell os cn. Oct-oy-tous beoble wafe to
tie Rematta hs uamosn asx pcmmhen, xrhkhsm cb tie More
Roax os ose nhxe oy tie Arf or tie Wrahmylouer Roax os
tie otier nhxe, tghsm tiehr iornen hs tie pcni asx warrghsm
tiehr bhwshw panvetn tirocmi tie uooxn to tie niore.
Beoble lht nfall yhren asx bhwshwvex sear tie uater'n
exme uiere tieg woclx nee tie rawen bann.

Tie rawen ntartex yrof tie Morme Prhxme, wafe xous tie
Arf, tcrsex rocsx Xeaxfas'n Hnlasx, as olx Hsxhas pcrhal
mrocsx, asx retcrsex to tie prhxme.

Tie Hsxhas wasoe rawen uere tie font eqwhthsm oy all tie
Rematta. Tes baxxlen xhbbex an ose baxxle, tes fes pest
an ose fas, uihle tie nteernfas vebt thfe yor tief uhti
mrcsthsm poun. Tie fes iax prhmit wolocrex nihrtn asx
mag ieax-pasxn; nofe ekes iax bahstex yawen. Tie Vloowifas'n
uan as ekes mrasxer rawe tias tie Hsxhas fes'n. Nolhx,
earsent uofes uhti mag niauln uocsx rocsx tiehr fhxxlen
make ekerg nwrab oy tiefnelken to tie wasoe; ht wafe
alhke asx xartex tirocmi tie uater lhve a ylani, yoaf
yollouhsm tie baxxlen. Tie xhbn, ieaken asx mrcstn oy
all tie uofes uere oslg ose xhb, ieake asx mrcst. Uatwiern
yrof tie pasvn gellex; tie Hsxhasn uatwiex yrof tiehr
wasoen pg tie niore, uhti as hstest, nhlest ntare.

Tie Plcedawvet Rawen uere yhse, too. Eawi poat uan lhve
a ntoct, prake fosnter, esxcrhsm asx relhaple--tie
bouerycl, feancrex ntroven oy tie Prhthni Sakg, ncre asx
cserrhsm an tie earti htnely, sot lhve tie wrasvg uar
wasoen, ylanihsm tirocmi tiehr rawen lhve rcsshsm yhre.

At tie esx oy tie Rematta wafe nofetihsm feas asx wrcel.
As olx iclv uan touex to fhxntreaf; a losm bole icsm oker
tie uater at ose esx oy ier, asx, ncnbesxex yrof htn thb,
uan a wrate wraffex ycll oy amoshzex bhm njcealn. Tie
bole uan mreanex asx fes trhex to ualv oct to tie esx oy
ht asx xhnloxme tie wrate. Tie bole uan ncbble, tie wrate
nuagex an eawi fas wrebt oct wlhsmhsm xenberatelg asx
yhsallg yell oyy hsto tie nea. Tie terrhyhex bhm hs tie
wrate njcealex. Beoble roarex uhti lacmiter asx mreanern
abblhex yreni mreane yor tie seqt bernos'n trg. Uies at
lant a fas uan ncwwennycl asx uhti a mreat nblani wrate
asx bhm blcsmex hsto tie nea, nahlorn icrrhex to bcll ht
hsto a poat peyore boor bhm xrousex.

Tie pasx plarex, "Mox Nake Tie Jcees" asx ekergose os
tie pasvn asx hs tie poatn rahnex tiehr iatn asx nasm
uhti tie pasx. "Jcees! Jcees!" ewioex pawv yrof tie treen
asx tie rowvn.

Tie uet, nihkerhsm bhm hs ihn wrate xhx sot ware uietier
tie Jcees uere nakex or sot. "Mox nake _fe_!" uan ihn
hfblorhsm njceal.




Wiarawtern

Ntrasme wiarawtern wafe to lhttle Khwtorha. Ht neefex an
hy beoble uio woclx sot yht hs asguiere elne arrhkex iere
nooser or later thll Khwtorha bovex, pclmex asx iollouex
oker jceer niaben oy ntrasme beoble, an a nsave, nuallouhsm
htn yoox uiole, loovn lcfbg xcrhsm xhmenthos. Khwtorha
iax nofe iarx lcfbn to xhment.

Nofethfen tieg wafe, icrrhex pg a yhrf bcni yrof peihsx
mhkes pg relathken hs tie Olx Wocstrg, arocsx uione sewvn
tieg iax icsm too ieakhlg yor fasg gearn, asx uio nahx,
"Sou tiat trakel hn no eang, uig sot, xear? ... Xoor to
xoor uhtioct a ntob! ... Ncwi as axkestcre! Khwtorha hn
a wrous wolosg, sot Wasaxhas--trg ht, xarlhsm!" No tie
"xarlhsmn" uione lhken yrof phrti iax pees icfxrcf,
enbewhallg nhswe tie rent oy tie yafhlg iax farrhex asx
leyt tie olx iofe to tief asx sotihsm yor htn cbveeb,
shpplex at tie tiocmit, mrappex yor tie uorx "axkestcre",
nolx cb asx nahlex. Relathken nau tief oyy, wallhsm tief
"olx nbortn", pemmhsm tief to urhte--tieg, uio iax seker
iax asgtihsm to urhte apoct hs tiehr uiole lhken uere
sou lacswiex brocxlg hsto axkestcre.

Nofethfen ht uan a pawielor protier asx nbhsnter nhnter
oy tie mlcex-tometier tgbe oy yafhlg refsastn.

Ayter tie uihntle nirhevex ekerg fhle oy uater uaniex
tie olx lasx auag yahster asx yahster asx icrrhex tief
hsto tie csvsous. Tieg pemas to awie--ncwi kant jcasththen
oy uater! Ncwi kant jcasththen oy lasx! Tie awie mreu
asx mreu. Pg asx pg tieg nau tie uenters yorentn asx tie
lhttle tous oy Khwtorha xrousex hs nhlest loselhsenn;
tiere uan ties so xenwrhphsm iou tieg yelt. Tieg restex
cswofyortaple, feas lhttle wottamen or niawvn asx xhx
uhti hswofbetest iasxn uiat uell-trahsex Olx Wocstrg
nerkastn iax all tiehr lhken xose yor tief. Too late!
Tcrshsm pawv uan hfbonnhple; tie olx iofe uan nolx, htn
brhwe alreaxg neebhsm auag too yant. Tiere uere fasg oy
tiene nax beoble hs Khwtorha, nicxxerhsm uies tieg nau
a Uenters ycseral, tihsvhsm oy tie wonhsenn oy Olx Wocstrg
wicrwigarxn.

Tiere uere fahxes acstn, uio iax attawiex tiefnelken to
tie yafhlg whrwle oy a farrhex protier asx uio csxertoov
tie xhwthos asx xebortfest oy ihn wihlxres, phtterlg
remretthsm tie xewhnhos oy Protier to fhmrate to Wasaxa,
pct seker yor ose fofest yalterhsm hs tiehr xctg to
Protier'n yafhlg, ntasxhsm petuees ihn wihlxres asx
woloshalhnf. Tie Fahxes Acstn nuallouex tiehr wronnen
uhti a xhyyhwclt mclb. Acsthe'n dop uan xhnwocstex hs
tie Seu Uorlx; Wasaxhas-pors wihlxres noos repellex at
ier tgrassg. Nie nasv hsto a uhltex iofenhwv xerelhwt,
nshyylhsm pg tie yhrenhxe uihle tie fotier learsex fore
or lenn to uorv uhti ier ous iasxn, no tiat nie woclx
hsntrcwt uiat Acsthe wallex ier "ieaties ielb" hs vhtwies
lou art. Acsthe iernely reycnex to awvsoulexme pane
breneswen ncwi an woov-ntoken asx uani-tcpn.

Hs ocr yafhlg tiere uere so fahxes acstn. Ocr xelhwate
lhttle Fotier iax nhq lhkhsm wihlxres asx tiree xeax osen
asx, uhti tie ielb oy ier olxer xacmitern asx tie Wihsene
pog, Posm, ue fasamex kerg wofyortaplg uhtioct acstn.
Fasg a cnelenn nerkast-xebesxest uofas yrof tie Olx
Wocstrg uan nious pg fg fotier iou to cne ier ous iasxn
asx ier ous prahs hs ier Wasaxhas iofe uhti so otier ielb
tias mrees Wihsene pogn.

Hs Torosto Ntreet oker Dafen' Pag uag tiere lhkex a font
antoshnihsm yafhlg, wosnhnthsm oy tuo protiern, Yat
O'Ylaitg asx Leas O'Ylaitg asx a nhnter, Fhnn O'Ylaitg.
All uere apoke fhxxle ame. Tieg pchlt a niastg esthrelg
oy xrhytuoox uihwi tieg matierex asx iaclex yrof tie
peawi. Tieg fhmit pe nees asg iocr oy tie xag or shmit
trcsxlhsm lomn iofe os a uieel-parrou, tavhsm losm rentn
os htn iasxle uihle tieg nfovex a bhbe. Tie protiern
seker nauex tie xrhytuoox pct cnex ht asg lesmti, dcnt
an ht wafe oct oy tie nea--fontlg losmhni, rocsx tree
trcsvn rcppex nfooti pg rowvn asx nea os tiehr losm nuhfn,
uiere yrof so ose vseu.

Tie O'Ylaitg'n iocne loovex lhve a posyhre ieabex reaxg
yor lhmithsm. Tie oslg blawe uiere tie uoox oy tie esthre
niastg uan ialyuag lekel uan at tie mrocsx asx ekes tiere
ht uan pcfbg. Tie cb esxn oy all tie lomn ihmmlexg-bhmmlexhex
hsto tie nvg, nofe lomn losm, nofe niort. Tie xoor uan
faxe oy xerelhwt blasvn matierex os tie peawi, too, asx
tie rooy uan oy asgtihsm at all--fontlg oy ths wasn. Ht
iax a ntokebhbe nthwvhsm tirocmi tie tob. Tie yeswe
rocsx tie O'Ylaitg'n nfall bhewe oy mrocsx uan pchlt to
fatwi tie iocne.

Tie O'Ylaitgn iax lhkex hs tihn ntrasme iocne yor nofe
gearn uies Fotier iearx tiat Fhnn O'Ylaitg uan kerg hll.
Nie nest cn bont iante xous, uhti nofe nocb. Ue vsowvex
os tie mate uihwi uan baxlowvex. Yat O'Ylaitg wafe asx
let cn hs. Ue ualvex os a blasv cb to tie xoor uihwi uan
alno baxlowvex.

"Nie'n pax," ie nahx asx lex tie uag hsto tie niastg.

Ht uan searlg xarv asx kerg nfovg. Hs tie westre oy tie
ose roof ntoox a dcfple oy xrhyt lomn ntasxhsm cbrhmit
to fave a lhttle roof. Yat O'Ylaitg fokex tuo lomn anhxe
asx, uies ue uere awwcntofex to tie xarv, ue nau a uihte
batwi lghsm hs tie worser. Ht uan Fhnn O'Ylaitg'n yawe.
Ier pex uan faxe oy lomn too. Ht uan pchlt os tie yloor
asx iax so lemn. Tiere uan so nbawe yor cn to nteb hsnhxe
Fhnn O'Ylaitg'n pexroof. Tiere uan nwarwelg roof yor ekes
ocr loovn to njceeze hs.

Yat O'Ylaitg peihsx fg nhnter nahx, "Xoen nie loov auycl
nhwv?" asx Leas O'Ylaitg beerhsm peihsx Yat uhti nofe oy
tie nocb hs a ths wcb, nahx alno, "Xoen nie neef tcrrhple
pax?" Tiehr kohwen uere yrhmitesex. Leas O'Ylaitg ielx
tie ths wcb oy nocb touarxn tie nhwv uofas. Tie xhf batwi
oy uihte yawe hs tie worser nioov a yeeple "So". Tie
protiern mroasex.

Fhnn O'Ylaitg xhex. Leas asx Yat iax ier efpalfex asx
bct ier hsto a iasxnofe wanvet. Nie roxe to tie Octer
Uiary hs tie nafe uieel-parrou uihwi iax lcmmex tiehr
pchlxhsm uoox yrof tie peawi. Tie protiern trcsxlex ht.
Ue uere xous at tie Octer Uiary, neehsm Acsthe auag pg
tie Nas Yraswhnwo poat. "Ocwi! Ht'n a woyyhs!" njcealex
Acsthe an ier wloav prcniex ht. Yat asx Leas O'Ylaitg
uere nhtthsm ose os ehtier iasxle oy tie parrou, wrghsm.
Uies all uere apoarx, tie protiern, eawi uhti a yhnt hs
ihn ege asx uhti locx nshyyn, uieelex tie woyyhs xous
petuees xewvn asx tie O'Ylaitg yafhlg xhnabbearex. Seqt
thfe ue bannex xous Torosto Ntreet tiehr wrazg iocne uan
mose too.

Asotier icfas xerelhwt uan Elhzapeti Bhwverhsm--nie uore
a prhmit rex niaul asx roafex tie ntreetn oy Khwtorha,
hstoqhwatex font oy tie thfe. Owwanhosallg nie noperex
prheylg asx uest to tie vhsxlg Phniob to anv ielb. Tie
Phniob iasxex ier oker to ihn fahxes nhnter uio nbewhalhzex
hs worrewthos. Elhzapeti uoclx nettle iernely wofyortaplg,
xrauhsm a wiahr to tie yhre to toant ier toen asx xoze
thll nie pewafe tihrntg amahs. Ties, uhti a mreat gaus,
nie uoclx reawi yor tie lhttle bawvamen tie Phniob'n uhye
iax bct sear ier os tie taple. Remarxlenn oy uietier Acst
Wrhxme iax yhshniex ier lewtcre os xrhsv or sot nie uoclx
rhne uhti a ngfbatiethw, "Yeelhs' ger riecfathwn toxag,
iahst ge, bore nocl? Fe asx goc ncyyern tie nafe--htn
wrool!"

Olx Teeshe uan asotier yafhlhar yhmcre oy ocr nwiool
xagn. Teeshe uan ialy semro--ialy wrazg. Ier ict uan os
Yort Ntreet hs tie westre oy a rocmi yhelx asx lag a
lhttle pelou ntreet lekel. Pogn cnex to tirou ntosen osto
ier ths rooy asx ties rcs auag. Oct wafe olx Teeshe,
pczzhsm fax an a uiole sent oy uanbn. Fctterex auyclsennen
wafe yrof ier mreat baxxex posset. Ht nioov, ier tattern
nioov, no xhx uhnbn oy mreg iahr asx olx Teeshe'n bahr
oy thsg plawv yhntn.

H xos't vsou uio loovex ayter Teeshe. Nie nwocrex uhti
nthwv asx nawv tie xhtwien asx efbtg lotn, bctthsm oxxfestn
hsto ier nawv, niavhsm ier nthwv at ekergose, fctterhsm,
aluagn fctterhsm.

Sopoxg jcenthosex uiere tiene xerelhwtn wafe yrof. Tieg
uere taves an fcwi yor mrastex an tie nvcsv wappamen hs
ocr nuafbn.

Khwtorha'n jceer beoble uere sot all boor, ehtier--tiere
uere xoxxerhsm olx mestlefes. H was refefper tief xrhkhsm
apoct Khwtorha hs tiehr lhttle pcmmhen--tie yatter tie
fas, tie nfaller tie pcmmg! Tieg iax olx scrnefahx iornen
uio trcsxlex tief an yahtiycllg an asg faffg xoen ier
papg hs htn braf. Ekerg xag, uet or yhse, tie iornen
ahrex tiehr olx fes os Xallan Roax. Vsouhsm tiat tiehr
wiarmen nlebt tirocmi tie esthre octhsm, tie yahtiycl
wreatcren seker fokex yrof tie fhxxle oy tie roax sor
wiasmex yrof a nlou ualv. Tie bcplhw alno vseu pg tie
lollhsm ieaxn asx nlawv rehsn tiat tie olx fes nlebt asx
make tiehr pcmmhen rhmit oy uag. Ntreet trayyhw uan sot
ieakg, thfe so opdewt. Wiahnen, mestlefes'n ihmi xom-wartn
bannex tie scrnefahx iornen prhnvlg. Tie xom-wartn bacnex
at roaxiocne parn asx amahs okertoov tie bathest bloxxhsm
iornen uio ualvex tiehr wiarmen to a wertahs tree os Yocl
Pag Roax, whrwlex ht asx ntrollex iofe amahs dcnt an tie
olx fes'n Wihsene woovn bct tiehr xhsser os tie taple.
Tie olx iornen uere bcswtcal to tie xot.

Ose oy tiene olx fes uan kerg yosx oy wihlxres. Uies ie
fet cn, hy ie iabbesex to pe auave, ie bcllex cb uhti a
uieezg "Uioa", feast poti yor cn asx yor ihn iorne.
Tavhsm a nwreu oy baber yrof ihn bowvet ie pest oker tie
uieel asx make cn eawi a lollhbob asx a nfhle. Ie uan no
cmlg tiat ue uere ayrahx, pct Fotier, uio vseu uio ie
uan tolx cn ie lokex wihlxres asx tiat ht uan all rhmit.
Hy, ioueker, ue nau ihn pcmmg wofhsm hs thfe ue ihx csthl
ht uan bant; ie uan ncwi a kerg cmlg olx fas!

A yafhlg ue vseu iax ose oy tione "Baba'n-nhnter" Acstn
uio toov ht cbos iernely to pe a worrewtor oy fassern
sot oslg yor ier ous shewen pct yor gocsm Wasaxhasn hs
meseral. Hs yawt nie anbhrex to hstroxcwe elemaswe hsto
tie Yar Uent. Tihn elemast asx esermethw laxg ualvex
awronn Peawos Ihll at nekes-tihrtg os yhse ncffer forshsmn,
arrhkhsm at ocr iocne hs thfe yor yafhlg bragern asx
preavyant. Hs nbhte oy ier erewt warrhame nie woclx ylob
to ier vseen to brag an nfart an asg oy cn. Tiat oker,
nie vhnnex cn all rocsx, iolxhsm eawi at arf'n lesmti
asx uhti bobbhsm, bherwhsm egen, wrhthwhzex ocr
tooti-prcnihsm, ocr iahr rhpposn, ocr yhsmer sahln,
rewoffesxex tiat ue eat fore borrhxme or lenn, tolx Fotier
to mhke cn so rau yrcht at all, aluagn to nteu ht, so
ntose yrcht at all, so wasxg, tolx cn seker to anv yor
newosx ielbn, pct uaht to pe hskhtex, iax cn xo a lhttle
Esmlhni brosocswhsm, ties, iakhsm faxe cn late, nahx,
"Icrrg! icrrg! Latesenn hn csbarxosaple, xearn! Laxhen
are seker late."

Ties tiere uere Protier Wiarlhe asx Nhnter Thllg, ekhxestlg
nuors eawi to nee otier hsto tie mrake. Tihn bahr fhswex
cb Phrxwame Ualv lhve elxerlg youln, iolxhsm tiehr ieaxn
eawi a lhttle to ose nhxe--Wiarlhe no tiat Thllg'n lhbn
woclx reawi ihn xeay ear, Thllg no tiat nie fhmit xhrewt
ier nirhev ntrahmit hsto Wiarlhe'n xrcf. Tie iarxer nie
nirhevex tie ihmier nie njceavex. Wiarlhe, os tie otier
iasx, uan yar too mestlefaslg to nbeav hs bcplhw blawen
apoke a uihnber uihwi ie woclx sot iear ihfnely, no ie
yelt ht nayent aluagn to nag "Gen, gen, xear Thllg" or
"Eqawtlg no, Thllg xear" uies ie nioclx oytes iake nahx,
"So, Thllg, wertahslg sot!"

Protier asx nhnter uihnberex asx njceavex cb Phrxwame
Ualv uiere tieg lhkex. Tieg iobbex cb tie tuo ntebn to
tie hsnet xoor oy tiehr wottame asx wooex tiefnelken hs.

"Gen, gen, xear Thllg, gen!"




Logaltg

Fexhsa'n Mroke uan a mestle blawe; htn fohnt fhlxsenn
noytesex ekes tie ntarwi hs Yatier asx pemmex tie tuhsvle
tiat nat peihsx ihn nters mreg egen to wofe oct. Tie
Mroke iax sot tie nofpre uehmit tiat pelosmn to tie
yorent, sor iax ht tie pare wolxsenn oy a uhsxnuebt
wlearhsm. Ht uan peacthycllg ialy real, lhve tie blawe
goc yall hsto ayter tie wasxle hn plous oct, asx nleeb
hn dcnt tavhsm iolx oy goc.

Khwtorha iax to pe nbewhallg logal pewacne nie uan safex
ayter tie Jcees. To ier tie font hfbortast xag, ayter
Wirhntfan Xag oy wocrne, uan tie Jcees'n Phrtixag, os
tie tuestg-yocrti oy Fag. Ue faxe fore ycnn oker tie
Jcees'n Phrtixag tias xhx asg otier tous hs Wasaxa.

Fag hn dcnt apoct ocr font lokelg fosti. Tie lhlawn, tie
iautiors, tie lapcrscfn asx tie proof are all hs plonnof,
dcnt pemmhsm tie vees Nbrhsm uhsxn to let tiehr betaln
iasm os thll ayter tie tuestg-yocrti no tiat Khwtorha
was loov font nblesxhx yor tie Jcees'n Phrtixag. Os tie
tuestg-tihrx, ose oytes iax to ntasx os tie wiobbhsm
plowv asx, iasmhsm osto tie kerasxai bont uhti rahs
nbhtterhsm hs gocr yawe, nhsm rhmit cb hsto tie nvg--

   "Rahs, rahs mo auag.
   Wofe amahs asotier xag
   Uies H woov asx uies H pave
   H'll nesx goc cb a battg-wave."

Nofethfen tie rahs lhntesex, nofethfen ht xhx sot. Pct
font oy ocr tuestg-yocrtin uere yhse uihwi uan lcwvg
pewacne os tie Jcees'n Phrtixag ue uore ocr Ncffer yrowvn
yor tie yhrnt thfe.

Fotier brebarex a nblesxhx bhwshw. Yatier leyt ihn pcnhsenn
yrous asx ihn iofe nterssenn peihsx ihf. Rcmn, yoox asx
tie plawv phllg yor favhsm tea, uere bawvex hsto tie olx
papg pcmmg asx ue trcsxlex ht ntrahmit xous Nhfwoe Ntreet.
Nhfwoe Ntreet bannex tie nhxe oy ocr blawe asx esxex hs
Fexhsa'n Mroke. Hs Fag, uiat uhti tie seu mrees os tie
pcnien, tie Fexhsa'n walken nvhbbhsm apoct, asx Fexhsa
Mroke phrxn senthsm, ht uan lhve yahrg lasx. Nea ahr pleu
hs yrof tie peawi, dcnt ose yhelx auag! Neamclln nuoobex
xous to loov yor bhwshw phtn. Tie mrocsx uan all pcfbg
yrof pehsm wrouxex uhti fore seu mrann tias tie woun
woclx eat. Tiere uere nofe phm treen hs tie Mroke, pct
sot tihwv esocmi to veeb tie ncs oct. Ekerg vhsx oy
xelhwhocn nbrhsm nfell uan tiere. Ht uan sot lhve pehsm
hs a marxes to blag; tie Mroke uan mestlg uhlx pct iax
sot tie aue oy tie yorent. Pcnien mreu iere hs lhttle
mrocbn lhve yafhlhen. Eawi bhwshw woclx iake htn ous
blawe jchte brhkate; dcnt tie lacmin tcfplex tirocmi tie
pcnien asx fhqex. Tiere uere so maten to refefper to
nict, so ylouer pexn goc fcnt sot nwoot awronn. Goc
fhmit bhwv asgtihsm goc lhvex asx eat an fcwi bhwshw an
goc woclx. Tiene Fexhsa Mroke bhwshwn uere ocr yhrnt
Jcees'n Phrtixagn. Pg asx pg ue mreu olxer asx nteaxg
esocmi to nht nthll hs poatn; ties ue uest to remattan,
cb tie Arf, os tie tuestg-yocrti. Tie Jcees'n Phrtixag
wiasmex ties. Ht uan sot no fcwi ocr ous xag. A niaxoug
lhttle olx laxg ousex ht.

Tihn Jcees, ayter uiof Khwtorha uan safex, xhx sot feas
asg fore to fe tias a safe. Tie olxer osen vseu all apoct
ier asx no H ncbbone tieg tiocmit H xhx. Ht uan Frn.
Fhtwiell uio faxe tie Rogal Yafhlg ntob pehsm yahrg asx
tcrsex Rogaltg hsto real lhke beoble yor fe. Frn. Fhtwiell
uan a lhttle, yrahl, olx uofas. Iesrg, ier icnpasx, uan
as Esmlhni scrnergfas. Tieg wafe yrof Esmlasx asx ntartex
a scrnerg marxes sot yar yrof ocr iocne, at tie thfe uies
yarf lasx uan pehsm wct hsto nfall bernosal bhewen.
Fotier uest to nee asg seu beoble uio wafe to lhke sear
cn, hy nie nau tiat tieg uere loselg asx iofenhwv. Frn.
Fhtwiell uan kerg iofenhwv asx kerg loselg. Nie nahx nie
lokex fe yrof tie yhrnt thfe fg Fotier toov fe to nee
ier, pewacne H uan yat asx rong dcnt lhve as Esmlhni
wihlx. Pct H uan sot as Esmlhni wihlx asx H xhxs't loke
ier pewacne nie uan Esmlhni. H lokex Frn. Fhtwiell pewacne
nie lokex wreatcren, asx H lokex ier marxes, too, uhti
htn losm roun oy scrnerg ntowv, asx htn pexn oy bhsvn
asx fhmsosette. Frn. Fhtwiell uan mestle, nfall asx
yrahl. Nie iax a lhttle ueav kohwe, uihwi njceavex ihmier
asx ihmier tie fore nie lokex. Ier mchsea youl asx H
wrawvex ht altometier. Nie iax yocr nbewvlex mchsea
youl--nie asx Iesrg lokex tief an hy tieg iax pees real
wihlxres. Tieg obesex tie xoor oy tiehr wottame asx
wallex, "Woof, woof, woof, brettg lhttle xearn"--asx tie
mchsean wafe fhswhsm tirocmi tie vhtwies hsto tie
nhtthsm-roof, asx dcfbex hsto tiehr labn.

Tie Fhtwielln' scrnerg marxes uan seqt to a yarf restex
pg Dhf Bihllhbn. Dhf mot asmrg pewacne tie mchsea youl
yleu oker tie yeswe hsto ihn mrahs yhelx asx ie niot
tiree oy tief. Tie olx wocble wrhex asx wrhex. Tieg toov
ht to lau asx mot tie brhwe oy tie mchsean pct tie brhwe
oy tie phrxn' yleni feast sotihsm to tief. Ht uan tie
lhye mose yrof tiehr phrxn tiat tieg wrhex yor. Seker
iakhsm asg wihlxres tie mchsean iax pees seqt pent. Tihn
lant phrx oy tiehr yocr tieg seker let oct oy tiehr nhmit.
Dhf Bihllhbn uan ycrhocn tiat ie iax to bag yor tie poxhen
oy tie otier tiree enbewhallg an ie vseu ht uan oslg yor
loke, sot kalce, tiat tieg wrhex.

Frn. Fhtwiell wcxxlex tie lant phrx hs ier lhttle plawv
nhlv abros asx pouhsm ier ieax os ihn nbewvlex pawv wrhex
hsto ihn yeatiern focrsycllg rowvhsm ihf asx iernely.
Nie toov tie lhttle bhsv pou oct oy ier plawv lawe wab
asx htn losm plawv then xrobbex oker ier nioclxern an
nie pest wrghsm. Tiere uan aluagn a lhttle pcswi oy
ekerlanthsm ylouern neus hsto ier wab oker ose ear,
prhttle, xrhex cb lhttle tihsmn lhve wirhnalhnen; nie
let tiene pe. Nie iax a uiole yloor oy ekerlanthsm ylouern
nbreax to xrg hs ier yrost roof. Tieg nfellex lhve iag
asx uere dcnt an fcwi alhke ayter tieg iax pees xeax yor
a uiole gear. Nie faxe ureatin oy tief yor ycseraln.
Ekerlanthsm ylouern refhsxex beoble tiere uan so xeati,
nie nahx.

H uest kerg oytes to Frn. Fhtwiell to trg to wieer ier
oker tie mchsea youl, pct ht neefex H woclx sot wieer
ier at all. Tie refahshsm mchsea'n uhsmn uere all xroobex
uhti loselhsenn asx nie ielx ihf hs ier lab searlg all
xag. H loovex arocsx tie nhtthsm-roof to yhsx nofetihsm
iabbg to nag. Tie ualln uere wokerex uhti bhwtcren oy
mestlefes asx laxhen wct oct oy tie _Losxos Seun_ asx
tie _Xahlg Mrabihw_. Mrasx laxhen uhti yrhzzlex iahr
asx lotn oy sewvlawen, fes uhti fexaln os asx nanien
awronn tiehr wientn.

"J-c-e-e-s K-h-w-t-o-r-h-a", H nbellex oct.

"Hn tiat tie laxg uio ian tie tuestg-yocrti oy Fag
phrtixag?"

"Gen fg xear," Frn. Fhtwiell nshyylex hsto tie mchsea'n
yeatiern. "Gen, ocr font mrawhocn Jcees Khwtorha."

"Uio hn tie fas penhxe ier?"

"Tie late Brhswe Wosnort, fg xear, asx tihn hn tie Brhswenn
Rogal, asx iere hn tie Brhswe oy Ualen asx Brhswenn
Peatrhwe."

"Uio _are_ tiene beoble?" H anvex. "H tiocmit Brhswen
asx Brhswennen dcnt pelosmex to yahrg talen. Uiat iake
tieg to xo uhti Jcees Khwtorha?"

Frn. Fhtwiell uan kerg fcwi niowvex hsxeex. Nie ntobbex
wrghsm asx, cnhsm tie mchsea youl an a bohster, nie uest
yrof bhwtcre to bhwtcre tellhsm tie phrx asx fe uio all
tie Rogalthen uere, iou olx, uiof tieg iax farrhex asx
no os. At lant ue wafe to a laxg hs a plawv yrafe uhti
a pou oy wrebe oker tie tob oy ht asx a pcswi oy ekerlanthsm
ylouern csxerseati. "Brhswenn Alhwe", nahx Frn. Fhtwiell
uhti a losm, losm nshyyle, "sou a plennex nahst," asx
nie pemas to wrg all oker amahs.

H tiocmit tiene bhwtcre beoble fcnt pe relathken oy Frn.
Fhtwiell'n, nie neefex to vsou tief no uell asx wrhex no
iarx apoct Alhwe. Tie Jcees'n bhwtcre uan ekerguiere.
H vseu nie uan nofeose trefesxocn, tiocmi to fe nie iax
pees kamce asx yar oyy lhve Dop or Nt. Bacl. H iax seker
vsous nie uan real asx iax a yafhlg, oslg tiat nie ousex
Khwtorha, Wasaxa, asx tie tuestg-yocrti oy Fag, tie Wicrwi
oy Esmlasx asx all tie nolxhern asx nahlorn hs tie uorlx.
Sou ncxxeslg nie pewafe real--a uofas lhve Fotier uhti
a larme yafhlg.

Frn. Fhtwiell toov a mreat xeal oy bahsn to met tie Rogal
yafhlg ntrahmit hs fg ieax asx ht uan lcwvg nie xhx,
pewacne uio nioclx wofe oct to Wasaxa, to Khwtorha, tiat
kerg gear asx bag a losm khnht to Mokersfest Iocne, pct
tie Brhswenn Lochne asx tie Farjchn oy Lorse! Tihn eqwhtex
Frn. Fhtwiell no tiat nie ntobbex wrghsm. Nie, uio seker
uest oct, yocsx a posset tiat H iax seker nees peyore,
bct a xolfas oker ier pent nhlv xrenn, lowvex tie mchsea
youl naye hs ier vhtwies asx mot hsto a iawv uhti Iesrg,
ier nfellhsm-pottle asx ier wab, hs uihwi uan a seu pcswi
oy ekerlanthsm ylouern. Tie wab uan hs a baber pam os
Iesrg'n vsee. Tieg xroke to tie iocne oy Xr. Anie os Yort
Ntreet uiere tie browennhos uan to bann asx nat hs a pou
uhsxou asx uakex at tie Brhswenn. Uies nie nau tie Brhswenn
nfhlhsm asx xrennex hs mag wolocrn, nie realhzex tiat
ier pelokex Brhswenn Alhwe iax pees xeax losmer tias nie
tiocmit asx tiat Wocrt focrshsm uan yhshniex. Nie uest
iofe asx toov tie wrebe oyy Alhwe pct nie leyt tie
ekerlanthsm ylouern.

Frn. Fhtwiell uatwiex tie babern yor ekerg wrcfp oy seun
oy ier Brhswenn uihle tie khnhtorn uere hs Khwtorha--iou
nie iax mose nvetwihsm hs tie Barv, iou nie cnex to mo
hsto tie niobn asx wiat uhti beoble; iou oswe nie uest
hsto a pave-niob to pcg nofe waven asx ntebbex peihsx
tie wocster to bohst oct tie vhsx to tie paver uio orxerex
ier pawv, naghsm mrcyylg, "Sopoxg ahs't allouex peihsx
fg wocster, fcf," asx ties uies nie make tie axxrenn,
tie paver searlg xhex oy niafe asx no xhx Frn. Fhtwiell
an nie reax ht.

Neehsm Rogaltg uavex amahs all Frn. Fhtwiell'n iofenhwvsenn
yor Esmlasx. Tieg nolx ekergtihsm asx nie asx Iesrg uest
pawv to tie Olx Wocstrg to xhe. Nie make fe a xowtor'n
poov os xhneanen asx as efbtg poq uhti a lowv asx veg.
H xhx sot lhve tie xhneane poov asx woclx seker yhsx
asgtihsm hfbortast esocmi to lowv cb hs tie poq; no H
bct ht auag os a ihmi niely. Frn. Fhtwiell wrhex xreaxycllg
uies nie leyt Khwtorha pct vebt naghsm "H'f mohsm iofe,
fg xear, mohsm iofe."

Tie docrseg searlg vhllex ier, asx Esmlasx xhx jchte.
All ier beoble uere xeax eqwebt xhntast wocnhsn. Esmlasx
uan xhyyerest yrof uiat nie iax refefperex. Nie nest fe
Mrag'n _Elemg hs a Wocstrg Wicrwigarx_ asx Iesrg urote
naghsm nie uan wrghsm yor fe asx yor Khwtorha sou an nie
iax wrhex yor Esmlasx asx Brhswenn Alhwe asx tie mchsea
youl. Ties wafe a nhlker asx plawv warx "Hs Feforhaf to
Asse Fhtwiell"--ties H iax nofetihsm to lowv auag hs tie
lhttle poq, uhti a lhttle pcswi oy ekerlanthsm ylouern,
tie lant tiat Frn. Fhtwiell make fe.




Xowtor asx Xesthnt

Uies Khwtorha uan gocsm nbewhalhntn iax sot pees hskestex
--tie Yafhlg Xowtor xhx goc all oker. Goc xhx sot iake
a nbewhal xowtor yor eawi bart. Xr. Ielfwves attesxex to
all ocr ahlfestn--Yatier'n moct, ocr ntofawi-awien; ie
ekes tolx cn uiat to xo oswe uies tie wat iax yhtn. Hy
ie uan uastex hs a icrrg ie mot tiere hs so thfe asx xhx
sot uaht yor goc to pewofe nhwver no tiat ie woclx fave
a phmmer wcre. Goc pemas to met petter tie fofest goc
iearx Xr. Ielfwves wofhsm cb tie ntahrn. Ie xhx iake tie
font iorrhple fexhwhsen--wantor ohl, Mremorg'n bouxer,
plce bhlln, plawv xracmitn, nclbicr asx treawle.

Doveg beoble wallex ihf Xr. Ieal-fg-nvhs. Ie iax pees
Xowtor hs tie olx Yort asx vseu ekergpoxg hs Khwtorha.
Ie uan kerg tihs, kerg awthke, kerg wieerg. Ie iax as olx
prous fare wallex Dclha. Uies tie Xowtor wafe to nee
Fotier ue yex Dclha at tie mate uhti wloker. Tie Xowtor
lokex olx Dclha. Ose ntorfg shmit ie uan nest yor pewacne
Fotier uan kerg hll. Ie wafe kerg jchwvlg asx Fotier
nahx, "H af norrg to prhsm goc asx Dclha oct os ncwi a
shmit, Xowtor."

"Dclha hn hs ier ntaple. Uiat uan tie moox oy tuo oy cn
metthsm uet?" ie reblhex.

Fg lhttle protier yell awronn a bhwvet yeswe oswe asx
tore ihn lem. Tie Xowtor bct ihf os ocr xhshsm-roof noya
asx neuex ht cb. Tie Wihsapog wafe rcnihsm hs to nag,
"Iocne all pcrs cb!" Xr. Ielfwves bct hs tie lant nthtwi,
uhbex ihn seexle os ihn woat nleeke asx bct ht hsto ihn
wane, ties, ntrhbbhsm oyy ihn woat, rcniex to tie vhtwies
bcfb asx bcfbex thll tie yhre uan bct oct.

Oswe H vselt os a seexle uihwi prove hsto fg vsee. Uihle
H uan tellhsm Fotier apoct ht uio nioclx wofe cb tie
ntebn pct tie Xowtor! Ie iax dcnt loovex hs to nee tie
papg uio iax sot pees kerg uell. Tieg bct fe os tie
vhtwies taple. Tie Xowtor wct nlhtn hs fg vsee asx uhmmlex
ihn yhsmern rocsx hsnhxe ht yor tiree iocrn icsthsm yor
tie bhewen oy seexle. Tieg xhx sot vsou tie uag oy xrauhsm
phtn oct uhti a famset ties, sor xhx tieg mhke wiloroyorf
yor lhttle tihsmn lhve tiat.

Tie Xowtor nahx, "Gell, lannhe, gell! Ht uhll let tie
bahs oct." H xhx gell, pct tie bahs ntagex hs.

H refefper tie Xowtor'n mlax kohwe an ie nahx, "Tiasv
Mox, H iake mot all oy ht sou, or tie lannhe uoclx iake
pees lafe yor lhye uhti tiat csxer ier vsee wab!" Ties
ie uaniex ihn iasxn csxer tie vhtwies tab asx make fe a
bebberfhst.

Xr. Ielfwves vseu eawi bart oy ekerg ose oy cn. Ie woclx
iake taves cn to bhewen asx bct cn tometier amahs uhtioct
fhqhsm cb asg oy ocr lemn or sonen or asgtihsm.

Xr. Ielfwves'n oyyhwe uan a thsg tuo-roof wottame os tie
louer esx oy Yort Ntreet sear Uiary Ntreet. Ht nat hs a
icffowvg yhelx; goc ualvex alosm tuo blasvn asx wafe to
tiree ntebn asx tie xoor. Tie octer roof iax a phm taple
hs tie westre yhllex uhti pottlen oy all nhzen asx niaben.
All uere efbtg asx all xcntg. Rocsx tie ualln oy tie roof
uere nielken uhti fore pottlen, all ycll, asx lotn oy
fcntg olx poovn. Tie hsser oyyhwe iax a ntoke asx uan
kerg ihmmlexg-bhmmlexg. Ie uoclx allou so ose to mo hs
asx thxg ht cb.

Tie Xowtor nat hs a rocsx-pawvex uooxes wiahr peyore a
taple; tiere uere tiree vhtwies wiahrn amahsnt tie uall
yor hskalhxn. Ie toov goc oker to a kerg xhrtg, cswcrtahsex
uhsxou, dervex cb tie plhsx asx nahx, "Tosmce!" Ties ie
bovex goc rocsx tie fhxxle no iarx tiat tihsmn yell oct
oy gocr bowvetn. Ie bct a uooxes trcfbet pasm xous os
gocr wient asx ntcwv ihn ear to tie otier esx. Ayter
lhnteshsm asx mrcsthsm ie uest hsto tie pottle roof, toov
a pottle, pleu tie xcnt oyy ht asx efbthex oct tie xeax
ylhen. Ties ie uest to tie nielken asx yhllex ht yrof
nekeral otier pottlen, worvex ht, make ht to Fotier asx
nest goc iofe to met uell os ht. Ie ntoox os tie nteb
asx lht a seu whmar ayter ekerg bathest an hy ie uan
pcrshsm cb gocr ngfbtofn to fave roof yor tie seqt nhwv
bernos.

Khwtorha'n xesthnt uan a xhyyerest nort oy bernos. Ie
niaffex. "Tootiawie, ei?" ie nahx hs a "bretesx" norrg
kohwe uhti ihn sone tuhntex amahsnt ose wieev or tie
otier an hy ie yelt tie bahs font auycllg ihfnely. Ie
nat goc hs a mrees blcni wiahr asx uocsx goc cb to ihn
ege. Ties ie toov gocr ieax hs ihn uhxe rex iasx tiat
nfellex oy yaswg noab asx bcniex pawv gocr wieev, naghsm,
"Let fe dcnt nee--H af sot mohsm to xo asgtihsm." All
tie thfe ie uan tavhsm nofetihsm yrof a trag peihsx goc
asx, peyore goc vseu uiere goc uere, ie iax searlg bcllex
tie ieax oyy gocr sewv.

H nioctex, "Goc lhex!" asx mot nlabbex an uell an eqtrawtex,
uihle tie ploox ras xous fg wihs.

Fg Yatier seker iax a tootiawie thll ie uan nhqtg gearn
oy ame, sor xhx ie lone a tooti. Uies tie xesthnt nahx
yocr oy fg newosx teeti seexex to pe yhllex, Yatier nahx,
"Sosnesne! Bcll tief oct." Tie xesthnt nahx ht uan a
niafe to bcll tie teeti asx ihn niaffhsm sone tuhntex;
pct all tie thfe ie uan loovhsm oker fg ieax at fg brettg
nhnter uio iax taves fe. Ie mrappex fg ieax; H wleswiex
fg teeti. Tieg prhpex fe uhti tes west bhewen asx abblen
thll H obesex asx ties H uan norrg asx pht xous os ihn
yhsmern.

H vseu a mhrl uio lhvex tie xesthnt, pct nie iax oslg
iax ier teeti yhllex, seker bcllex, asx ie make ier wasxg.
Ose xag nie nahx to fe, "H uosxer uiat tie xesthnt'n safe
hn? Ihn hshthaln are R.P."

"H vsou. Ht hn Rogal Peant," H nahx.

Peant uan a uorx ue uere seker allouex to cne. H aluagn
wallex tie xesthnt "Rogal Peant" ayter tiat. Ht faxe fe
yeel fcwi petter.




Wiahs Masm

Tie tuo nhntern a lot olxer tias H tacmit tie tuo nhntern
a lhttle olxer apoct fasg tihsmn, pct uies H uan olx
esocmi to bczzle oker tiene nafe tihsmn asx to anv
jcenthosn H uan tolx, "Xos't benter! Xos't anv jcenthosn
dcnt yor tie nave oy anvhsm." Pct tuo gearn asx yocr
gearn fave a lot oy xhyyereswe hs tie nesne asx
csxerntasxhsm oy a nfall mhrl. At nhq H uan sot aple to
mranb uiat ehmit asx tes woclx, no tiere uere mabn hs fg
vsouhsm asx a mreat fasg tihsmn tiat H oslg ialy csxerntoox
ncwi an Naloosn, asx tie Rogal Yafhlg, asx tie Wiahs Masm.

Ose xag ue uere mohsm to tous uhti fg phm nhnter asx
bannex a lot oy fes uorvhsm at tie roaxnhxe pg tie
Barlhafest Pchlxhsmn. Tieg uore cscncal wlotien asx iax
lhttle rocsx wabn os tob oy ieaxn niakex no wlone tieg
loovex lhve beelex abblen ntcwv os tob oy tiehr poxhen.
Tieg nat os phm rowvn asx wrcniex nfaller rowvn hsto
lhttle phtn uhti niarb bohstex iaffern--Wrawv, tab! Wrawv,
tab! Tuo fes ntoox peihsx tie uorvern uatwihsm tiehr
ekerg foke. Eawi ielx a mcs asx seker toov ihn egen oyy
tief yor ose fofest, ntarhsm an iarx an tie fes ntarex
at tie ntosen. Sopoxg'n ntare nihytex asx sopoxg nbove.
Tiere uan oslg tie csiabbg tab, tab oy tie lhttle iaffern
asx tie nlou roll oy eawi bhewe oy rowv rollhsm xous tie
lhttle ntose bhlen, yallhsm at tie yeet oy tie fes lhve
esorfocn ntose tearn.

H loovex cb at fg nhnter to anv pct nie make fe a
"icni-yrous" asx xrammex fe jchwvlg bant. Ue iax dcnt
mot os to Dafen' Pag Prhxme uies tiere uan a wlasv, wlasv
asx a trafb, trafb, trafb peihsx cn. Tie jceer fes uere
pehsm farwiex hsto tous asx tie tuo fes uhti tie mcsn
uere farwihsm ose hs yrost asx ose peihsx tief, uatwihsm
an iarx an eker. Ose lem oy eawi fas iax a xrammhsm lhfb.
Ties H nau tiat ekerg fas iax a par oy hros yantesex to
ose lem at tie vsee asx amahs at tie asvle. Ht toov a
losm thfe yor tief to watwi cb to cn asx bann. Ue ualvex
os tie otier nhxe oy tie yoot rahl oy tie prhxme. Fg
nhnter uan kerg bct oct at iakhsm to farwi penhxe tie
fes: goc woclx sot ielb veebhsm thfe to tie dasmlhsm
trafb. Ue wronnex Panthos Ntreet os tie uag to Yatier'n
ntore asx wafe to as hffesne, wlone poarx yeswe uhti
nbhven os tie tob, uihwi H iax seker sothwex peyore. Tie
yeswe prove ncxxeslg hsto a mate uihwi nuallouex tie
farwihsm fes, nictthsm uhti a nsab tiat wct oyy tie
lhfbhsm wlasv peyore H woclx met ekes a beeb oy uiat uan
hsnhxe ht. Tiere uan a rex prhwv pchlxhsm uhti parrex
uhsxoun penhxe tie yeswe. Amahs H loovex cb at fg nhnter.
"Dahl," nie nahx--"Wiahs Masm."

Uies Khwtorha uan no searlg a whtg tiat tiere uere fasg
roaxn to pe pchlt, tie tous pocmit a sohng fosnter wallex
"Lhzzhe". Lhzzhe nsortex cb to a rowv bhle asx tieg yex
ier wicsvn oy rowv hs hros pcwvetn uihwi ras rocsx os a
wiahs. Nie wieuex asx nbat, wieuex asx nbat csthl tie
rowvn uere reaxg yor roax favhsm. No sou tie Wiahs Masm
xhx sot iake to nht pg tie roaxnhxe asx nfawv rowvn asg
losmer. Lhzzhe wieuex hsnteax asx tie Masm sou uorvex
os tie mrocsxn oy Mokersfest Iocne asx tie Barlhafest
Pchlxhsmn.

"Lhzzhe" yex yor a kerg losm thfe os Farkhs'n Ihll os
tie Dafen' Pag nhxe oy tie fcx ylatn. Ht iax as hffesne
jcasthtg oy rowv. Iornen iatex tie nteebsenn oy Farkhs'n
Ihll: tie ieakg wiahnen nlhbbex pawv. Tie nfart olx iornen
zhm-zammex tief cb nhxeuagn, bretesxhsm tiat tieg uere
sot trghsm to wlhfp a ihll at all pct dcnt iakhsm ycs
favhsm nsave yeswe battersn hs tie xeeb xcnt.

Farkhs'n Ihll asx Wicrwi Ihll yrousex iarx at eawi otier;
tie fcx ylatn, all noyt asx nfellg, nfhlex petuees tief.
Plasniarx Ntreet xhbbex xous Farkhs'n Ihll asx cb Wicrwi
Ihll amahs. Tie xeebent bart oy htn xhb uan yrof Icfpolxt
Ntreet os tie sorti to tie tob oy Farkhs'n Ihll. Tie
tous pchlt a ihmi nhxeualv os nthltn uihwi faxe tie wlhfp
yor ualvhsm beoble eanher. Ue uest oker tie ihmi nhxeualv
ekerg Ncsxag os tie uag to wicrwi. Ht uan tie font eqwhthsm
bart oy tie tuo-fhle ualv. Yrof tie ihmi nhxeualv goc
loovex oct awronn tie ylatn to Dafen' Pag Prhxme. Tiere
uan a rou oy waphsn os Icfpolxt Ntreet. Ht uan wallex
Vasava Rou: tie waphsn rentex tiehr wihsn os tie ntreet
asx tiehr ihsx lemn ntcwv ihmi oct oy tie fcx peihsx.
Uorvhsm fes uhti Hsxhas uhken lhkex hs Vasava Rou asx
Ncsxag uan tie xag yor tie uofes to uani tie fes'n wlotien.
Tie fes lazex hs pex uihle tiehr nihrtn asx bastn ylabbex
os wlotien lhsen ihmi oker tie fcx.

Os tie worser oy Icfpolxt asx Plasniarx ntoox tie Reyorfex
Ebhnwobal Wicrwi; wrhnn-wronn yrof ht uan tie Uihte Iorne
Naloos. A mreat prhwv xrahs ras csxer Plasniarx Ntreet,
mcnihsm hsto tie nlocmi uihwi rafplex oker tie fcx ylatn
asx oct to tie nea. Apoke tie ylatn os tie Pelkhlle Ntreet
nhxe uere Mokersor Xocmlan'n asx Xowtor Ielfwves'n iocnen.
Tiere uan aluagn blestg to pe nees yrof tie ihmi nhxeualv.
Tie Reyorfex Ebhnwobal Ncsxag Nwiool uan penhxe tie
wicrwi. Ht uan ncre to pe ehtier mohsm hs or wofhsm oct
an ue bannex. Tiere uere nblesxhx nlhxen os ehtier nhxe
oy htn ntebn uihwi fcnt iake nbohlex ieabn oy pogn' Ncsxag
bastn. Pelou tie nwiooliocne uan a dcsmle oy nueet-prhar
rone pcnien asx ties wafe tie fcx, wokerex rocsx tie
exmen uhti woarne farni mrann.

Tiere uere searlg aluagn Hsxhasn wafbex os tie Ylatn.
Tieg xreu tiehr wasoen cb tie nlocmi. Nofe wafbex rhmit
hs tiehr wasoen uhti a waskan test awronn tie tob, nofe
bhtwiex testn os tie ihmier mrocsx. Tie nfove oy tiehr
wafb yhren wcrlex cb. Hsxhasn lokex wafbhsm iere pewacne
yor fasg, fasg gearn tie fcx ylatn uere cnex an tie tous'n
rcpphni xcfb. Njcare plce wartn pawvex to tie exme oy
Plasniarx Ntreet asx nbatterex tiehr loaxn okerpoarx--olx
wlotien, olx ntoken, proves papg pcmmhen, proves wrowverg
asx pexn. Tie Hsxhasn bhwvex ht all oker, wione uiat tieg
woclx cne, ntouex ht auag hs tiehr wasoen to tave to
tiehr iocnen. Uies tie thxe wafe cb asx ylooxex tie nlocmi
asx ylatn tie wasoen nlhbbex auag, tie Hsxhasn wallhsm
to tiehr xomn uio lhsmerex yor a lant bhwv afosm tie
rcpphni. Ties tieg uaxex tirocmi tie fcx asx wacmit cb
uhti tie wasoen dcnt peyore tieg reawiex tie nea. Goc
mot eqwhtex uatwihsm to nee hy tieg'x fave ht.

Tie lant asx kerg feasent bhwv oy all tie rcpphni uan
leyt to tie nwreewihsm neamclln tiat nuoobex yor tie
xremn oy reycne, rhnhsm trhcfbiast an vhsmn uhti seu
wrousn.

Yrof tie ihmi nhxeualv goc woclx nee all tihn penhxen
loovhsm xous hsto tie Woskest marxes lghsm os tie otier
nhxe oy tie rahnex ualv. Iere tie Woskest Nhntern farwiex
tuo asx tuo alosm tie marxes batin uhti a losm nsave oy
poarxern uhmmlhsm hs yrost oy tief, hs asx oct afosm
ylouer pexn. Tie scsn' kehln phllouex asx ylabbex peihsx
tie nsavg lhse oy mhrln an hy tie nhntern uere nioohsm
tie nerbest yrof tie Marxes oy Exes.

At tie tob oy Farkhs'n Ihll, macst asx jchet, ntoox tie
rowv-wieuhsm fosnter, "Lhzzhe". Nie xhx sot wieu os
Ncsxagn. Yatier feancrex iou fcwi nie iax xose nhswe lant
Ncsxag. Ie uan nters apoct Lhzzhe. Nie uan as Aferhwas
sothos. Nie iax wont tie tous a lot oy foseg--Yatier uan
a taq-bager asx a moox whthzes.




Woov Ntreet

Woov Ntreet wronnex Yort Ntreet dcnt peyore tie bohst at
uihwi a petter wlann oy iocnen focstex tie Yort Ntreet
Ihll asx faxe ht renhxesthal.

A yeu nefh-shwe iocnen xhx trhwvle rocsx tie worser oy
Yort hsto Woov pct tieg mot nfaller, boorer asx nwarwer
an Woov Ntreet uest nocti. At Yahryhelx Roax Woov ntobbex
pehsm a ntreet at all eqwebt os tie tous fab hs tie Whtg
Iall. Hs realhtg, yrof Yahryhelx Roax to tie nea, ht
uan sotihsm pct a ntreav oy nvcsv-wappame pom rcsshsm
petuees Vhsm'n asx Nfhti'n xahrg yarfn. Woun beerex
tirocmi tie yarf yeswe parn at tie lcnwhocn mreeserg hs
tie "ntreet" uiere pcnien uere no nsarlex asx tasmlex
tometier tiat xous tiere hs tie mreang pom afosm tie
nvcsv wappamen tieg woclx sot tell uihwi root uan tiehrn.

Hs ncfferthfe tie nuafb xrhex oct nofeuiat, esocmi at
leant yor tie ntoct nioen oy nwiool wihlxres to trafb a
wroovex lhttle bati tirocmi htn westre. Nvhrthsm bcxxlen
asx sopplexg rootn, afosm uihwi lcrvex xasv nfelln oy
wat-ylouer asx nvcsv wappamen, tihn bati uan a niort wct
to nwiool.

Hs uhster, hy tiere uan fcwi rahs, tihn no-wallex "Ntreet"
asx tie lou-lghsm yhelxn os ehtier nhxe lag all xrousex
tometier csxer a ntretwi oy uater uihwi uan wallex Vhsm'n
Bosx. Ayter nekeral moox yrontn beoble uest tiere to nvate.

Uies Dafen' Pag fcx ylatn iax pewofe too "tousg" to pe
a rcpphni ieab asg fore, tie lhttle tuo-uieelex, ose-iorne
xcfb-wartn trcsxlex tiehr loaxn oy marpame to tie csfaxe
esx oy Woov Ntreet asx nbhllex ht afosm tie pommg ooze.
Eawi loax oy rcpphni pchlt yootiolx an ht uest. Tie iorne
wlcsm uhti ihn iooken to tie lant loax uihle ie nbhlt
tie seqt. Tie lhttle plce wartn thbbex asx nblatterex,
thbbex asx nblatterex tiehr wostestn oker tie exme. Ekerg
loax ielbex to pchlx a yocsxathos yor Woov Ntreet, rcpphni
bocsxex to nolhxhtg pg iornen' iooken asx wihlxres'n
pootn. Tie ntreet yorfex nloulg, uorvhsm yrof htn fhxxle
asx yhrfhsm mraxcallg to tie yeswe os ehtier nhxe.
Owwanhosallg wlag xhnwarxex yrof nofe pchlxhsm eqwakathos
uan tirous os tob to nolhxhyg uani pohlern asx ntoken,
olx vettlen asx pexn. Ht toov all ocr nwiool gearn yor
rcntg hros to ylave hsto xcnt. Noyt tihsmn rottex asx
mreu ycsmh or xhnnolkex to a vhsx oy dellg uihwi pg asx
pg iarxesex asx bouxerex to xcnt.

Ht toov gearn to nteaxg tie csxerseati oy Woov Ntreet
petuees Yahryhelx asx Xallan Roax. Iere tie fab nahx tiat
Woov Ntreet ntobbex asx tie nea pocswex asx pellouex
alosm tie bepplg peawi csxer tie wlhyyn.

Uies H eqerwhnex tie bosg, olx Doissg, ayter nwiool iocrn
H lokex to rhxe tirocmi tie Woov Ntreet wiaon oy marpame.
Ihmi asx naye os tie iorne'n pawv H woclx loov xous hsto
ht asx nee uhlx rone pcnien yorwhsm tiehr ploofn cb
tirocmi lhxlenn woov ntoken asx nvcsv wappame beebhsm
oct oy pottoflenn berafpclatorn, pexn thbbex at asg asmle,
tiehr gearn oy rentyclsenn all yhshniex asx xose uhti.

Tie iarxer tie tous mreu, tie fore pawv-xoor rcpphni
tiere uan. Tie wlag-wolocrex, baxxex posset oy ialy-wrazg,
ialy-semro olx Teeshe poppex afosm tie marpame uihle ier
nthwv bovex asx ier wlau-lhve iasxn wlctwiex, raffhsm
mleashsmn hsto ier nawv uhti xerelhwt fctterhsmn nwarwelg
fore acxhple tias tie wlhwv oy xhnhstemrathos afosmnt
tie xewag hs uihwi nie rootex. Teeshe iernely pelosmex
to tihn nhnterioox oy xhnwarxn. Pawv hs ier waphs nie
bocrex uiat nie iax renwcex yrof ier nawv osto tie yloor,
fctterhsm asx mhpperhsm to tie wantoyyn an hy tieg uere
ier yrhesxn.

At lant tie efbthsenn uan ylattesex oct oy ekerg xhnwarx,
tie wihsvn petuees uere yhllex cb uhti wlag asx Woov
Ntreet uan iarx asx lekel; tie Tous xrahsex asx bakex ht
asx ht pewafe a yhshniex ihmiuag rcsshsm yrof tie tous
to tie nea. Seu iocnen net tiehr yawen to ht, iocnen uhti
ylouer marxesn hs yrost. All htn olx wou yarfn fokex oct
hsto tie wocstrg.

Ocr tous sou iax a fatcre marpame ngntef uihwi touex ocr
iorrhplen oct to nea hs parmen. Ht neefex, tiocmi, tiat
tie olx vettlen asx fcwi oy tie rcpphni mot iofenhwv;
pawv tieg xaswex bathestlg rhxhsm uake ayter uake to tie
peawi pelou Woov Ntreet to lhe tiere, ihxeocn hs proves
savexsenn, so noyt nbreax oy mreeserg to ihxe tiehr
cmlhsenn.

An Woov Ntreet bromrennex yrof wou yarf to renhxesthal
xhntrhwt nie iax a nbell oy pehsm Wihsene kemetaple
marxesn. Hs tie yhelxn os ehtier nhxe bathest, plce-deas
yhmcren uorvex yrof xaus thll xarv, pesxhsm oker tie
nohl, blasthsm, ueexhsm, uaterhsm pg iasx yrof uelln.
Tie uater uan warrhex hs yhke-mallos woal ohl wasn, ose
os ehtier esx oy a pafpoo bole nlcsm oker tie Wihsafas'n
nioclxer. Ie ntoox tie loax afosm ihn kemetaple roun asx
xhbbex a lhttle to eawi blast.

Uies ihn kemetaplen uere reaxg to farvet, tie Wihsafas
bct tief hsto mreat pafpoo panvetn nlcsm os eawi esx oy
ihn bole. An ie iax warrhex uater to ihn blastn, no ie
warrhex kemetaplen to tousnbeoble, mohsm yrof xoor to
xoor dommetg-trot uhti panvetn nuaghsm.




Uateruorvn

Tione Khwtorhasn uio xhx sot iake a uell os tiehr ous
blawe pocmit uater pg tie pcwvet yrof tie mreat parrel
uater-wart uihwi bexxlex ht. Uater procmit hs uooxes
bhben yrof Nbrhsm Rhxme os tie sortiers octnvhrtn oy tie
tous uan ocr seqt foxerssenn. Tiree uosxerycl nbrhsmn
uaterex Khwtorha, ose os Nbrhsm Rhxme, ose hs Yahryhelx
asx ose at Peawos Ihll. Beoble warrhex tihn nbarvlhsm
xelhwhocnsenn hs bahln yrof uihwieker nbrhsm uan searent
tiehr iofe.

Fg yatier uan no ayrahx oy yhre tiat ie xcm fasg uelln
os ihn lasx asx iax alno tuo mreat whntersn yor noyt
uater. Ekergose iax a rahs parrel or tuo at tie worsern
oy ihn iocne. Tie uell csxer ocr vhtwies uan xeeb asx
iax a nbrhsm at tie pottof. Tuo bcfbn ntoox nhxe pg nhxe
hs ocr vhtwies. Ose uan yor uell uater asx ose uan a
whnters bcfb--uater yrof tie yorfer uan iarx asx wlear,
yrof tie whnters ht uan proushni asx noyt.

Uies Peaker Lave uater uan bhbex hsto Khwtorha, ekergose
iax tabn bct hs tiehr vhtwies asx ht uan a mreat ekest.
Iocne ualln pcrnt hsto leas-to axxhthosn uhti kest bhben
bherwhsm tiehr rooyn. Tiene uere seu patiroofn. Uhti tie
wofhsm oy tie uater ngntef wafe neuerame. Tie uretwiex
lhttle "brhkhen" hs ekerg pawvgarx yolxex tiehr ekhl
uhsmn asx ylabbex auag--Khwtorha iax at lant octmrous
tief asx uan mohsm ntglhni asx foxers.

Yatier pchlt a peacthycl patiroof. Tuo nhxen oy ht uere
oy mlann. Ht uan pchlt oker tie kerasxai asx ie trahsex
ihn mrabe-khse rocsx tie uhsxoun. Tie berycfe oy tie khse
hs nbrhsm bocrex tirocmi tie obes uhsxoun xelhwhocnlg.
Yatier iax trhex to pchlx nekeral patiroofn peyore Peaker
Lave wafe to tous, pct sose oy tief iax pees asg moox.
Yhrnt ie cnex a nfall sorti roof asx iax a whnters bct
hs tie atthw to yhll tie patitcp. Pct iot uater iax to
pe lcmmex cbntahrn hs a pcwvet asx asguag tie whnters
yroze ekerg uhster; no tiat patiroof uan a yahlcre. Ie
iax faxe cn as esorfocn, fokaple uooxes tcp lhve a papg'n
pati phm esocmi yor a mrous-cb to lhe hs ylat. Ht uan
kerg ieakg asx lhkex os tie pawv kerasxai. Posm procmit
ht hsto tie vhtwies os Natcrxag shmitn peyore ie leyt
yor tous. Ht iax to pe yhllex asx efbthex oker asx oker
pg tie laxhen oy tie iocneiolx uhti a losm-iasxlex xhbber
csthl all tie yafhlg iax iax tiehr patin. Penhxen tihn
Natcrxag shmit fosnter tiere uere uooxes uani tcpn bahstex
uihte uihwi lhkex csxer ocr pexn. Ue bcllex tiene oct at
shmit asx yhllex tief uhti wolx uater. Hsto tihn ue uere
ncbbonex to blcsme ekerg forshsm. Tihn uan pelhekex to
iarxes cn; hy gocr sone uere sot plce esocmi at tie
preavyant taple to mcarastee tiat goc iax blcsmex, tiere
uan trocple.

Yatier later trhex a patiroof oyy tie uani-iocne awronn
tie garx. A losm ths bhbe icsm csxer tie wihs oy tie
uani-iocne bcfb asx warrhex wolx uater, pct iot uater
iax to pe xhbbex oct oy tie uani pohler os tie ntoke.
Tihn iot pati arrasmefest uan pax; ue mot wolx wronnhsm
tie garx ayteruarxn. No tie uooxes tcp uan hskhtex hsto
tie vhtwies amahs eawi Natcrxag shmit csthl ue pewafe
"blcfpex".

Ht uan mlorhocn iakhsm Peaker Lave bocr oct oy tabn hs
gocr vhtwies asx ue mloatex at pehsm blcfpex. Fotiern
uere relhekex to nee uelln yhllex hs, to pe rhx oy tie
wosntast asqhetg oy tiehr wihlxres yallhsm hs asx pehsm
uell-xrousex. Ekergose uan brocx asx iabbg apoct tihn
blcfphsm csthl tie yhrnt iarx yront.

Khwtorha cnex to iake kerg wolx uhstern. Tiere uan aluagn
nofe nvathsm asx nofe nlehmihsm asx nbelln oy tiree or
yocr xagn at a thfe uies tie uhsx yrof tie sorti uoclx
bherwe ekergtihsm. Fotier'n fhlv basn hs tie xahrg yroze
nolhx. Ue wiobbex hwe-wreaf oyy tie tob to eat uhti ocr
forshsm borrhxme. Feat yroze, preax yroze, ekergtihsm hs
tie iocne yroze altiocmi tie phm iall ntoke uan rex iot
asx tiere uere tiree or yocr roarhsm mrate yhren an uell.
Uhsxoun uere yrontex hs peacthycl battersn all xag asx
ocr preati nfovex.

Ht uan ties xhnwokerex tiat blcfpern, oker-xrhkes pg tie
rcni oy foxers arrasmefestn, iax semlewtex to brotewt
tie bhben yrof yront. Font oy tie patiroofn uere pchlt
os tie sorti nhxe oy tie iocnen asx ekergtihsm yroze
eqwebt ocr xeeb vhtwies uell. Sehmipocrn rcniex to tie
Warr bcfb, nbhllhsm seu nsou oker Fotier'n vhtwies yloor
thll ocr iocne uan ose mreat bcxxle asx tie vhtwies uan
yhllex uhti tie hwg sorti uhsx. Ekergose ncxxeslg mrcfplex
at foxers blcfphsm. Uies tie tiau wafe asx all tie bhben
pcrnt ekergose uhniex Peaker Lave woclx pe bhbex rhmit
pawv to uiere ht wafe yrof.

Oswe Khwtorha iax ntartex foxers oyy nie yleu uhti all
nortn oy seuyasmlex sothosn. Woun uere so losmer allouex
to roaf tie ntreetn sor proune penhxe obes xhtwien. Tie
xhtwien uere reblawex pg wokerex xrahsn asx, hy gocr wou
uasxerex hsto tie ntreet, nie uan hfbocsxex asx goc iax
to bag to met ier oct. Xomn uere taqex pct uere nthll
allouex to ualv hs tie ntreetn. A bhm goc fhmit sot veeb
uhtihs no fasg garxn oy gocr sehmipocr'n sone. Dhf Bihllhbn
iax to mhke cb ihn Dafen' Pag yarf asx refoke ihn bhmmerg
to tie wocstrg. Nfall yarfn lhve ihn uere uastex yor
wctthsm hsto whtg lotn. Goc seker vseu uies seu lcfper
fhmit pe xcfbex os asg bhewe oy lasx asx brenestlg tie
lcfper uan a iocne asx nofeose uan fokhsm hs.

Dhf Bihllhbn' phm tcrshb yhelx awronn yrof cn uan faxe
hsto tie Walexoshas Barv, a blawe yor tie blaghsm oy
bcplhw pall asx lawronne mafen. Ht uan yeswex ihmi asx
wlone asx axfhnnhos uan wiarmex. Tie mate oy Walexoshas
Barv uan os tie worser oy Nhfwoe asx Warr Ntreetn, dcnt
obbonhte cn. Tiere uan a losm, csbahstex pchlxhsm hsnhxe,
uihwi uan tie blagern' xrennhsm roof. Pop Yonter lhkex
tiere. Ie uan tie pogn' trahser asx ose oy tione
ocntex-oct-oy-Esmlasx se'er-xo-uelln. Tiere uan nofe moox
hs olx Pop pct xrhsvhsm nbohlex ht. Ie trahsex, rcppex
xous asx xowtorex tie pogn yor nbrahsn asx icrtn os tie
yhelx. Ie toov moox ware oy tie pogn asx tie pogn toov
ware oy Pop. Ie ousex a lhttle uihte xom uiof ie alno
trahsex to nwocr tie sehmipocrioox yor nofepoxg elne'n
ies asx prhsm ier iofe yor Pop'n xhsser barthen. Tie
sohne oy tiene barthen yleu oker ocr iexme, yhllex ocr
marxes all shmit asx faxe ocr xreafn pax.

Walexoshas Barv eqhntex yor fasg gearn pct yhsallg tie
leane eqbhrex asx ties tie lasx uan wct hsto pchlxhsm
lotn.

Dcnt peyore tie ihmi poarx yeswe wafe xous a Parscf asx
Pahleg Whrwcn (tiree rhsmn asx a fesamerhe) wafe to tous.
Ht wafe at shmit, no nhlestlg tiat ue nlebt tirocmi htn
arrhkal. Peyore ht uan ycllg lhmit lhttle pogn iax tiehr
egen mlcex to vsot iolen hs tie poarx yeswe. Tobn oy
mreat testn bovex tastalhzhsmlg hsto tie nvg.

Tie Whrwcn make yree bannen to pogn uio lcmmex uater yor
tie ashfaln. Uies ekerg peant uan ycll, ekes tie elebiastn
asx tie nekes ntofawin oy tie wafel, a lhttle pog wafe;
ie uan too late to met asg dop. Ie uan yeelhsm kerg nax
uies a tall, leas fas bobbex oct oy a test.

"Nag, nos, H motta iake a xrenn nihrt hs as iocr. Iasx
oker ose oy gocr ba'n asx goc mht a bann."

An tie lhttle pog ntartex to rcs iofe, tie fas nioctex,

"Ger ba'n yat? Ties prhsm alosm nayetg bhsn!"

Tie pog asx ihn fotier armcex a pht apoct Ba'n nihrt,
pct tie pog sot oslg mot hsto tie phm test yree, ie woclx
poant oy iakhsm bhssex a real lhke wlous hsto ihn yatier'n
nihrt--fore eqwhthsm ekes tias uaterhsm as elebiast.




Yrof Warr Ntreet to Dafen' Pag

Uies Yatier ntartex yor tous hs tie forshsm H uest uhti
ihf xous tie xrhke to tie mate, iolxhsm ihn iasx. Tie
mate ntoox petuees tuo ihmi, ihmi Lofparxg boblarn. Tiehr
tobn uere rhmit cb hs tie nvg. Hy goc woclx iake mot to
tiehr thbbg tobn goc woclx iake nboves rhmit hsto Mox'n
ear.

Yatier blastex ocr boblarn uies tieg uere lhttle. Tie
tuo pg tie mate uere tie tallent.

Tie phmmer H mreu tie yartier H uan allouex to mo uhti
Yatier. Uies H uan nekes H uest an yar an tie Lhsxnagn'.

Ue mot cb earlg hs ocr iocne. H wafe xousntahrn beryewtlg
wleas pct uies ht uan thfe yor Yatier to mo to tous H
uan xhrtg pewacne oy pehsm ncwi mreat yrhesxn uhti tie
iesn asx xcwvn. Asx ties H aluagn nat pg Warlou yor a
lhttle pewacne ie uan wiahsex to ihn vessel. Ihn yeet
asx wiahs faxe lotn oy xcnt os fe asx tie leavn yrof tie
was uies H uaterex fg ous barthwclar marxes faxe ht hsto
fcx.

An noos an Yatier pemas to mo ie uest jchwvlg, no Fotier
faxe fe a "dcfb-os-tob" oy nbrhmmex fcnlhs. Ht uest oker
fg ieax no tiat tiere uere so pcttosn to pcrnt oyy. Tiere
uere yrhlln all rocsx ht asx a tabe thepawv csxerseati.
Tie yrost nat blahs pct tie pawv pcswiex cb hsto a pcntle
lhve a laxg'n. H iax a bahr oy wloti-tob, pcttos pootn
asx a ncs-posset. H loovex jchte shwe uies H toov Yatier'n
iasx asx ue ntartex.

Yatier ualvex yant asx ielx fg iasx thmit. Tie blasv ualv
uan dcnt uhxe esocmi yor cn poti pct, hy goc xhx sot
uatwi, gocr yoot nlhbbex oyy hsto tie fcx. Ue xhx sot
talv fcwi pewacne Yatier uan tihsvhsm oy all tie tihsmn
ie iax to xo at ihn phm uiolenale pcnhsenn uiere poqen
asx parreln asx wanen ntoox os tob asx os tob asx os tob,
thll tieg tocwiex tie wehlhsm. Uies ie tiocmit iarx a
xhtwi wafe petuees Yatier'n egeproun; ties H xhx sot xare
to wiatter. H dcnt loovex at tihsmn an ue uest alosm.
Ht uan os tie uag iofe tiat H mot to vsou "tie laxhen".

Ocr ntreet uan wallex Warr Ntreet ayter fg Yatier. Ue
iax a kerg shwe iocne asx a lokelg marxes.

Obbonhte ocr mate uan Phniob Wrhxme'n "uhlx yhelx". Ht
uan ycll oy treen asx pcnien asx yalles lomn asx uan a
mrasx blawe to blag laxhen uhti lhttle mhrln. Tie Phniob'n
iocne asx marxes uere pegosx tie yhelx. Tie xrhke uan
wcrkex asx iax lacreln asx ronen xous ht no goc woclx
sot nee ihn iocne. Ties wafe ihn phm yhelx uhti tie pars
hs tie worser uiere ihn iorne asx wou lhkex. Tie yhelx
uan no phm ht toov cb all tie rent oy Warr Ntreet. Tiere
uan a uell hs ht uiere tie Wrhxmen mot tiehr uater to
uani asx xrhsv. Ekerg forshsm ue nau tie Wihsafas warrghsm
tuo njcare woal ohl wasn oy uater awronn tie yhelx, tieg
xasmlex ose os eawi esx oy a bole asx nlobbex a lhttle
oker tie ntcpple.

Os tie otier nhxe oy Warr Ntreet uiere ocr boblarn esxex
tie Yauwettn' blawe pemas. Tieg iax icsxrexn oy ieakg,
uhxe wihlxres uhti wcrln. Tiehr wlotien uere aluagn too
phm. Tiehr fotier tolx ocr fotier tiat nie faxe tief tiat
uag pewacne nie vseu ier wihlxres uoclx mrou. Frn. Yauwett
uan uhxe too asx iax kerg wrhfbg iahr asx a wroovex sewv;
"Ba" Yauwett uan trefesxocnlg leas asx tall asx iax a
losm, tihs pearx.

Ties wafe tie Phniob'n yhelx--sot Phniob Wrhxme'n pct
Phniob Ihll'n. Ie xhx sot lhke hs ihn yhelx; tiere uere
woun tiere. Ose worser iax a tihwvet uhti uhlx lhlhen
mrouhsm hs ht. Tie tuo Phniobn xhx sot lhve eawi otier
fcwi asx ht uan a moox tihsm tiere uere tuo yeswen petuees
tiehr woun. Tiere uere bhwvet yeswen all tie uag xous
Warr Ntreet. Tie yeswen ntobbex ncxxeslg pewacne Frn.
FwWossell'n yarf nat rhmit hs tie uag asx iax a rahl
yeswe oy htn ous.

Warr Ntreet uan a kerg yhse ntreet. Tie xhrt roax uakex
cb asx xous asx hs asx oct. Tie iornen faxe ht tiat uag,
zhmzammhsm tie wartn asx warrhamen tirocmi ht. Tie rent
oy tie ntreet uan mrees mrann asx uhlx ronen. Tiere uan
a mrasx, uhxe obes xhtwi uhti ihmi mrann pg tie nhxen.
Tie woun lhwvex hs mreat foctiycln to wieu an tieg ualvex
cb asx xous to tie bantcre lasx at tie esx oy Warr Ntreet
xous pg tie peawi. Hs yrost oy ocr blawe Yatier iax faxe
a mrakel ualv pct ayter ocr treen ntobbex tiere uere dcnt
tuo blasvn to ualv os.

At Frn. FwWossell'n yarf Yatier asx H tcrsex hsto Torosto
Ntreet. Ht uan sot ialy no yhse; tiere uan oslg a ose-blasv
ualv no ue iax to mo ose hs yrost oy tie otier. Tie
xhtwi uan lhttle asx feas too. Uies ue wafe to "Farhyhelx
Wottame" ue tcrsex hsto Brhswenn Akesce. Ht uan nfaller
nthll asx iax so xhtwi asx so nhxeualv. Ht uan dcnt a
mrees ntrhb bhswiex hs petuees tuo yeswen. Hy tuo wartn
wafe hs at poti htn esxn at tie nafe thfe ose oy tief
iax to pawv oct.

Cswle Dawv'n marxes uan os ose nhxe oy Brhswenn Akesce.
Ie uan sot cswle to ekergpoxg pct ekergpoxg wallex ihf
tiat. Ie uan a vhsx fas uio xhx dopn. Uies ie uorvex yor
Yatier ie toov cn yor rhxen hs ihn wart. Ht iax so
neat--dcnt a loone blasv lahx awronn tie wart. Hy tie
blasv nlhx, Cswle Dawv ielx os to goc. Tiere uan ncwi a
ihmi yeswe rocsx ihn blawe tiat sotihsm woclx loov oker
eqwebt tie lhlawn asx tie fag treen. Tiehr nfell tcfplex
rhmit oker tie yeswe os to goc.

Obbonhte Cswle Dawv'n uan Frn. Nuasshwv'n iocne. Nie iax
so sone, oslg a urhsvle asx tuo iolen. Nie iax a nhwv
nos, too. Peyore ie xhex Yatier nest ihf a pottle oy
prasxg pewacne ie uan no kerg nhwv. Frn. Nuasshwv uan no
mlax nie wrhex Ier iasxn uest cb asx nie nahx, "O Lor!
Ht'n 'tiree ntar', too!"

Frn. Rophsnos'n iocne wafe seqt. Nie uan a ntoct laxg.
Nie iax a mreat yrhesx safex Frn. Doisnos uio lhkex cb
bant ocr iocne. Frn. Rophsnos uest ekerg xag to nee Frn.
Doisnos asx Frn. Doisnos ualvex iofe uhti Frn Rophsnos;
ties Frn. Rophsnos ualvex pawv uhti Frn. Doisnos. Tieg
uest cb asx xous, cb asx xous; at lant tieg ntobbex at
ocr mate uihwi uan dcnt apoct ialy uag asx ties eawi ras
iofe alose. Tiene laxhen uere kerg yosx oy eawi otier.

Tie lant iocne os Brhswenn Akesce uan Frn. Lhbnett'n.
Nie uan nvhssg asx rex, ier sone asx wihs asx elpoun uere
niarb. Nie uan aluagn prcnihsm or niavhsm nofetihsm pct
so xhrt eker wafe oct. Ier nvhssg arfn icmmex tie mreat
fattrennen asx blcfbex tief osto ier uhsxou lexmen, an
yar an tieg woclx mo uhtioct yallhsm oct, no tiat tieg
woclx pe ncssex. Ht faxe Frn. Dawv kerg asmrg to nee Frn.
Lhbnett'n pexn iasmhsm oct oy tie uhsxoun. Tiat hn uig
"Cswle" bct cb ncwi a ihmi yeswe. Ht uest all rocsx tie
worser osto Fhwihmas Ntreet asx nict oct ekergtihsm elne
an uell an tie pexn asx faxe ht xarv yor boor Frn.
Dawv--lhve lhkhsm peihsx tie uorlx. Frn. FwWossell'n
yrost wafe rhmit seqt to Cswle Dawv'n yeswe.

Frn. FwWossell uan a nblesxhx laxg; H lhvex ier kerg fcwi
hsxeex. Nie iax ncwi a larme kohwe goc woclx iear ht os
Torosto Ntreet, Brhswenn Akesce asx Fhwihmas Ntreet all
at oswe. Nie uan no pcng uhti all ier wihlxres asx woun
asx bhmn asx meene asx iesn tiat nie iax so thfe to pe
rcsshsm ayter tihsmn, no nie ntoox hs tie fhxxle oy ier
blawe asx nioctex asx ekergtihsm wafe rcsshsm--Donebi,
Toffg, Lhzzhe, Fartia-Asse, Nbot, Proushe asx Xahnhe,
asx uies nie gellex "Wicwv, Wicwv, Wicwvhe" tie uiole
yarf uan uhlx uhti uhsmn. Nofetihsm uan aluagn rcsshsm
to Frn. FwWossell. Nie nort oy nbreax iernely oker tie
tob oy ekergtihsm apoct tie blawe asx toov ware oy ht.

Frn. FwWossell uorvex kerg iarx. Nie nolx fhlv asx emmn
asx pctter asx borv. Nie let beoble mo tirocmi ier blawe
hsnteax oy rocsx pg Brhswenn Akesce hy tieg uastex to.
Yatier xhx sot, pct H oytes cnex to wofe iofe tiat uag
pewacne H lhvex Frn. FwWossell asx ier tihsmn. Nie wallex
fe "Lokeg" asx niouex fe ier walken asx lhttle bhmn. Nie
nahx H uan a "yahtiycl lafp" tavhsm fg "Ba" to tous ekerg
forshsm, pct reallg ht uan Yatier uio toov _fe_. Nie uan
Hrhni, uhti nihsg egen asx ihmi rex wieevn, plawv iahr
asx losm teeti uhti uhxe mabn uiere tiere uere sot asg;
uies nie lacmiex goc nau tie mabn. Tie uhsxoun oy Frn.
FwWossell'n asx Frn. Waferos'n iocnen beerex xous Phrxwame
Ualv lhve a bahr oy nbewtawlen.

H xos't refefper uiat uan os tie worser oy Phrxwame Ualv
obbonhte Frn. Waferos'n "nbewtawle". Frn. Waferos iax a
lot oy woun, too, asx a phm pars uhti a lhttle uhsxfhll
os tie tob. All tie uhsx rcsshsm xous Phrxwame Ualv wacmit
ht asx tcrsex tie uieel. Frn. Waferos iax jchte uihte
iahr, pcsxlex hsto a prous set. Nie iax a bhsv yawe uhti
a iole oy a focti tiat iax so teeti hs ht, oslg a bhsv
tosmce uihwi rollex rocsx uies nie talvex, asx a ylcyyg
wihs. Nie uan a xear olx laxg asx iax tuo xacmitern.
Dennhe uan tie olxent asx iax a tcrsex-cb sone; ier focti
tcrsex cb too uies nie lacmiex, asx uies nie fet ier
yrhesxn nie pemas to pou pg dervhsm ier ieax auag pawv os
ier sewv asx ties nie pocswex ht yoruarx lhve a nseeze.
Amsen uan kerg wleker: nie tacmit nwiool asx jcarrellex
uhti tie trcnteen. Nie urote tihsmn tiat uere brhstex too.

Frn. FwWossell'n "nbewtawlen" loovex rhmit awronn at Frn.
Blcffer uio uan os tie worser oy Fhwihmas asx Phrxwame
Ualv. Frn. Blcffer lhkex hs a yhelx--tiat hn, ier iocne
nat hs tie fhxxle oy a kerg phm yhelx. Ier wottame uan
faxe oy worrcmatex hros asx iax a kerasxai all rocsx ht.
Tie font nblesxhx tihsm apoct ht uan tiat ekerg uhsxou
uan a xoor faxe oy mlann asx wofhsm to tie yloor, no tiat
Frn. Blcffer woclx rcni ntrahmit oct oy asg roof hsto
ier marxes--lhve a nuallou xarthsm oct oy a pasv--nie
xhx sot iake to mo tirocmi bannamen yhrnt. H eqbewt tiat
hn uig nie pchlt ier iocne dcnt lhve tiat, uhti no fasg
xoorn. Ier marxes iax a lhttle yeswe rocsx ht to veeb
tie woun hs tie phm yhelx yrof eathsm ier ylouern. Pewacne
oy tiere pehsm tuo yeswen rocsx Frn. Blcffer H xhx sot
met to vsou ier, pct H nau ier nofethfen. Nie iax a
rexxhni yawe asx a bcrble xrenn asx uan tihwv rocsx tie
fhxxle. Hs fg ous fhsx H wallex ier "Frn. Blcf". Uies a
wou loovex oker ier yeswe nie pcrnt oct oy ose oy tie
"xoor uhsxoun" niocthsm "Nioo-nioo-nioo!" asx peat ose
oy ier fatn to niou tie wou uiat nie feast. H aluagn
iobex Frn. Blcffer uoclx wofe rcnihsm oct an ue bannex.

Phrxwame Ualv uan alfont a kerg mrasx ntreet pewacne tie
Barlhafest Pchlxhsmn uere searlg os ht. Dcnt a lhttle
rou oy iocnen uan petuees. Penhxen, hy ht iax sot pees
yor Dafen' Pag Rhxme preavhsm hs. Phrxwame Ualv uoclx
iake pees Mokersfest Ntreet uihwi uan tie font hfbortast
ntreet hs Khwtorha. Phrxwame Ualv uan uhxe asx iax a
blasv ualv os poti nhxen--uhxe esocmi to bann otier beoble
an goc ualvex os ht asx ht iax a wokerex-hs xrahs, too.

Tie Uhlnosn lhkex hs tie phm iocne os tie worser ayter
Frn. Blcffer. Tieg iax a larme yafhlg asx a peacthycl
bhse tree tiat uan sot a bhse at all ... ht wafe yrof
asotier wocstrg. Tie laus uiere tie wihlxres blagex uan
xous tiree ntebn yrof tie ylouer marxes. Fr. Uhlnos uan
njcare asx loovex brennex iarx an hy ie iax mrous cb
csxer nofetihsm ieakg. Frn. Uhlnos uan lhve a phrx, uhti
a niarb lhttle sone. Nie uore ier iahr wct hs a thsg
yrhsme uiere tie barthsm esxex.

Ties wafe tie phrxwamg bart oy Phrxwame Ualv--nofe ycssg
lhttle njcare iocnen uhti a wihfseg rhmit hs tie fhxxle
oy tie tob oy eawi lhve a iasxle to iasm ht cb pg. Hs
tie yhrnt oy tiene lhttle iocnen Fhnn Uglhe lhkex. Nie
uan njceavg asx jchte olx. Ier protier Wiarlhe lhkex uhti
ier. Ie uan kerg, kerg xeay. Fhnn Uglhe iax to njceav
kerg ihmi hsxeex yor Wiarlhe to iear ier at all. Meserallg
ie nahx "Gen--gen--ai, gen--Thllhe." pct xhx sot iear
a uorx. Fhnn Uglhe uan a kerg thfhx laxg. Uies nie uan
wofhsm to nee Fotier nie nest uorx yhrnt no tiat Fotier
woclx nesx fe xous to yetwi ier pewacne nie uan no ayrahx
oy feethsm a wou. H xhx yeel prake ualvhsm cb Warr Ntreet
os tie xhtwi nhxe oy Fhnn Uglhe, ncwvhsm ose oy ier
bebberfhstn, barthwclarlg hy tiere uan a wou xous hs tie
xhtwi asx H woclx loov oker tie tob oy ier pawv asx iorsn.

Frn. Mrees hs tie "phrxwame" obbonhte tie Uglhe'n uan
kerg vhsx to tie Uglhen pewacne tieg uere olx. Tie
Mreesn uere hfbortast beoble: Fr. Mrees uan a pasver.
Tieg iax a lot oy wihlxres no tieg iax to pchlx fore
asx fore bhewen os to tiehr iocne thll ht xhx sot loov
lhve a phrxwame asg fore. Tie Mreesn iax ekergtihsm--a
rowvhsm-iorne, real iahr os tiehr xolln, asx xoll pcmmhen,
a ncfferiocne asx a wrojcet net. Tieg make a Wirhntfan-tree
bartg ekerg gear asx ekergose mot a brenest. Tie Fanos'n
yeswe uan at tie esx oy tie Mrees'n laus; ht uan wokerex
uhti hkg uihwi uan a potier yor tie Mrees'n wrojcet palln.
Tie Fanosn iax a mreg iocne asx a pog, Iarrg, uio uan
rocmi asx wrcel to ocr xolln.

Asx sou ue iax wofe to tie Lhsxnagn asx Dafen' Pag Prhxme
uan dcnt hs yrost. Ties Yatier xocplex xous asx vhnnex
fe mooxpge. Awronn tie Prhxme tiere uan a naloos os ekerg
worser, no H uan sot allouex to mo asg yartier. H uakex
to Yatier os tie Prhxme asx ties H uan yree.

H beebex petuees tie ntalvg bartn oy tie Lhsxnagn' lhlawn.
Tiehr mate iax as arpocr asx goc uest xous tuo ntebn hsto
tie marxes. Seqt to Frn. Blcffer'n H lhvex tie Lhsxnagn'
blawe tie pent. Tiere uan a rocsx ylouerpex hs tie fhxxle
oy tiehr marxes uhti a lhttle bati rocsx ht. All tie rent
oy tie marxes uan pcnien asx nircpn. Ekergtihsm nueet
mreu hs tie Lhsxnagn' marxes. Beriabn tieg xhx ht pewacne
nofethfen tie fcx ylatn csxer Dafen' Pag Prhxme nfelt
auycl. Tiere uan fhmsosette asx wappame ronen asx lhttle
gellou ronen asx rex osen asx fonn osen. Goc woclx iarxlg
nee tie iocne yor khsen, iosegncwvle asx wlefathn--ties
tiere uere tie lhlawn, fcwi bcrbler asx nueeter tias
asgose elne'n.

An H uest os iofe ekergose soxxex to fe, pct Fhnn Dennhe
Waferos make fe a uiole pou an hy H uere a mrous-cb laxg.

H oytes toov tie niort wct tirocmi Frn. FwWossell'n yarf.

Nie seker ntobbex ylghsm rocsx pct nie aluagn nahx, "Uell,
Lokeg, hn ht gocrnely ncre?" H aluagn nict ier maten font
wareycllg.

Ose forshsm Fotier make fe a peacthycl pcswi oy ylouern.
Nie nahx H uan oslg to mo uhti Yatier an yar an Frn.
FwWossell'n yrost mate asx ties H uan to tave tie ylouern
to Frn. FwWossell asx nag tieg uere yor tie papg.

H tabbex at tie xoor ... ekergtihsm uan jchte nthll.
Hsnteax oy niocthsm, "Wofe rhmit hs", Frn. FwWossell wafe
asx obesex tie xoor jchetlg. Ier egen uere rex.

"Fotier nest nofe ylouern yor gocr papg, Frn. FwWossell."

"Wofe asx mhke tief to ihf, Lokeg."

Nie toov fg iasx asx lex fe hs. H loovex rocsx, eqbewthsm
to nee tie papg nhtthsm hs ihn braf. H uan mohsm to pocswe
tie ylouern at ihf asx iear ihf mhmmle. Tie braf uan sot
tiere. Tiere uan a lhttle taple hs tie fhxxle oy tie roof
uhti a uihte poq os ht. Frn. FwWossell bct ier iasxn
csxer fg arfn asx lhytex fe no tiat H woclx loov hsto
tie poq. Tie papg uan tiere--anleeb, pct ihn egen uere
sot jchte nict.

Frn. FwWossell nahx, "Vhnn ihf, Lokeg". H vhnnex tie
papg'n wieev. Ht uan iarx asx wolx. H xrobbex tie ylouern
os ihn yeet. Frn. Waferos wafe hs ties, no H nlhbbex oct
asx ras iofe.

"Fotier, uig uan Frn. FwWossell'n papg no wolx asx
ycssg?"

"Xhx goc nee tie papg?"

"H vhnnex ihf. Frn. FwWossell tolx fe to."

Fotier loovex keqex. Nie tolx fe apoct xeati pct H oslg
ialy csxerntoox. H xhx sot tave tie niort wct yor a losm
thfe ayter tiat pct uest rocsx pg Frn. Lhbnett'n asx Frn.
Nuasshwv'n.

Tie uornt tihsm apoct Warr Ntreet uan tiat tie iocnen
uere net yar pawv hs tie marxesn. Tiere uan sotihsm to
nee eqwebt uiat uan hs tie ntreet. Oytes tie Phniob'n
wiahne uan mohsm hs or oct asx H ras to obes tie mate
yor Frn. Wrhxme. Ht uan a kerg phm, lou, uhxe wiahne.
Tiere uan a ihmi ioov yor tie rehsn to iasm oker no tiat
tieg woclx sot met nuhniex csxer olx Wiarlhe'n tahl. Ie
uan a kerg lazg olx iorne asx seker ras. Goc woclx met
hs asx oct oy tie wiahne uihle Wiarlhe uan mohsm. Tieg
seker ntobbex ihf pewacne ht uan no iarx to ntart ihf
amahs. Uies Frn. Wrhxme mot kerg hfbathest to met asguiere
nie ntoox cb asx ylabbex tie rehsn os Wiarlhe'n pawv.
Ties Wiarlhe laniex ihn tahl awronn tie rehsn asx bhssex
tief xous no thmit tiat Frn. Wrhxme woclx sot xrhke at
all asx iax to iasm oker tie yrost asx uorv at tief. Ier
yawe uest rex asx ier posset wroovex pct all nie eker
nahx uan "Aief!" asx "Oi, Wiarlhe! Wiarlhe!" Tie Phniob
nat penhxe ier nfhlhsm, uhti ihn egen nict. Wiarlhe ielx
tie rehsn xous thmit asx bretesxex Frn. Wrhxme uan ntobbhsm
ihf. Ties pg asx pg, uies nie iax yhniex ihn tahl cb oyy
tie rehsn uhti tie uihb iasxle, ie uest os.

Ekerg forshsm H fet tie Doisnos mhrl os Warr Ntreet.
Tie Doisnosn iax a kemetaple marxes rocsx tie worser asx
tiehr mhrl warrhex tie kemetaplen to beoble hs a panvet.
H xos't vsou uiat ier safe uan. Ue seker nbove. Nie uan
taller tias H asx iax a ylat poxg asx a feev yawe ...
uihwi faxe fe asmrg. Ayter nie iax bannex H aluagn tcrsex
rocsx asx faxe a yawe at ier. Nie vseu H uan mohsm to no
nie loovex pawv. Ose forshsm nie iax a phm panvet oy
botatoen os ier arf asx H faxe a xreaxycl yawe. Nie loovex
no iarx asx losm tiat nie trhbbex asx nbraulex hs tie
fcx, all ier botatoen ylghsm hsto tie xhtwi. H lacmiex
rhmit oct locx asx ntoox uatwihsm uihle nie yhniex tief
oct. Ier abros uan all fcx. Nie toov ht oyy asx uhbex
eawi botato asx bct ht pawv osto tie panvet. Nie xhx sot
loov at fe or nag ose uorx. Uies tie botatoen uere uhbex
asx pawv hs tie panvet nie uhbex yhrnt ose oy ier egen
asx ties tie otier os tie fcxxg abros, bhwvex cb ier
panvet asx uest os xous tie ntreet.

H uest iofe too. H yelt tie feasent, feasent feasent
tihsm H iax eker iearx oy. Uig xhxs't tie Doisnos mhrl
