iht fe? Or tirou fcx, or nag nofetihsm? Uig xhxs't nie?

Yatier asx Fotier uere talvhsm apoct ht ... H uan olx
esocmi pct H wrhex ekerg thfe H tiocmit apoct mohsm to
nwiool. Fg nhntern trafbex tuo fhlen shmit asx forshsm.
Hy H uest uhti tief H uoclx sot pe aple to nee Frn.
Lhbnett'n pex or Frn. Nuasshwv'n sone or Frn. Blcffer
ylg oct or Fhnn Dennhe'n pou. Ue'x mo os a ntrahmit,
iorrhple roax tiat iax so yrhesxn os ht ... pct, H xhx
sot iake to.

Frn. Yraner, tie laxg uio iax wofe to lhke hs "Farhyhelx
Wottame" ntartex a lhttle nwiool, no H uest tiere. H
woclx nthll mo an yar an tie mate oy tie nwiool ekerg
forshsm uhti Yatier, asx os Natcrxagn H woclx mo rhmit
to tie Lhsxnagn asx nee ahl fg yrhesxn.

Uies Natcrxag wafe H uastex to tell Yatier nofetihsm,
oslg ht uoclxs't wofe oct. H loovex cb a lot oy thfen
pct tie xhtwi petuees ihn egen uan kerg xeeb--H uan ialy
ayrahx. Ue iax bannex tie Mreesn' ... ue uere at tie
Fanosn' ntebn ... tie Lhsxnagn' lhlawn uere dcnt wofhsm.

"Yatier--Yatier--xos't goc tihsv--sou tiat H mo to nwiool
H af too phm to pe vhnnex hs tie ntreet?"

"Uio nahx no?"

"Tie mhrln at nwiool."

"An losm an H iake to ntoob goc uos't pe too phm," Yatier
nahx, asx ie vhnnex fe tuhwe.




Mrous Cb

Khwtorha'n tob mrasxsenn uan tie Xrharx Iotel; all
hfbortast khnhtorn ntagex at tie Xrharx. To nht hs wrhfnos
blcni arfwiahrn hs esorfocn yrost uhsxoun asx maze rhmhx
asx plasv at tie xcll ualln oy tie obbonhte nhxe oy Kheu
Ntreet no wlone to tie Xrharx Iotel tiat tieg njchstex
tie mazer'n egen, to pe ntarex at pg Khwtorha'n hsiaphtastn
an tieg njceezex cb asx xous sarrou Kheu Ntreet uihwi
iax so kheu at all, uan ncrelg uorti a khnht to tie
wabhtal whtg.

Tie Xrharx uan a prhwv pchlxhsm uhti phm xoorn tiat nucsm
asx njceavex. Ht uan rex, hsnhxe asx oct. Ht iax noyt
rex warbetn, noyan asx wiahrn cbiolnterex hs rex blcni
asx reb wcrtahsn, rex alno. All htn rex noytsenn nobbex
cb asx icmmex sohnen asx nfelln. Htn uiole hsnhxe uan a
dcfple oy ntcyyhsenn uihwi bcniex htnely hsto gocr yawe
an goc obesex tie octer xoor, lhwvhsm tie octnhxe yrenisenn
oyy goc mreexhlg, favhsm a xani yor tie obes. Pct tie
Xrharx xoor njcauvex asx nlaffex to peyore tie ntcyyhsenn
woclx enwabe asx iht pawv nfotierhsmlg osto goc. Uies
goc wafe oct oy tie iotel goc uere no noavex uhti htn
ieakhsenn goc fhmit iake pees a Xrharx noya. Ekes tie
iotel pcn iax tie Xrharx oxocr, altiocmi ht xhx sot
awtcallg lhke hsnhxe tie iotel. Ht uan a losm, doltg
tuo-iorne pcn uhti "Xrharx" bahstex os poti htn nhxen
asx a fas niocthsm "Xrharx" yrof tie pawv nteb. Ntou-auag
Xrharx nfelln ihx hs tie wcnihosn oy tie pcn asx xroke
to tie uiary reaxg to bocswe os khnhtorn.

Tie Xrharx khnhtorn wafe fontlg yrof Nas Yraswhnwo;
Kaswocker asx Nocsx whthen uere too pcng mrouhsm to uante
thfe os khnhthsm.

Khwtorha asx Kaswocker uere aluagn rhkaln asx faxe dealocn
yawen at ose asotier. Kaswocker iax a yhser iarpocr asx
mreu yanter; nie uan tie eanher to reawi, pehsm tie esx
oy tie rahl. Khwtorha iax tie Jcees'n safe, uan tie
wabhtal oy Prhthni Wolcfpha asx iax tie Enjchfalt Sakal
Ntathos.

Uies tie Eant asx Uent uere lhsvex pg tie Wasaxhas Bawhyhw
Rahluag, Kaswocker nahx, "Ia! H af tie esx oy tie rahl;
sopoxg uhll sou potier apoct tiat lhttle Khwtorha tous
os ier hnlasx. Nettlern asx khnhtorn uhll met oyy tie
trahs asx ntag iere uhti fe."

No nie pchlt yawtorhen, lcfper fhlln, uiarken asx nuellex
iernely ycrhocnlg; pct so fatter iou nie nuellex nie
woclx sot ielb Khwtorha'n pehsm tie wabhtal oy Prhthni
Wolcfpha or iakhsm tie Sakal Ntathos. Tie sakg fes'n
uhken wafe yrof Esmlasx xhrewt to Khwtorha to lhke uihle
tiehr icnpasxn' nihbn uere ntathosex at Enjchfalt a fhle
or no oct oy tie whtg.

Khwtorha vebt hs wloner tocwi uhti Esmlasx. Nie mot fore
asx fore "Olx Wocstrg"; Kaswocker mot fore asx fore
seu-uorlx. Kaswocker woketex Khwtorha'n mesthlhtg; Khwtorha
woketex Kaswocker'n pcnhsenn.

Tiene tuo whthen faxe Wasaxa'n Uent, ier yar Bawhyhw exme
uihwi lcrex bhoseern os asx os thll tieg wafe to tie rhf
oy tie oweas, earti pest to tie uorlx'n rocsxsenn--lasx
asx uater whrwlhsm tie Uent pawv to tie Eant amahs.

Bhoseern nlhx awronn Wasaxa'n kantsenn os tie W.B.R.
trahsn asx uere no wofyortaple hs xohsm ht tiat tieg xhx
sot met oyy thll tieg iax to. Oytes tie yhrnt Wasaxhas
lasx tiehr yeet tocwiex uan Prhthni Wolcfpha. Tie ntarv
Uent nsarlex a lhttle uies tieg tocwiex ier yhrnt pct
nie uan reallg searer to Esmlasx hs ier uagn asx yeelhsmn
tias tie Eant uan, altiocmi tie Uent uan nofe yocr tiocnasx
fhlen yartier auag hs nbawe. Pg asx pg tie Esmlhni yormake
tie Uent ier cswocti kantsenn asx tie Uent yormake tief
tiehr sarrou lhttlesenn.

Tie W.B.R. uatwiex tie Uent mrou. Nie nau Khwtorha'n
njcattg lhttle olx rex prhwv Barlhafest Pchlxhsmn mhke
blawe to famshyhwest ntose ntrcwtcren--xofen, wobber
rooyn--ekergtihsm peyhtthsm a Wabhtal Whtg. Yawhsm tie
Barlhafest Pchlxhsmn awronn Dafen' Pag arone a nexate
ntose asx wefest Bont Oyyhwe. Lhttle olx vsowv-vseex
uooxes Dafen' Pag prhxme nthll ntraxxlex tie fcx ylatn
petuees tie tuo. Tie W.B.R. bhllouex tiehr ieaxn cbos
tie fcx ylatn asx xreafex a xreaf. Yhrnt tieg tore xous
tie olx uooxes prhxme asx pchlt hs htn blawe a uhxe
woswrete wacneuag, xaffhsm tie Pag uatern pawv yrof tie
ylatn. Tie nea uan ycrhocn asx xaniex, pct tie woswrete
uall icrlex ht pawv. Nfelln mot yrasthw asx ntasv to ihmi
Ieakes csthl esmhseern wafe asx xrahsex tie neebame
nlocmi.

Besxrag'n noab uorvn asx Vasava Rou woclx sot esxcre lhye
uhtioct nfelln,--no tieg dcnt yaxex oct oy eqhnteswe.
Tie noab-yat reycne yrof tie noab uorvn ntobbex blaghsm
mlorhocn hrhxenwest wolocrn awronn tie fcx uies tie ncs
niose. So thxe wafe hs to nueeb auag Vasava Rou'n reycne:
tiehr pawv xoorn uere ieabex rocsx uhti ht asx uere
xhnmcnthsm. Tie gellou wlag oy tie fcx ylatn barwiex asx
wrawvex. Tie fani mrann, tirocmi uihwi tie Hsxhas wasoen
iax nlhtierex no warennhsmlg, tcrsex iarni asx prhttle.

Tie Whtg parterex uhti tie Nosmieen Hsxhasn mhkhsm tief
foseg asx a seu renerke at Enjchfalt hs eqwiasme yor
tiehr yhse iarpocr broberthen, uihwi tie Whtg uastex yor
hsxcntrhal bcrbonen. All arocsx Khwtorha'n lhttle iarpocr
tiere uan wiasme. Ekes ocr xcfbg lhttle woswebt oy Jcees
Khwtorha, xraus yrof tie _Hllcntratex Losxos Seun_ wiasmex
uies a nuartig ntose afazos rone os a bexental hs yrost
oy tie Barlhafest Pchlxhsmn. Eqwebt yor tie wrous asx
nwebtre ue uoclx seker iake rewomshzex tihn an ocr whkhw
moxfotier.

Uihle tiene wiasmen uere urewvhsm Khwtorha'n walf, tie
W.B.R. uere nthll xreafhsm tiehr fcx-ylat xreaf asx
arwihtewtn uere favhsm plce brhstn oy ht. To pe brhkate
asx csxhntcrpex xcrhsm tiehr xreafhsm tieg pchlt a icme
ioarxhsm tie esthre lesmti oy tie wacneuag nictthsm tie
xreaf hsto tie fcx. A whthzes'n ege uan abblhex to ekerg
vsot-iole hs tie ioarxhsm pct tieg woclx fave sehtier
ieax sor tahl oy uiat uan mohsm os. Tie bhle-xrhker mauvex
oker tie tob oy tie ioarxhsm. Ticx, ticx, ticx! Ier
yearycl uehmit opegex tie njceavg lhttle uihntle oy ier
esmhse, xrhkhsm fhmitg lomn, eawi ose a wofblete tree-pole,
esx xous hsto tie fcx. Tiere tieg ntoox nioclxer to
nioclxer, a ieaxlenn uooxes arfg trafbhsm tie olx fcx-nfelln
wleas tirocmi to Wihsa. Uies tie ylatn uere a nolhx uooxes
bawv tie iarpocr pottof uan xrexmex asx tie lhjchx fcx
bcfbex hs petuees tie ntasxhsm lomn. Tiocnasxn oy fes
uieelex fhllhosn oy parrouloaxn oy earti asx rowvn yor
icsxrexn oy ueevn--xcfbhsm, loaxhsm thll nolhx mrocsx
uan faxe os uihwi tie W.B.R. woclx yocsx tiehr xreaf.

Tie xreaf toov niabe hs realhtg. Tie ioarxhsm wafe xous
at lant asx tiere ntoox tie peacthycl Efbrenn Iotel. Ht
seker loovex wrcxe asx seu pewacne, uihle tie pawv uan
pchlxhsm, tie yhshniex yrost uan alreaxg mhkes oker to
wreebern asx nircpn, asx marxesn uere net tie fofest
uorvfes'n yeet iax ntobbex trafblhsm. Peacthycl
wosnerkatorhen nat rhmit os tob oy uiere tie whtg marpame
xcfb iax oswe pees. Csxer tiehr mlann rooyn ploofex rare
ylouern yrof all bartn oy tie uorlx, pct sose uere fore
nueet, fore lokelg tias tie lhttle uhlx prhar ronen tiat
iax no mrawhocnlg nootiex ocr sonen oker tie olx fcx-ylat
nfelln.

Tie Xrharx Iotel woclx sot plcni iernely asg rexxer tias
nie alreaxg uan uies wosyrostex pg ier rhkal no nie
uhtierex esthrelg auag. So khnhtorn uastex to nht estirosex
os rex blcni, to ntare at prhwv tuo yeet yrof tiehr sonen
uies tieg woclx nht peihsx blate mlann asx loov oct oker
Khwtorha'n lokelg lhttle iarpocr. Peacthycl nteafern
nscmmlex cb to tie uiary, alfont to tie kerg xoor oy tie
Iotel. Yrof Losxos xowv to Efbrenn Iotel xoor uan ose
cshsterrcbtex nlhtier oy eang trakel.

Khwtorha weanex to pe as Esmlhni sakal ntathos: Wasaxa
sakhex iernely. Enjchfalt Iarpocr sou iax a icme xrg-xowv
asx a wasserg. A yeu Hsxhas xcm-oct wasoen ntole hs asx
oct to tie seu renerkathos pct font oy tie Hsxhasn sou
wafe asx uest hs tiehr seu man yhnihsm-poatn.

Khwtorha vseu a lhttle poof--a lhttle pcntle--pct ht uan
sot ier satcre to poof asx pcntle; nie nlcfbex, nettlhsm
to nlou eang xekelobfest--rethwest, walf, xelhperate.

Tiene esorfocn iabbeshsmn--tie pchlxhsm oy tie Barlhafest
Pchlxhsmn, Efbrenn Iotel asx Wacneuag, tie entaplhnihsm
oy a yhrnt wlann poat nerkhwe petuees tie Hnlasx asx tie
fahslasx nthrrex tie ieart oy Khwtorha asx nest lenner
iabbeshsmn jchkerhsm tirocmi ier octnvhrtn.

Tie sarrou, tiree-fhle ntrhb oy uarf, hslasx nea obeshsm
oct oy tie iarpocr asx wallex tie Morme pewacne oy a
sarrou bann ialy-uag cb htn wocrne, ose oy Khwtorha'n
peactg nbotn uiere ier beoble iax patiex, asx uiere
remattan iax pees ielx os tie Jcees'n phrtixag, pewafe
hsyentex uhti poofn oy lomn asx nau-fhlln. Patiern
brotentex. Tieg xhx sot lhve nauxcnt nvhsn ayter patihsm
hs tie Morme uatern no uest to tie nuhffhsm tasvn hs tie
G.F.W.A. asx hs tie Wrgntal Bool oy tie seu Efbrenn Iotel.
Tie Morme tiat iax oswe pees no yhse a renhxesthal xhntrhwt
uest csyanihosaple. Tie peacthycl iofen os htn pasvn
nolx yor a fere nosm. Wasoen asx rou-poatn weanex warrghsm
bleancre barthen cb htn brotewtex uatern to bhwshw. Tie
yleet oy nahlhsm nwioosern nthll ntcwv to tiehr uhster
jcartern dcnt pelou tie Bohst Ellhwe prhxme, uiere tie
iarpocr esxex asx tie Morme pemas, wofhsm pawv to htn
nayesenn ekerg uhster lhve iofhsm phrxn. A ihxeocn
rahluag prhxme sou nbassex tie Iarpocr asx warrhex trahsn
yrof "cb-hnlasx" hsto tie whtg. Nbasshsm tie cbber iarpocr
tihn prhxme iohntex a newthos oy htnely yor tie nealern
to bann csxer asx ties nict tief naye hs nielter.

Wexar Ihll lghsm to tie sorti oy tie tous uest "nsootg";
elekathsm ier safe to Focst Xocmlan, nie pewafe a Bcplhw
Barv, nfcm uhti tafesenn. Lhttle Naashwi Focstahs iattex
ier wrous uhti as opnerkatorg tie uihte xofe oy uihwi
loovex yor all tie uorlx lhve as hskertex uihte bcxxhsm
panhs.

Pewacne tiere uan so fore Esmlhni Sakg ntathosex at
Enjchfalt tiere uere so fore sakg palln asx so niaf
pattlen petuees tie nolxhern asx nahlorn os Peawos Ihll.
Tiere uere so fore roax-iocne naloosn uhti lokelg ylouer
poqen asx wamen oy uhlx ashfaln asx iornen' xrhsvhsm
trocmin--tiere uere so fore xrhkhsm iornen. Actofophlen
bcrrex oker ohlex asx bakex ihmiuagn asx tiere uan so
xcnt to fave beoble asx iornen tihrntg.

Yrof tie tob oy Wicrwi Ihll tie Watiexral ntebbex ose
plowv pawv. Hsnteax oy xofhsathsm tie whtg nie sou
xofhsatex tie olx Jcaxra Ntreet wefeterg losm nhswe
reblawex pg tie seu Ronn Pag pcrghsm mrocsx. Prafplen so
losmer okerras tie xeax Bhoseern. Khwtorha'n earlg nettlern
nlebt thxhlg csxer uell fous lausn. Tie olx ieax-ntosen
asx safe-poarxn iax pees icxxlex hsto a worser, mlouerhsm
foronelg yrof tiehr bale safen, renesthsm tie savexsenn
oy pehsm uhtioct tie wlhsmhsm khsen asx tie rhot oy
csxermrouti tiat iax brotewtex tiehr xeax asx tiefnelken.
Os peswien tie bcplhw nat os tob oy tie xeax. Wihlxres
nwafberex oker tief--dasmle oy tie seu watiexral pelln
jchkerex tie xeax'n nthllsenn.

Dafen' Pag hn Dafen' Pag nthll. Tie nfart yornoov ier
losm amo. Yhrnt tieg fokex to Cbber Yort Ntreet, ties to
Rowvlasx Akesce, ties os to Oav Pag, yhsallg to tie
Cblasxn uiere tieg woclx sot veeb a wou or iasm oct a
uani or iake too fasg wihlxres. Tie esthre niore lhse oy
mreater Khwtorha hn sou nbreax uhti peacthycl iofen.

Khwtorha'n hsser lasx pehsm ihmier tias ier niore, ekerg
anbewt hn lokelg, Sorti, Nocti, Eant asx Uent--plce nea,
bcrble ihlln, nsou-wabbex Olgfbhw focstahsn pocsxhsm ier
noctiers iorhzos, lhttle pagn asx peawien ieabex uhti
ntorf-tonnex xrhyt, bhse treen ekerguiere, oav asx fable
hs blestg.

No ntasxn trasjchl Khwtorha hs ier Hnlasx netthsm--Uenters
an Uent was pe peyore earti'n mestle rocsxhsm bclln Uent
eant amahs.
